
[p. 1]
[।। ṇamō aṇuōgadharāṇaṁ ।।]

[sirīvimalāyariyaviraïyaṁ
[p. ]
paümacariyaṁ]

[suttavihāṇaṁ]

[maṅgalam —]
siddha-sura-kinnarōraga-daṇuvaï-bhavaṇindavandaparimahiyaṁ
usahaṁ jiṇavaravasahaṁ, avasappiṇiāititthayaraṁ // PaumaCa.1

ajiyaṁ vijiyakasāyaṁ, apuṇabbhava saṁbhavaṁ bhavaviṇāsaṁ
abhinandaṇaṁ ca sumaī, paümābhaṁ paümasacchāyaṁ // PaumaCa.2

tijaguttamaṁ supāsaṁ, sasippabhaṁ jiṇavaraṁ kusumadantaṁ
aha sīyalaṁ muṇindaṁ, sēyaṁsaṁ cēva vasupujjaṁ // PaumaCa.3

vimalaṁ tahā aṇantaṁ, dhammaṁ dhammāsayaṁ jiṇaṁ santi
kunthu kasāyamahaṇaṁ, araṁ jiyāriṁ mahābhāgaṁ // PaumaCa.4

malliṁ maliyabhavōhaṁ, muṇisubaya suvayaṁ tiyasanāhaṁ
paümassa imaṁ cariyaṁ, jassa ya titthē samuppannaṁ // PaumaCa.5

nami nēmi taha ya pāsaṁ, uragamahāphaṇimaṇīsu pajjaliyaṁ
vīraṁ vilīṇarayamalaṁ, tihuyaṇaparivandiyaṁ bhayavaṁ // PaumaCa.6

annē vi jē mahārisi, gaṇahara aṇagāra laddhamāhappē
maṇa-vayaṇa-kāyaguttē, savvē sirasā namaṁsāmi // PaumaCa.7


[p. 2]
[abhidhēyam —]
nāmāvaliyanibaddhaṁ, āyariyaparaṁparāgayaṁ sabaṁ
vōcchāmi paümacariyaṁ, ahāṇupurvi samāsēṇa // PaumaCa.8

kō vaṇṇiūṇa tīraï, nīsēsaṁ ṣaümacariyasaṁbandhaṁ
mōttūṇa kēvalijiṇaṁ, tikālanāṇaṁ havaï jassa // PaumaCa.9

jiṇavaramuhāō atthō, jō puciṁ niggaō bahuviyapṣō
sō gaṇaharēhi dhariuṁ, saṁkhēvamiṇō ya uvaïṭṭhō // PaumaCa.10

ēvaṁ paraṁparāē, parihāṇī puvagantha-atthāṇaṁ
nāūṇa kālabhāvaṁ, na rūsiyavvaṁ buhajaṇēṇaṁ // PaumaCa.11

atthēttha visamasīlā, kēvi narā dōsagahaṇatallicchā
tuṭṭhā vi subhaṇiēhiṁ, ēvaṁ pi guṇaṁ na gēṇhanti // PaumaCa.12

sabannubhāsiyatthaṁ, bhaṇanti kaïṇō jahāgamaguṇēṇaṁ
kiṁ vajjasūibhinnē, na riyaï tantū mahārayaṇē // PaumaCa.13

ētthaṁ ciya parisāē, narāṇa cittāim̐ bahuviyappāiṁ
kō sakkō ghēttu jē pavaṇahayāī va pattāī? // PaumaCa.14

titthayarēhi vi na kayaṁ, ēkkamayaṁ tihuyaṇaṁ suyadharēhiṁ
amhārisēhi kiṁ puṇa, kīraï iha mandabuddhīhiṁ? // PaumaCa.15

jaï vi hu duggahahiyaō, lōgō bahukūḍa-kavaḍamēhāvī
taha vi ya bhaṇāmi saṁpaï, sabuddhivihavāṇusārēṇaṁ // PaumaCa.16

dēhaṁ rōgāiṇṇaṁ, jīyaṁ taḍivilasiyaṁ ṣiva aṇiccaṁ
navaraṁ kavaguṇarasō, jāva ya sasi-sūra-gahacakaṁ // PaumaCa.17

tamhā narēṇa niyayaṁ, mahaïmahāpurisakittaṇucchāhaṁ
hiyaē cciya kāyavvaṁ, attāṇaṁ cēyamāṇēṇaṁ // PaumaCa.18


[p. 3]
[dēhāvayavasāphalyam —]
tē nāma hōnti kaṇṇā, jē jiṇavarasāsaṇammi suipuṇṇā
annē vidūsagassa va, dārumayā cēva nimmaviyā // PaumaCa.19

taṁ cēva uttimaṅgaṁ, jaṁ ghummaï vaṇṇaṇāisāmannē
annaṁ puṇa guṇarahiyaṁ, nāliyarakaraṅkayaṁ cēva // PaumaCa.20

jiṇadarisaṇujjayā vi hu, jē nayaṇā tē havanti supasatthā
micchattamaïliyā puṇa, cittayarēṇaṁ va nimmaviyā // PaumaCa.21

jiṇavarakahāṇurattā, dantā tē hōnti kantisaṁjuttā
sēsā silēsakajjē, jāyā vi hu vayaṇabandhammi // PaumaCa.22

kiṁ nāsiyāe kīraï, bahuvihasasugandhagandhaluddhāē?
susuyatthagandhagandhaṁ, jā na vi jāṇēi lōgammi // PaumaCa.23

jē cciya saṁmaüllāvaṁ, bhaṇanti tē uttamā ihaṁ ōṭṭā
annē suttajalūgā-paṭṭīsaṁvukkasamasarisā // PaumaCa.24

jā jāṇaï samayarasaṁ, sā jīhā sundarā havaï lōē
duvayaṇatikkhadhārā, sēsā churiya va navaghaḍiyā // PaumaCa.25

taṁ pi ya havaï pahāṇaṁ, muhakamalaṁ jaṁ guṇēsu taïttillaṁ
annaṁ vilaṁ va bhaṇṇaï, bhariyaṁ ciya dantakīḍāṇaṁ // PaumaCa.26

jō paḍhaï suṇaï purisō, sāmaṇṇē ujjamēi sattīē
sō uttamō hu lōē, annō puṇa sippiyakaō ca // PaumaCa.27

sabāyarēṇa ēvaṁ, purisēṇaṁ ujjhiūṇa mūḍhattaṁ
hōyavvaṁ nayamaïṇā, jiṇasāsaṇabhattijuttēṇaṁ // PaumaCa.28

aha paümacariyatuṅgē, vīramahāgayavarēṇa nimmaviē
maggē paraṁparāē, ajjavi kaïkuñjarāṇa gamō // PaumaCa.29

taha kaïvaragayamayagandhalōluō mahuyarō va maggēṇaṁ
payadāṇabindudiṭṭhī, ahamavi tēṇaṁ ciya payaṭṭō // PaumaCa.30

suttāṇusārasarasaṁ, raïyaṁ gāhāhi pāyaḍaphuḍatthaṁ
vimalēṇa paümacariyaṁ, saṁkhēvēṇaṁ nisāmēha // PaumaCa.31


[p. 4]
[granthaviṣayānukramaṇikā —]
ṭhiīvaṁsasamuppattī, patthāṇaraṇaṁ lavaṁkusuppattī
nivāṇamaṇēyabhavā, satta purāṇēttha ahigārā // PaumaCa.32

paümassa cēṭṭhiyamiṇaṁ, kāraṇamiṇamō'higārasaṁjuttaṁ
tisalāsuēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ, suttaṁ saṁkhēvaō suṇaha // PaumaCa.33

vīrassa pavaraṭhāṇaṁ, viulagirīmatthaē maṇabhirāmē
taha indabhūikahiyaṁ, sēṇiyaraṇṇassa nīsēsaṁ // PaumaCa.34

kulagaravaṁsuppattī, nīīē lōgakāraṇaṁ cēva
usabhajiṇajammaṇubbhava, ahisēyaṁ mandaragirimmi // PaumaCa.35

uvaēsaṁ ciya vivihaṁ, lōgassa ya attināsaṇaṁ cēva
sāmaṇṇa kēvalubbhava, aïsaya kusumōhavuṭṭīō // PaumaCa.36

sabasurā-'suramahiyaṁ, nivāṇaṁ paramasōkkhamāhappaṁ
bharahassa bāhubaliṇō, taha saṁgāmaṁ jahāvattaṁ // PaumaCa.37

jāīṇa ya uppattī, kutitthagaṇa-vivihavēsadhārīṇaṁ
vijjāharavaṁsassa ya, uppattī vijjudantassa // PaumaCa.38

uvasaggaṁ pi ya ghōraṁ, muṇivaravasahassa saṁjayantassa
kēvalanāṇuppattī, vijāharaṇaṁ ca dharaṇēṇaṁ // PaumaCa.39

ajiyassa ya uppattī, puṇṇaghaṇasuhā-'suhaṁ samōsaraṇē
vijjāharassa dinnaṁ, saraṇaṁ jaha rakkhasindēṇaṁ // PaumaCa.40

dinnaṁ rakkhasavaïṇā, ṭhāṇaṁ ca varō jahā kumārassa
sagarassa ya uppattī, dukkhaṁ sāmaṇṇa nivāṇaṁ // PaumaCa.41

aïkantamahārakkhō, jammaṇavihavassa kittaṇaṁ cēva
taha rakkhasavaṁsassa ya, ṣavattaṇaṁ cēva nāyavvaṁ // PaumaCa.42

vāṇarakēūṇa tahā, vaṁsuppattī kamēṇa nāyabā
taḍikēsissa ya cariyaṁ, udahikumārēṇa sahiyassa // PaumaCa.43

kikkindhiandhayāṇaṁ, sirimālākhēyarāṇa āgamaṇaṁ
vahaṇaṁ ca vijayasīhassa kōvaṇaṁ asaṇivēyassa // PaumaCa.44


[p. 5]
andhayavahaṁ pavēsō, pāyālaṁkārapuravarē taïyā
kikkindhipuranivēsaṁ, mahugiriuvariṁ maṇabhirāmaṁ // PaumaCa.45

laṅkāgamaṇa-pavēsaṁ, sukēsiputtāṇa balamahantāṇaṁ
nigghāyamaraṇahēū, mālissa ya saṁpayaṁ viulaṁ // PaumaCa.46

vēyaḍḍadakkhiṇāē, sēḍhīē cakkavālanayarammi
indassa ya uppattī, vijjāharasēḍhisāmittaṁ // PaumaCa.47

mālissa vahaṁ jujjhē, vēsamaṇakumārajammaṇuppattī
kusumantavarujjāṇē, sumāliputtassa ya pavēsaṁ // PaumaCa.48

kēkasisahasaṁjōgaṁ, nidarisaṇaṁ tattha paramasumiṇāṇaṁ
jaṇaṇaṁ ca dahamuhassa ya, vijjāsamuvāsaṇaṁ cēva // PaumaCa.49

khōhaṁ jakkhassa aṇāḍhiyassa taha āgamaṁ sumālissa
mandōyarīe lambha, kannāṇa nirikkhaṇaṁ cēva // PaumaCa.50

taha bhāṇukaṇṇacariyaṁ, kōvaṁ vēsamaṇaünbhavaṁ cēva
rakkhasajakkhāṇa raṇaṁ, dhaṇayassa tavō ya nāyavō // PaumaCa.51

dahamuhalaṅkāgamaṇaṁ, avalōyaṇa pucchaṇaṁ jiṇaharāṇaṁ
harisēṇassa ya cariyaṁ, puṇṇaṁ taha pāvamahaṇaṁ ca // PaumaCa.52

gahaṇaṁ mattamahāgayabhuvaṇālaṁkāranāmadhēyassa
ṭhāṇaṁ jamassa laddhaṁ, rikkharayāiccakikkindhī // PaumaCa.53

dahavayaṇa-dūsaṇāṇaṁ, pāyālaṁkārapuravarapavēsaṁ
candōyarassa virahē aṇurāhādukkhasaṁghaṭṭa // PaumaCa.54

taṁ sō virāhiyapurē, suggīvasirīsamāgamaṁ cēva
vālissa khōha aṭṭhāvayanagassa // PaumaCa.55

suggīva sutārāē, lambhaṁ maraṇaṁ ca sāhasagaïssa
saṁtāvaṁ ciya paramaṁ, yaḍḍagamaṁ dahamuhassa // PaumaCa.56

aṇaraṇṇa-sahasakiraṇāṇa tāṇa vēragga jannanāsaṁ ca
mahupubabhavakkhāṇaṁ, uvarambhāē ya ahilāsaṁ // PaumaCa.57

vijāṇaṁ ciya lambha, mahindarāyassa lacchināsaṁ ca
dahamuhamandaragamaṇaṁ, puṇaravi ya niyattaṇaṁ cēva // PaumaCa.58

aṇagāramaharisissa vi, aṇantaviriyassa kēvaluppattī
rāvaṇaniyamaggahaṇaṁ, haṇuyassa samubbhavaṁ cēva // PaumaCa.59

aṭṭhāvayassa uvariṁ, mahinda-palhāyadarisaṇasiṇēhaṁ
pavaṇañjayassa kōvaṁ, taha añjaṇaüjjhaṇaṁ cēva // PaumaCa.60

siṭṭhaṁ ca muṇivarēṇaṁ, haṇuyaparabbhavasamūhasaṁbandhaṁ
sūī haṇurūhapurē, kayā ya paḍisūranāmēṇaṁ // PaumaCa.61


[p. 6]
bhūyāḍavīe majjhē, pavaṇañjayakhēyarassa ya niōgaṁ
taha darisaṇūsavasuhaṁ, vijjāhariañjaṇāe samaṁ // PaumaCa.62

pavaṇañjayaputtamahābalassa taha dāruṇaṁ raṇaṁ paramaṁ
rajaṁ dasāṇaṇassa ya, jiṇaüssēhantaraṁ cēva // PaumaCa.63

bala-kēsava-paḍisattūṇa cēṭṭhiyaṁ cakkavaṭṭipamuhāṇaṁ
dasaraharajjuppattī, kēgaïvarasaṁpayaṁ paramaṁ // PaumaCa.64

indēṇa samaṁ jujjhaṁ, kāūṇa ya gihiyaṁ dahamuhēṇaṁ
saṁvēgasamāvannō, naravaï dikkhaṁ samaṇupattō // PaumaCa.65

rāmassa lakkhaṇassa ya, bharahassa ya taha ya sattunihaṇassa
uppattī sīyāē, vidēha taha sōgasaṁbandhaṁ // PaumaCa.66

nārayasīyālihaṇaṁ, daddūṇa sahōyarassa mūḍhattaṁ
kannāsayaṁvaratthaṁ, uppattī cāvarayaṇassa // PaumaCa.67

dasarahanivassa dikkhaṁ, pāsē muṇisababhūyasaraṇassa
vavagayabhavāṇa kahaṇaṁ, samāgamaṁ cēva sīyāē // PaumaCa.68

kēgaïvarassa lambha, rajaṁ bharahassa paramamāhappaṁ
taha lakkhaṇō ya rāmō, sīyā ya gayā vidēsammi // PaumaCa.69

taha vajjakaṇṇanaravaï-vicēṭṭhiyaṁ varakumārilambhaṁ ca
vasikāraruddabhūī, vimōyaṇaṁ vālikhillassa // PaumaCa.70

aruṇuggāmāsannē, rāmapurinivēsaṇaṁ paramarammaṁ
vaṇamālāsaṁjōyaṁ, aïviriyasamunnaī cēva // PaumaCa.71

lābhō jiyaṣaümāē, kula-dēsavihūsaṇāṇa uvasaggaṁ
vaṁsagirimatthaōvari, jiṇaharakaraṇaṁ ca rāmēṇa // PaumaCa.72

daḍhūṇa dāṇavibhavaṁ, jaḍāuṇō niyamaladdhamāhappaṁ
nāgarahārōhaṁ ciya, saṁbukkavivāyaṇaṁ cēva // PaumaCa.73

kēgaïputtāgamaṇaṁ, kharadūsaṇaviggahaṁ paramaghōraṁ
sīyāharaṇanimittaṁ, sōgaṁ ciya sīyāharaṇanimittaṁ, sōgaṁ ciya rāmadēvassa // PaumaCa.74

sigdhaṁ virāhiyassa ya, āgamaṇaṁ dūsaṇassa ya vahaṁ ca
rayaṇajaḍivijanāsaṁ, suggīvasamāgamaṁ cēva // PaumaCa.75

sāhasagaïssa ya vahaṁ, sīyāṣaḍivattikāraṇaṁ lambhaṁ
milaṇaṁ vihīsaṇēṇaṁ, vijjābalakēsisaṁpattī // PaumaCa.76

taha kumbhayaṇṇa-indaïbhuyaṅga pāsēsu bandhaṇaṁ paramaṁ
lakkhaṇasattiṣahāraṁ, taha ya visallāgamaṁ cēva // PaumaCa.77


[p. 7]
dahamuhaṣavēsaṇaṁ ciya, bhavaṇaṁ jiṇasantisāmināhassa
taha pāḍihēragamaṇaṁ, laṅkāe pavēsaṇaṁ cēva // PaumaCa.78

cakkuppattī taha lakkhaṇassa dahamuhavivāyaṇaṁ cēva
varajuvaīṇa palāvaṁ, āgamaṇaṁ cēva kēvaliṇō // PaumaCa.79

indaïpamuhāṇa tahā, dikkhā sīyāsamāgamaṁ vattaṁ
nārayalakāgamaṇaṁ, sāēyapurīṣavēsaṁ ca // PaumaCa.80

puvabhavāṇa ya cariyaṁ, bharahagayāṇaṁ jahā samakkhāyaṁ
bharahassa ya pavajjā, ṭhaviō ciya lakkhaṇō rajjē // PaumaCa.81

laddhā maṇōramā vi ya, sirivacchālīḍhadēhadhārissa
maraṇaṁ ca samāvannaṁ, sumahallavaṇassa saṁgāmē // PaumaCa.82

mahurāpuridēsassa ya, uvasaggaviṇāsaṇaṁ jaṇavayassa
sattarisīṇa uvattī, sīyānivāsaṇaṁ cēva // PaumaCa.83

aha vajjajaṅghanaravaï, diṭṭhā sīyā lavaṁkusuppattī
jēūṇa naravarindē, piyarēṇa samaṁ kayaṁ jujjhaṁ // PaumaCa.84

sayalajaṇabhūsaṇāṇaṁ, nāṇuppattī surāṇa āgamaṇaṁ
vattaṁ ca pāḍihēraṁ, sīyāē bhīsaṇabhavōhaṁ // PaumaCa.85

ghōraṁ tavōvihāṇaṁ, kayantavayaṇē sayaṁvarē khōhaṁ
dikkhā ya kumārāṇaṁ, bhāmaṇḍaladuggaī cēva // PaumaCa.86

haṇuyassa ya pavajā, lakkhaṇaparalōgagamaṇahēummi
lavaṇaṁkusāṇa ya tavō, rāmapalāvaṁ ca sōgaṁ ca // PaumaCa.87

puvabhavadēvajaṇiyaṁ, dikkhaṁ ciya rāghavassa nigganthaṁ
kēvalanāṇuppattō, tahēva nivāṇagamaṇaṁ ca // PaumaCa.88

saba pi ēvamēyaṁ, suṇantu iha sajjaṇā ya majjhatthā
siddhipahaṁ saṁpattaṁ, paümaṁ vimalēṇa bhāvēṇa // PaumaCa.89

ēyaṁ aṭṭhamarāmadēvacariyaṁ vīrēṇa siṭuṁ purā, pacchā uttamasāhavēhi dhariyaṁ lōgassa ubbhāsiyaṁ
ēttāhē vimalēṇa pāyaḍaphuḍaṁ gāhānibaddhaṁ kayaṁ, suttatthaṁ nisuṇantu saṁpaï mahāpuṇṇaṁ pavittakkharaṁ // PaumaCa.90


iti paümacariē suttavihāṇō nāma uddēsō samattō


---------------------------------------------------------------------

[p. 8]
[sēṇiyaciṁtāvihāṇaṁ]

[magadhā janapadaḥ —]
iha jambudīvadīvē, dakkhiṇabharahē mahantaguṇakaliō
magahā nāma jaṇavaō, nagarā-''garamaṇḍiō rammō // PaumaCa.1

gāma-pura-khēḍa-kabbaḍa-maḍamba-dōṇīmuhēsu parikiṇṇō
gō-mahisi-valavapuṇṇō, dhaṇanivahaniruddhasīmaṣahō // PaumaCa.2

satthāha-sēṭṭhi-gahavaï-kōḍumbiyaṣamuhasuddhajaṇanivahō
maṇi-kaṇaga-rayaṇa-mōttiya-bahudhannamahantakōṭṭhārō // PaumaCa.3

dēsammi tammi lōgō, vinnāṇaviyakkhaṇō aïsurūvō
bala-vihava-kantijuttō, ahiyaṁ dhammujjuyamaīō // PaumaCa.4

naḍa-naṭṭa-chatta-laṅkhayaniccanaccantagīyasaddālō
nāṇāhārapasāhiyabhujāvijjantapahiyajaṇō // PaumaCa.5

ahiyaṁ vīvāhūsavaviyāvaḍō gandhakusumatattillō
bahupāṇa-khāṇa-bhōyaṇa–aṇavarayaṁvaḍḍiucchāhō // PaumaCa.6

pukkharaṇīsu sarēsu ya, ujjāṇēsu ya samantaō rammō
paracakka māri-takkara-dubbhikkhavivajjiō muiō // PaumaCa.7

[rājagr̥hanagaram —]
tassa bahumajjhadēsē, pāyārubbhaḍavisālaparivēḍhaṁ
nayaraṁ ciya pōrāṇaṁ, rāyapuraṁ nāma nāmēṇaṁ // PaumaCa.8

varabhavaṇa-tuṅgatōraṇa-dhavalaṭṭālaya kalaṅkaparimukkaṁ
phalihāsu saṁpaüttaṁ, kavisīsayaviraïyābhōyaṁ // PaumaCa.9


[p. 9]
bahubhaṇḍasāragaruyaṁ, jala-thalayasamiddharayaṇabhariyagharaṁ
nāṇādēsasamāgaya-vaṇiyajaṇullāvasaddālaṁ // PaumaCa.10

bhavaṇaṅgaṇaccaṇēsu ya, maragaya-māṇikkakiraṇakabburiyaṁ
aguruya-turukka-candaṇa-jaṇavayaparibhōyasusuyandhaṁ // PaumaCa.11

cēiyagharēhi ramma, ārāmujjāṇa-kāṇaṇasamiddhaṁ
sara-sarasi-bāvi-vappiṇa-saēsu aïmaṇaharālōvaṁ // PaumaCa.12

caccara-caükkamaṇahara-pēcchaṇayamahantamahuranigdhōsaṁ
paṇḍiyajaṇasusamiddhaṁ, akkhaliyacarittabahusatthaṁ // PaumaCa.13

kiṁ jaṁpiēṇa bahuṇā. taṁ nayaraṁ guṇasahassaāvāsa
amarapurassa ya sōhaṁ, ghēttūṇa va hōja nimmaviyaṁ // PaumaCa.14

[śrēṇīkō rājā —]
ēvaṁvihē ya nayarē, vasaï nivō tattha sēṇiō nāma
naravaïguṇēhi juttō, vēsamaṇō cēva pañcakkhō // PaumaCa.15

bhamaranibhaniddhakēsō, viyasiyavaraṣaümasarisamuhasōhō
ghaṇa-pīṇa-kaḍhiṇakhandhō, thōrunnaya-dīhabāhujuō // PaumaCa.16

vitthiṇṇapihulavacchō, karayalasamagijjhalaliyataṇumajjhō
mayarāyasarisakaḍiyaḍa, samahiyavarahatthihatthōrū // PaumaCa.17

kummavaracārucalaṇō, sōvaṇṇiyapavaō va dippantō
candō va sōmavayaṇō, salilanihī cēva gambhīrō // PaumaCa.18

taṁ natthi jaṁ na yāṇaï, narindavināṇa-nāṇamāhappaṁ
sammattaladdhabuddhī, guru-dēvayapūyaṇasamatthō // PaumaCa.19

vivihakalā-''gamakusalō vi māṇavō tassa varanarindassa
suciraṁ ṣi bhaṇṇamāṇō, guṇāṇa antaṁ na pāvijjā // PaumaCa.20

[sirivīrajiṇacariyaṁ]
[vīrajinajanma, surakr̥tō janmābhiṣēkaśca —]
atthēttha bharahavāsē, kuṇḍaggāmaṁ puraṁ guṇasamiddhaṁ
tattha ya narindavasahō, siddhatthō nāma nāmēṇaṁ // PaumaCa.21


[p. 10]
tassa ya bahuguṇakaliyā, bhajjā tisala tti rūvasaṁpannā
tīē gabbhammi jiṇō, āyāō carimasamayammi // PaumaCa.22

āsaṇakampēṇa surā, muṇiūṇa jiṇēsaraṁ samuppannaṁ
savē vi samuccaliyā, pariōsunbhinnarōmañcā // PaumaCa.23

āgantūṇa ya nayarē, gandhōdayavārivarisaṇaṁ kāuṁ
ghēttūṇa jiṇavarindaṁ, mandarasiharammi saṁpattā // PaumaCa.24

ṭhaviūṇa paṇḍukambala–silāe sīhāsaṇē maṇivicittē
abhisiñcanti surindā, khīrōdahivārikalasēhiṁ // PaumaCa.25

ākampiō ya jēṇaṁ, mērū aṅguṭṭaēṇa līlāē
tēṇēha mahāvīrō, nāma si kayaṁ surindēhiṁ // PaumaCa.26

namiūṇa jiṇavarinda, thōūṇa payāhiṇaṁ ca kāūṇaṁ
puṇaravi māusayāsē, ṭhavēnti dēvā tilōyaguruṁ // PaumaCa.27

suravaïdinnāhārō, aṅguṭṭayaamayalēvalēhēṇaṁ
ummukkabālabhāvō, tīsaïvarisō jiṇō jāō // PaumaCa.28

[vīrasya pravrajyā, jñānaṁ, atiśayāśca —]
aha annayā kayāī, saṁvēgaṁgaō jiṇō muṇiyadōsō
lōgantiyaparikiṇṇō, pabajjamuvāgaō vōrō // PaumaCa.29

aha aṭṭhakammarahiyassa tassa jhāṇōvaōgajuttassa
sayalajagujjōyagaraṁ, kēvalanāṇaṁ samuppannaṁ // PaumaCa.30

ruhiraṁ khīrasavaṇṇaṁ, malasēyavivajjiyaṁ surabhigandhaṁ
dēhaṁ salakkhaṇaguṇaṁ, ravippabhaṁ cēva aïvimalaṁ // PaumaCa.31


[p. 11]
nayaṇā phandaṇarahiyā, nahakēsā'vaṭṭhiyā ya niddhā ya
jōyaṇasayaṁ samantā, mārīi vivajjiō dēsō // PaumaCa.32

jattō ṭhavēi calaṇē, tattō jāyanti sahasapattāī
phalabharanamiyā ya dumā, sāsasamiddhā mahī hōi // PaumaCa.33

āyarisasamā dharaṇī, jāyaï iha addhamāgahī vāṇī
saraē va nimmalāō, disāō raya-rēṇurahiyāō // PaumaCa.34

ṭhāyaï jattha jiṇindō, tattha ya sīhāsaṇaṁ rayaṇacittaṁ
jōyaṇaghōsamaṇaharaṁ, dunduhi surakusumavuṭṭhī ya // PaumaCa.35

ēvaṁ sō muṇivasahō, aṭṭhamahāpāḍihērapariyariō
viharaï jiṇindabhāṇū, bōhintō bhaviyakamalāiṁ // PaumaCa.36

aïsayavihūisahiō, gaṇa-gaṇahara-sayalasaṅghaparivārō
viharantō ciya pattō, viulagirindaṁ mahāvīrō // PaumaCa.37

[kēvalamahimārtha dēvānāmāgamanam —]
nāūṇa dēvarāyā, viulamahāgirivarē jiṇavarindaṁ
ērāvaṇaṁ valaggō, himagirisiharassa saṁkāsaṁ // PaumaCa.38

siṁdūraraïyakumbhaṁ, viraïyanakkhattamālakayasōhaṁ
ghaṇṭāravanigdhōsaṁ, gaṇḍayalubbhinnamayalēhaṁ // PaumaCa.39

gumugumugumantamahuyara-nilōṇamayasurahivāsiyasuyandhaṁ
calacavalakaṇṇacāmara-vāuchuvantadhayamālaṁ // PaumaCa.40

sāmāṇiyaparikiṇṇō, accharasuggīyamāṇamāhappō
sabasurāsurasahiō, viulagiriṁ āgaō indō // PaumaCa.41

daḍhūṇa jiṇavarinda, karayalajuyalaṁ karīya sīsammi
sakō pahaṭṭamaṇasō, thōūṇa jiṇaṁ samāḍhattō // PaumaCa.42

[vīrastutiḥ —]
mōhandhayāratimirē, suttaṁ ciya sayalajīvalōyamiṇaṁ
kēvalakiraṇadivāyara!, tumēva ujjōiyaṁ vimalaṁ // PaumaCa.43


[p. 12]
saṁsārabhavasamuddē, sōgamahāsalilavīisaṁghaṭṭē
pōō tuma mahāyasa!, uttārō bhaviyavaṇiyāṇaṁ // PaumaCa.44

saṁsārabhavakaḍillē, saṁjōgaviōgasōgatarugahaṇē
kupahapaṇaṭṭhāṇa tuma, satthāhō nāha! uppannō // PaumaCa.45

tuha nāha! kō samatthō, sabbhūyaguṇāṇa kuṇaï parisaṁkhā?
suirammi bhaṇṇamāṇō, avi vāsasahassakōḍīhiṁ // PaumaCa.46

thōūṇa dēvarāyā, annē vi caübihā suranikāyā
bhāvēṇa kayapaṇāmā, uvaviṭṭhā sannivēsēsu // PaumaCa.47

magahāhivō vi rāyā, daṭṭaṇa surāgamaṁ jiṇasagāsē
bhaḍacaḍayarēṇa mahayā, tō rāyapurāō nīhariō // PaumaCa.48

pattō ya tamuddēsaṁ, mattamahāgayavarāō uttiṇṇō
thōūṇa jiṇavarindaṁ, uvaviṭṭhō magahasāmantō // PaumaCa.49

[samavasaraṇam —]
puvaviṇimmiyabhāgaṁ, jōyaṇaparivēḍhamaṇḍalābhōyaṁ
pāyāratiuṇamaṇimaya-gōuravitthiṇṇakayasōhaṁ // PaumaCa.50

aha dōṇi ya vakkhārā, aṭṭamahāpāḍihērasaṁjuttā
aṭṭha nāḍayāī, dārē dārē ya naccanti // PaumaCa.51

sōlasa varavāvīō, kamaluppalavimalasalilapuṇṇāō
caüsu vidisāsu majjhē, havanti cattāri cattāri // PaumaCa.52

bhayavaṁ pi tihuyaṇagurū, vicittasīhāsaṇē suhaniviṭṭhō
chattāichatta-cāmara-asōga-bhāmaṇḍalasaṇāhō // PaumaCa.53

ēvaṁvihammi tattō, suravaramēlīṇajaṇasamūhammi
pattēyaṁ pattēyaṁ, vakkhāraṁ kittaïssāmi // PaumaCa.54


[p. 13]
paḍhamammi ya vakkhārē, parisā nigganthamaharisīṇaṁ tu 1
tayaṇantaraṁ pi bīē, sōhammāīsuravahūṇaṁ2 // PaumaCa.55

taïyammi ya vakkhārē, parisā ajāṇa guṇamahantīṇaṁ3
tattō paraṁ tu niyamā, jōisakannāṇa parisā ya4 // PaumaCa.56

vantaravahūṇa tattō5, parisā uṇa bhavaṇavāsiyavahūrṇa6
tattō paraṁ tu niyamā, jōisiyāṇaṁ suravarāṇa7 // PaumaCa.57

vantarabhavaṇindāṇaṁ 8, vakkhārēsu ya havanti parisāō9
sōhammāīṇa taō, dēvāṇaṁ kappavāsīṇaṁ 10 // PaumaCa.58

avarammi ya vakkhārē, parisā maṇuyāṇa naravarindāṇaṁ 11
hōi tirikvāṇa puṇō, parisā puvuttarē bhāgē12 // PaumaCa.59

ēvaṁ pasannacittē, suravaramēlīṇapatthivasamūhē
pucchaï dhammā-'dhamma, titthayaraṁ gōyamō namiḍaṁ // PaumaCa.60

tō addhamāgahīē, bhāsāē sabajīvahiyajaṇaṇaṁ
jalaharagambhīraravō, kahēi dhammaṁ jiṇavarindō // PaumaCa.61

[vīrasya bhagavatō dēśanā —]
davaṁ ca hōi duvihaṁ, jīvā-'jīvā tahēva nāyabaṁ
jīvā havanti duvihā, siddhā saṁsāravantā ya // PaumaCa.62

jē hōnti siddhajīvā, tāṇa aṇantaṁ suhaṁ aṇōvamiyaṁ
akkhayamayalamaṇantaṁ, havaï sayā bāha parimukkaṁ // PaumaCa.63

tattha ya saṁsārasthā, duvihā tasa-thāvarā muṇēyavā
ubhaē vi hunti duvihā, pajattā taha apajjattā // PaumaCa.64

puḍhavi jala jalaṇa māruya, vaṇassaī cēva thāvarā bhaṇiyā
bēindiyāi jāva u, duviha tasā sanni iyarē ya // PaumaCa.65

naṁ taṁ ajīvadavaṁ, dhammā-'dhammāibhēyabhinnaṁ ca
bhavāṇa siddhigamaṇaṁ, taṁ vivarīyaṁ abhavāṇaṁ // PaumaCa.66

micchatta-jōgaṣaccaya, taha ya kasāēsu lēsasahiēsu
ēēsu cēva jīvō, bandhaï asuhaṁ sayā kammaṁ // PaumaCa.67


[p. 14]
nāṇēṇa daṁsaṇēṇa ya, cāritta-tavēṇa sammasahiēṇaṁ
maṇa-vayaṇa-kāyaguttō, ajjiṇaï aṇantayaṁ puṇṇaṁ // PaumaCa.68

aṭṭhavihabhēyabhinnaṁ, kammaṁ saṁkhēvaō samakkhāyaṁ
bajjhanti ya muccanti ya, jīvā pariṇāmajōgēṇaṁ // PaumaCa.69

saṁsāraṣavannāṇaṁ, jīvāṇaṁ visayasaṅgamūḍhāṇaṁ
jaṁ hōi takkhaṇasuhaṁ, taṁ puṇa dukkhaṁ aṇēgavihaṁ // PaumaCa.70

jāva ya nimisapamāṇō, kālō vaccēja narayalōgammi
tāvaṁ ciya natthi suhaṁ, jīvāṇaṁ pāvakammāṇaṁ // PaumaCa.71

damaṇēsu tāḍaṇēsu ya, bandhaṇanibbhacchaṇāidōsēsu
dukkhaṁ tirikkhajīvā, aṇuhavamāṇā ya acchanti // PaumaCa.72

saṁjōga-vippaōgē, lāhā-'lāhē ya rāga-dōsēsu
maṇuyāṇa havaï dukkhaṁ, sārīraṁ māṇasaṁ cēva // PaumaCa.73

appiḍḍiyadēvāṇa vi, daṭṭaṇa mahiḍḍiē surasamūhē
jaṁ uppajjaï dukkhaṁ, tattō guruyaṁ cavaṇakālē // PaumaCa.74

ēyārisammi ghōrē, saṁsārē cāuraṅgamaggami
dukkhēhi navari jīvō, bhaṭṭhō maṇuyattaṇaṁ lahaï // PaumaCa.75

laddhē vi māṇusattē, sabarāikulēsu manda vibhavēsu
uttamakulammi dukkhaṁ, uppattī hōi jīvassa // PaumaCa.76

uppannō vi hu sukulē, vāmaṇa-bahira-'ndha-mūya-kuṇi-khujjō
dukkhēhi lahaï jīvō, nirōgaṣañcindiyaṁ rūvaṁ // PaumaCa.77

sabāṇa sundarāṇaṁ, laddhē vi samāgamē apuṇṇassa
na havijja dhammabuddhī, mūḍhassa u lōbha-mōhēṇaṁ // PaumaCa.78

uppannā vi ya buddhī, dhammassuvariṁ kudhamma-hammēsu
taha vi ya puṇa bhāmijjaï, na lahaï jiṇadēsiyaṁ dhammaṁ // PaumaCa.79

laddhaṇa māṇusattaṁ, jassa na dhammē sayā havaï cittaṁ
tassa kira karayalatthaṁ, amayaṁ naṭuṁ ciya narassa // PaumaCa.80

kēittha dhīrapurisā, cārittaṁ gihiūṇa bhāvēṇa
akkhaṇḍiyacārittā, jāva ṭhiyā uttamajhummi // PaumaCa.81


[p. 15]
annē puṇō vi kēī, vīsaṁ jiṇakāraṇāim̐ bhāvēuṁ
tēlōkkakhōbhaṇakara, aṇantasaükkhaṁ samajanti // PaumaCa.82

annē tavaṁ vigiṭṭa, kāuṁ, thōvāvasēsasaṁsārā
dō tiṇṇi bhavē gantuṁ, nivāṇamaṇuttaramuvēnti // PaumaCa.83

kāūṇa tavamuyāraṁ, ārāhiya dhībalēṇa kālagayā
tē hōnti varaaṇuttara-vimāṇavāsēsu ahamindā // PaumaCa.84

tattō cuyā samāṇā, halahara-cakkaharabhōga-riddhīō
bhōttūṇa sucirakālaṁ, dhamma kāūṇa sijjhanti // PaumaCa.85

ghēttūṇa samaṇadhammaṁ, ghōraparīsahaparāiyā annē
bhajanti saṁjamāō, sēvanti aṇuvayāṇi puṇō // PaumaCa.86

tuṭṭhā havanti annē, darisaṇamēttēṇa jiṇavarindāṇaṁ
paccakkhāṇanivitti, na vi tē suviṇē vi gēhanti // PaumaCa.87

micchattamōhiyamaī, nissīlā nivayā gihārambhē
pavisanti mahāghōraṁ, saṁgāmaṁ visayarasalōlā // PaumaCa.88

annē vi karisaṇāī, bāvārā vivihajantusaṁbādhā
kāūṇa janti narayaṁ, tibamahāvēyaṇaṁ ghōraṁ // PaumaCa.89

māyā-kuḍilasahāvā, kūḍatulā-kūḍamāṇavavahārā
dhammaṁ asaddahantā, tirikkhajōṇī uvaṇamanti // PaumaCa.90

ujjuyadhammāyārā, taṇuyakasāyā sahāvabhaddā ya
majjhimaguṇēhi juttā, lahanti tē māṇusaṁ jammaṁ // PaumaCa.91

aṇuvaya-mahavaēhi ya, bālatavēṇa ya havanti saṁjuttā
tē hōnti dēvalōē, dēvā pariṇāmajōgēṇaṁ // PaumaCa.92


[p. 16]
dasaṇa-nāṇa-carittē, suddhā annōnnakaraṇajōēsu
dēhē vi niravayakkhā, siddhi pāvēnti dhuyakammā // PaumaCa.93

taṁ akkhayaṁ aṇantaṁ, abābāhaṁ sivaṁ paramasōkkhaṁ
pāvanti samaṇasīhā, kammaṭṭhavivajjiyā mōkkhaṁ // PaumaCa.94

caügaïmahāsamuddē, jīvā ghōlanti kammapaḍibaddhā
na ya uttarēja kēī, mōttu jiṇadhammabōhitthaṁ // PaumaCa.95

saṁsāramahāgimhē, dukkhāyavativavēyaṇumhaviyaṁ
jiṇavayaṇamēhasīyala-ulhaviyaṁ sayalajiyalōyaṁ // PaumaCa.96

[śrēṇikasya padmacaritē saṁśayaḥ —]
aha tē suṇittu dhammaṁ, jiṇavaramuhakamalaniggayaṁ dēvā
sammattaladdhabuddhī, gayā ya niyayāim̐ ṭhāṇāī // PaumaCa.97

magahāhivō vi rāyā, vīrajiṇaṁ paṇamiūṇa bhāvēṇaṁ
sabaparivārasahiō, kusagganayaraṁ samaṇupattō // PaumaCa.98

tāva ya divasavasāṇē, atthaṁ ciya diṇayarō samallīṇō
maülanti ya kamalāī, virahō cakkāyamihuṇāṇaṁ // PaumaCa.99

uccharaï tamō gayaṇē, maïlantō disivahē kasiṇavaṇṇō
sajjaṇacariujjōyaṁ, najaï tā dujaṇasahāvō // PaumaCa.100

rāyā vi niyayabhavaṇē, maṇidīvajalantakiraṇavicchuriē
sayaṇē suhappasuttō, kusumapaḍōcchaïyaṣallakē // PaumaCa.101

nidaṁ sēvantō cciya, suviṇē vi puṇō puṇō jiṇavarindaṁ
pēcchaï pucchaï ya taō, saṁsaya paramaṁ payattēṇaṁ // PaumaCa.102

ghaṇagurugabhīragajjiya-niṇāyabahutūrabandisadēṇaṁ
aha uṭṭiō mahappā, thuvantō maṅgalasaēhiṁ // PaumaCa.103


[p. 17]
cintēūṇa pavattō, bhaṇiyaṁ vīrēṇa dhammasaṁjuttaṁ
cakkaharāinarāṇaṁ, bhuvaṇamiṇaṁ havaï parihāṇaṁ // PaumaCa.104

paümacariyammi ēttō, maṇō mahaṁ kuṇaï paramasaṁdēhaṁ
kaha vāṇarēhi nihayā, rakkhasavasahā aïbalā vi? // PaumaCa.105

jiṇavaradhammēṇaṁ ciya, mahaïmahākulasamubbhavā jāyā
vijjāsayāṇa pāraṁ, gayā ya balagabiyā vīrā // PaumaCa.106

suvanti lōyasatthē, rāvaṇapamuhā ya rakkhasā savē
vasa-lōhiya-maṁsāī-bhakkhaṇa-pāṇē kayāhārā // PaumaCa.107

kira rāvaṇassa bhāyā, mahābalō nāma kumbhayaṇṇō tti
chammāsaṁ vigayabhaō, sējjāsu nirantaraṁ suyaï // PaumaCa.108

jaï vi ya gaēsu aṅga, pēllijjaï garuyapavayasamēsu
tēllaghaḍēsu ya kaṇṇā, pūrijantē suyantassa // PaumaCa.109

paḍupaḍahatūrasadaṁ, na suṇaï sō sammuhaṁ pi vajantaṁ
na ya uṭṭēi mahappā, sējjāē apuṇṇakālammi // PaumaCa.110

aha uḍhiō vi santō, asaṇamahā (ṇāmaha) ghōraparigayasarīrō
puraō havēja jō sō, kuñjara-mahisāiṇō gilaï // PaumaCa.111

kāūṇa udarabharaṇaṁ, sura-māṇusa-kuñjarāibahuēsu
puṇaravi sējjārūḍhō, bhayarahiō suyaï chammāsaṁ // PaumaCa.112

annaṁ pi ēva subaï, jaha indō rāvaṇēṇa saṁgāmē
jiṇiūṇa niyalabaddhō, laṅkānayarī samāṇīō // PaumaCa.113

kō niṇiūṇa samatthō, indaṁ sasurā-'surē vi tēlōkkē
jō sāgarapērantaṁ, jambuddīvaṁ samuddharaï // PaumaCa.114

ērāvaṇō gaïndō, jassa ya vajaṁ amōhapaharatthaṁ
tassa kira cintiēṇa vi, annō vi bhavēja masirāsiṁ(sī) // PaumaCa.115

sīhō maēṇa nihaō, sāṇēṇa ya kuñjarō jahā bhaggō
taha vivarīyaṣayatthaṁ, kaīhi rāmāyaṇaṁ raïyaṁ // PaumaCa.116

aliyaṁ pi sabamēyaṁ, uvavattiviruddhapaccayaguṇēhiṁ
na ya saddahanti purisā, havanti jē paṇḍiyā lōē // PaumaCa.117

ēvaṁ cintantō cciya, saṁsayaparihārakāraṇaṁ rāyā
jiṇadarisaṇussuyamaṇō, gamaṇucchāhō taō jāō // PaumaCa.118


[p. 18]
varakamalanibaddhā niggayālīsamattā, mahurasaranināyāccantarammā ṣadēsā
taruṣavaṇavalamgā puppharēṇuṁ muyantā, vimalakiraṇamantāiccabhāsā visuddhā // PaumaCa.119


iya paümacariē sēṇiyacintāvihāṇō nāma biīyō samuddēsaō samattō

[vijjāharalōgavaṇṇaṇaṁ]

[śrēṇikasya gaütamapārśvē gamanam , pr̥cchā ca —]
atthāṇimaṇḍavatthō, sabālaṁkārabhūsiyasarīrō
sāmantamaüḍamōttiya-kiraṇasamujjaliyapāvīḍhō // PaumaCa.1

sō tattha magaharāyā, muṇidarisaṇakāraṇē kaücchāhō
āruhaï varagaïndaṁ, parihatthaṁ lakkhaṇaṣasatthaṁ // PaumaCa.2

aha niggaō purāō, gayavararahajōhaturayaparikiṇṇō
vaccaï narindavasahō, jattha'cchaï gōyamō bhayavaṁ // PaumaCa.3

pattō ya taṁ paēsaṁ, muṇivaragaṇasaṅghamajjhayārammi
pēcchaï gaṇaharavasahaṁ, sarayaraviṁ cēva tēēṇaṁ // PaumaCa.4

ōyariya gayavarāō, kāūṇa ṣayāhiṇaṁ muṇiṁ rāyā
paṇamaï pahaṭṭhamaṇasō, añjalimaülaṁ sirē kāuṁ // PaumaCa.5

dinnāsīsa ciya sō, uvaviṭhṭhō muṇivarassa pāmūlē
dēhakusalāi savaṁ, pucchaï paramēṇa viṇaēṇaṁ // PaumaCa.6

nāūṇa ya patthāvaṁ, puṇaravi viṇaōvayārasaṁjuttō
saṁsayatimirāvaharaṁ, aha pucchaï gōyamaṁ rāyā // PaumaCa.7

paümacariyaṁ mahāyasa!, ahayaṁ icchāmi pariphuḍaṁ sōuṁ
uppāiyā pasiddhī, kusatthavādīhi vivarīyā // PaumaCa.8

jaï rāvaṇō mahāyasa!, nisāyarō suravarō va aïviriō
kaha sō parihūō cciya, vāṇaratiriēhi raṇamajjhē // PaumaCa.9

rāmēṇa kaṇayadēhō, sarēṇa bhinnō maō araṇṇammi

[lōkaḥ —]

bhajjā sumaṅgalā jiṇa-varassa nandā taō bhavē bīyā
bharahāikumārāṇaṁ, puttasayaṁ tassa uppannaṁ // PaumaCa.119

dōṇi ya varadhūyāō, jōvaṇa-lāyaṇṇa-kanti-kaliyāō
bambhī vi sundarī vi ya, jaṇammi vikkhāyakittīō // PaumaCa.120

sāmanta-bhaḍa-purōhiya-sēṇāvaï-sēṭi-bhōiyāṇaṁ ca
dāvēi rāyanīī, lōgassa vi lōgasaṁbandhaṁ // PaumaCa.121

ēva rāyavarasiriṁ, bhuñjantassa u aïcchiō kālō
nīlaṁ vāsaṁ daṭuṁ, saṁvēgaparāyaṇō jāō // PaumaCa.122

karṭa ahō! vilambaï, lōō parapēsaṇēsu āsattō
ummattaō va naccaï, kuṇaï ya bahucēṭṭhiyasayāī // PaumaCa.123

maṇuyattaṇaṁ asāraṁ, vijulayācañcalaṁ havaï jīyaṁ
bahurōga-sōgakimikula-bhāyaṇabhūyaṁ havaï dēhaṁ // PaumaCa.124

dukkhaṁ suhaṁ ti mannaï, jīvō visayāmisēsu aṇurattō
puṇaravi bahuṁ vinaḍiuṁ, na muṇaï āuṁ parigalantaṁ // PaumaCa.125

ēyaṁ ciya visayasuhaṁ, asāsayaṁ ujjhiūṇa nissaṅgō
siddhisuhakāraṇatthaṁ, karēmi tava-saṁjamujjōyaṁ // PaumaCa.126

jāva ya cintēi imaṁ, saṁsārōcchēyakāraṇaṁ usabhō
tāva ya bhisantamaüḍā, dēvā lōgantiyā pattā // PaumaCa.117

kāūṇa sirapaṇāmaṁ, bhaṇanti sāhu tti nāha! paḍibuddhō
vōcchinnassa subahuō, kālō iha siddhimaggassa // PaumaCa.128


[p. 28]
ēē bhamanti jīvā, puṇaruttaṁ jammasāyarē bhīmē
jiṇavayaṇapōyalaggā, tarantu mā ṇē cirāvēhi // PaumaCa.129

ēvaṁ daḍhavavasāyassa tassa nikkhamaṇakāraṇē dēvā
turiyaṁ ca samaṇupattā, surindaṣamuhā caüviyappā // PaumaCa.130

namiūṇa jiṇavarinda, jayasadālā ya saharisaṁ tuṭṭhā
dhaya-chatta-cārucāmara-calantakarapallavasaṇāhā // PaumaCa.131

vajindanīla maragaya-candaṇamaṇikhaciyakaṇayaparivēḍhaṁ
āruhaï surasamāhiya-khandhaṁ tu sudaṁsaṇaṁ sibiyaṁ // PaumaCa.132

aha niggaō mahappā, nayarāō 'sura-narindaparikiṇṇō
tūrasahassasamāhaya–bandiyaṇugghuṭṭhajayasaddō // PaumaCa.133

varabaüla-tilaya-campaya-asōga-punnāga-nāgasusabhiddha
pattō pavarujjāṇaṁ, vasantatilayaṁ ti nāmēṇaṁ // PaumaCa.134

āpucchiūṇa savaṁ, māyā-piya-putta-sayaṇa-parivaggaṁ
tō muyaï bhūsaṇāī, kaḍisuttaya-kaḍaya-vatthāī // PaumaCa.135

siddhāṇa namukkāra, kāūṇa ya pañcamuṭṭhiyaṁ lōyaṁ
caühi sahassēhi samaṁ, pattō ya jiṇō paramadikkhaṁ // PaumaCa.136

vaïjjāuhō vi tāhē, kēsē maṇiṣaḍalayammi ghēttūṇaṁ
kāūṇa sirapaṇāmaṁ, khīrasamuddammi pakkhivaï // PaumaCa.137

nikkhamaṇamahāmahimaṁ, dēvā kāūṇa suravarasamaggā
namiūṇa jiṇavarinda, gayā ya niyayāim̐ ṭhāṇāī // PaumaCa.138

caühi sahassēhi samaṁ, samaṇāṇaṁ jiṇavarō mahābhāgō
gahiuvavāsō viharaï, vasuhaṁ saṁvaccharaṁ dhīrō // PaumaCa.139

kēēttha paḍhamamāsē, bīē taïē u jāva chammāsē
parisahabhaḍēhi tāva ya, bhaggā samaṇā aparisēsā // PaumaCa.140

bharahassa bhaēṇa gharaṁ, na ēnti taṇhāchuhākilantā vi
lajjāē gāravēṇa ya, tāhē raṇṇaṁ parivasanti // PaumaCa.141

aha tē chuhākilantā, phalāim̐ giṇhanti pāyavagaṇēsu
ambaratalammi ghuṭuṁ, mā gēṇhaha samaṇarūvēṇa // PaumaCa.142


[p. 29]
tāhē vakkalacīvara-kusapattaniyaṁsaṇā phalāhārā
sacchandamaïviyappā, bahubhēyā tāvasā jāyā // PaumaCa.143

[vidyādharāṇāmutpattiḥ —]
tāva ya jiṇassa pāsē, pattā nami-viṇami bhōgavarakaḍī
kāūṇa sirapaṇāma, pāyabbhāsē suhaniviṭṭhā // PaumaCa.144

bhōgasamuhāṇa tāṇaṁ, dharaṇindō āsaṇē taō caliē
sabaparivārasahiō, sō vi tahiṁ cēva saṁpattō // PaumaCa.145

namiūṇa pāyakamalē, uvaviṭhṭhō jiṇavarassa āsannē
pēcchaï taruṇajuvāṇē, 'dōṇṇi jaṇē ṣaṅkayadalacchē // PaumaCa.146

aha bhaṇaï nāgarāyā, bhō bhō! tumhēttha kiṁnimittēṇaṁ
asilaṭṭhigahiyahatthā, ubhaō vi ṭhiyā jiṇasayāsē? // PaumaCa.147

tō bhaṇaï namī vayaṇaṁ, amhaṁ natthēttha rāyavaralacchī
ēyanimittaṁ ca pahū!, jiṇassa pāsaṁ samallīṇā // PaumaCa.148

ēvaṁ ca bhaṇiyamētē, dharaṇēṇaṁ tassa balasamiddhāō
dinnāō takkhaṇaṁ ciya, vijjāō'ṇēyarūvāō // PaumaCa.149

uvaïṭṭhō ya nagavarō, vēyaḍḍhō tāṇa uttamō vāsō
pannāsa jōyaṇāī, vitthiṇṇō suddharayayamaō // PaumaCa.150

ubiddhō paṇavīsā, dōsu ya sēḍhīsu ubhayaō rammō
chajjōyaṇāim̐ dharaṇiṁ, kōsō cciya hōi ubēhō // PaumaCa.151

dakkhiṇasēḍhī gantuṁ, rahanēuracakavālapamuhāiṁ
pannāsa puravarāī, kayāim̐ namikhēyarindēṇa // PaumaCa.152

aha gayaṇavallahapuraṁ, uttarasēḍhīe [viṇami vikkhāyaṁ
varabhavaṇa-tuṅgatōraṇa-bahujiṇaharamaṇḍiyaṁ ca kayaṁ // PaumaCa.153

tattō ya dasagamittā, uvariṁ gandhava-kinnarāīṇaṁ
varabhavaṇamaṇḍiyāī, kiṁpurisāṇaṁ ca nayarāiṁ // PaumaCa.154

uvariṁ taō vi gantuṁ, pañca'nnē jōyaṇē siharapaṭuṁ
jiṇabhavaṇēsu maṇaharaṁ, unbhāsēntaṁ dasa disāō // PaumaCa.155

bhavaṇēsu tēsu niyayaṁ, cāraṇasamaṇā vasanti guṇavantā
sajjhāya-jhāṇanirayā, tavatēyasirīe dippantā // PaumaCa.156


[p. 30]
bahugāma-nayara-paṭṭaṇa-ārāmujjāṇa-kāṇaṇasamiddhā
maṇi-rayaṇa-kañcaṇujjala-jalantagharanivahapantīō // PaumaCa.157

varamahisi-gāipaürō, bahuvihadhaṇṇēṇa maṇaharālōō
sabōsahisaṁpannō, mahu-khīra-ghaēṇa pajjhariō // PaumaCa.158

aïuṇha-sīyarahiō, uvaghāyavivajiō payaïsōmō
najjaï ya dēvalōō, dēsō vijjāharāiṇṇō // PaumaCa.159

ravikiraṇakōmalāhaya-viyasiyavarakamalasarisavayaṇāō
vijjāharajuvaīō, bahuvihalāyaṇṇakaliyāō // PaumaCa.160

vijjāharā u tattha vi, vijābaladappagaviyā sūrā
dēvā va dēvalōē, bhuñjanti jahicchiē bhōē // PaumaCa.161

ēvaṁvihā ubhayasēḍhigayā mahantā, āhāra-pāṇa-sayaṇā-''saṇasaṁpaüttā
vijjāharā aṇuhavanti suhaṁ samiddhaṁ, dhamma karinti vimalaṁ ca jiṇōvaï8 // PaumaCa.162

[śrēyāṁsagr̥hē r̥ṣabhasya bhikṣāprāptiḥ —]

ghuṭaṁ ca ahō dāṇaṁ, dunduhighaṇagurugahīrasaddālaṁ

tō amara-cāraṇagaṇā, bhaṇanti sādhu tti paramapurisa! tumē

ēvaṁ kāūṇa jiṇō, pavattaṇaṁ dāṇavantacariyāē

[p. 32]

lōgā-'lōgapagāsaṁ, kēvalanāṇaṁ samuppannaṁ // PaumaCa.17

uppannammi ya nāṇē, uppajjaï āsaṇaṁ jiṇindassa

kappaḍumō ya dibō, dunduhighōsaṁ ca pupphavarisaṁ ca

nāūṇa samuppatti, kēvalanāṇassa āgayā dēvā
kāūṇa jiṇapaṇāmaṁ, uvaviṭhṭhā sannivēsēsu // PaumaCa.20

[r̥ṣabhajinadēśanā —]
bhaṇiyaṁ ca gaṇaharēṇaṁ, bhayavaṁ jīvā aṇantasaṁsārē
parihiṇḍanti aṇāhā, tāṇuttāraṁ parikahēhi // PaumaCa.21

aha sāhiuṁ payattō, jalaharagambhīramahuranigghōsō

pañca ya mahatvayāī, samiīō pañca tiṇṇi guttīō
ēsō hu samaṇadhammō, jōgavisēsēṇa bahubhēō // PaumaCa.23

pañcāṇubayajuttō, sattahi sikkhāvaēhi parikiṇṇō
ēsō viṁ sāvayāṇaṁ, dhammō uddēsavirayāṇaṁ // PaumaCa.24

dhammēṇa lahaï jīvō, sura-māṇusaparamasōkkhamāhappaṁ
dukkhasahassāvāsaṁ, pāvaï narayaṁ ahammēṇaṁ // PaumaCa.25

mēhēṇa viṇā vuṭṭhī, na hōi na ya bīyavajjiyaṁ sassaṁ
taha dhammēṇa virahiyaṁ, na ya sōkkhaṁ hōi jīvāṇaṁ // PaumaCa.26

jaï vi hu tavaṁ vigiṭṭa, karanti annāṇiyā payattēṇaṁ

[p. 33]
tē bhavasahassapaürē, saṁsārē cāuraṅgamaggammi
dukkhāṇi aṇuhavantā, aṇantakālaṁ paribhamanti // PaumaCa.28

jiṇavaradhammaṁ kāūṇa, nivvuyā hōnti kēi ahamindā
kappālayāhivattaṁ, avarē pāvanti daḍhadhammā // PaumaCa.29

sōūṇa dhammavayaṇaṁ, jiṇavarakahiyaṁ narā-'marasamūhā

kēittha samaṇasīhā, havanti vavagayapariggahā-''rambhā

ēvaṁ sura-naravasahā, kahāvasāṇē jiṇaṁ paṇamiūṇaṁ
sabaï pariyaṇasahiyā, gayā ya niyayāim̐ ṭhāṇāī // PaumaCa.33

viharaï jattha jiṇindō, sō dēsō saggasannihō hōi

aha usahasēṇapamuhā, caürāsīyaṁ tu gaṇaharā tassa

tāva ya cakkaharattaṁ, saṁpattaṁ bharaharāiṇā sayalaṁ

usabhajiṇassa bhagavō, puttasayaṁ candasūrasarisāṇaṁ

takkhasilāe mahappā, bāhubalī tassa niccapaḍikūlō

aha ruṭṭhō cakkaharō, tassuvariṁ sayalasāhaṇasamaggō

pattō takkhasilapuraṁ, jayasadugghuṭṭhakalayalārāvō

[p. 34]
baladappagabiyāṇaṁ, ubhayabalāṇaṁ rasantatūrāṇaṁ
ābhiṭṭaṁ paramaraṇaṁ, naccantakabandhapēcchaṇayaṁ // PaumaCa.42

[bāhubalidīkṣā —]
jaṁpaï ahō! akajjaṁ, jaṁ jāṇantā vi visayalōbhillā

[bharatasya r̥ddhiḥ —]

[brāhmaṇānāmutpattiḥ —]
aha ēvaṁ parikahiē, puṇaravi magahāhivō ṣaṇamiūṇaṁ
pucchaï gaṇaharavasahaṁ, maṇaharamahurēhi vayaṇēhiṁ // PaumaCa.64

[p. 36]
ēvaṁ ca bhaṇiyamēttē, gaṇaharavasahō kahēi bhūyatthaṁ
nisuṇēhi tāva naravaï, ēgamaṇō māhaṇuppattiṁ // PaumaCa.67

sāēyapuravarīē, ēgantē nābhinandaṇō bhayavaṁ
ciṭṭhaï susaṅghasahiō, tāva ya bharahō samaṇupattō // PaumaCa.68

paṇaüttamaṅgamaggō, karajuyalaṁ kariya tassa pāmūlē
tō bhaṇaï cakkavaṭṭī, vayaṇamiṇaṁ mē nisāmēha // PaumaCa.69

bhayavaṁ! aṇuggahatthaṁ, karantu samaṇā imē samiyaṣāvā
bhuñjantu majjha gēhē, parisuddhaṁ phāsuyāhāraṁ // PaumaCa.70

tō bhaṇaï jiṇavarindō, bharaha na kappaï imō u āhārō
samaṇāṇa saṁjayāṇaṁ, kīyagaḍuddēsaniṣphaṇṇō // PaumaCa.71

ēvaṁ suṇittu vayaṇaṁ, rāyā cintēi tāgayamaṇēṇaṁ
uggaṁ tavōvihāṇaṁ caranti samaṇā samiyamōhā // PaumaCa.72

na ya bhuñjanti maharisī, maha gēhē maggiyā vi puṇaruttaṁ
tō sāvayāṇa dāṇaṁ, dēmi phuḍaṁ anna-pāṇāi // PaumaCa.73

ētē vi ya gihidhammē, pañcāṇuvayaguṇēsu uvaüttā
bhuñjāvēmi ya bahusō, hōhī dāṇassa puṇṇaphalaṁ // PaumaCa.74

saddāviyā ya tēṇaṁ, sāyāracarittadhāriṇō sakē
turiyaṁ ca samallīṇā, micchattāī narā taïyā // PaumaCa.75

na ya tē riyanti bhavaṇaṁ, dadu java-vīhiyaṅku rē puraō
kāgaṇirayaṇēṇa taō, suttaṁ ciya sāvayāṇa kayaṁ // PaumaCa.76

tō anna-pāṇa-dāṇā''saṇēsu saṁpūiyāṇa uṣpannaṁ
gavaṁ ciya aïtuṅgaṁ, vahanti itthaṁ kayattha'mhē // PaumaCa.77

maïsāyarēṇa bhaṇiō, bharahanarindō sahāē majjhammi
jaha jiṇavarēṇa bhaṇiyaṁ, taṁ ēkkamaṇō nisāmēhi // PaumaCa.78

jāṇaṁ tumē narāhiva! sammāṇō paḍhamasāvayāṇa kaō
tē vīrassa'vasāṇē, hōhinti kutitthaṣāsaṇḍā // PaumaCa.79

aliyavayaṇēsu satthaṁ, kāūṇaṁ vēyanāmadhēyaṁ tē
hiṁsābhāsaṇamittaṁ, jannēsu pasū vahissanti // PaumaCa.80

vivarīyavittidhammā, ārambha-pariggahēsu aṇiyattā
sayamēva mūḍhabhāvā, sēsaṁ pi jaṇaṁ vimōhanti // PaumaCa.81


[p. 37]
sōūṇa vayaṇamēyaṁ, parikuviō naravaī bhaṇaï ēvaṁ
sigdhaṁ ciya nayarāō, savē vi karēha nidēsā // PaumaCa.82

lōgēṇa hammamāṇā, saraṇaṁ titthaṁkaraṁ samallīṇā
tēṇa ya nivāriyā tē, pattharapaharēsu hammantā // PaumaCa.83

mā haṇasuputta! ēē, jaṁ usabhajiṇēṇa vāriō bharahō
tēṇa imē sayala cciya, vuccanti ya māhaṇā lōē // PaumaCa.84

jē vi ya tē ṣaḍhamayaraṁ, pavajaṁ gēṇhiūṇa parivaḍiyā
tē vakkalaparihāṇā, tāvasapāsaṇḍiṇō jāyā // PaumaCa.85

tāṇa ya sīsa-pasīsā, mōhantā naṇavayaṁ kusatthēsu
bhiggaṅgiramādīyā, jāyā bījaṁ vasumaīē // PaumaCa.86

ēsā tē parikahiyā, uppattī māhaṇāṇa bhūyatthaṁ
ēttō suṇasu narāhiva, puradēvajiṇassa nivāṇaṁ // PaumaCa.87

bhayavaṁ tilōyanāhō, dhammapadaṁ darisiūṇa lōgassa
aṭṭhāvayammi sēlē, nivāṇamaṇuttaraṁ pattō // PaumaCa.88

bharahō vi cakkavaṭṭī, tiṇamiva caïūṇa rāyavaralacchō
jiṇavarapahaṣaḍivannō, abārāhaṁ sivaṁ pattō // PaumaCa.89

ēvaṁ maē sēṇiya! tujjha siṭṭhā, lōgaṭṭiī puvajaṇāṇuciṇṇā
suṇāhi ēttō vimalappahāvā, cattāri nāmēhi narindavaṁsā // PaumaCa.90


iti paümacariē lōgaṭṭii-usabha-māhaṇāhigārō nāma caütthō uddēsaō samattō

[rakkhasavaṁsāhiyārō]

cattāri mahāvaṁsā, naravaï puhaïmmi jē u vikkhāyā
tāṇaṁ puṇa bahubhēyā, havanti avarassa saṁjuttā // PaumaCa.1

ikkhāga paḍhamavaṁsō, biiō sōmō ya hōi nāyabō
vijjāharāṇa taïō, havaï caütthō u harivaṁsō // PaumaCa.2


[p. 38]
[ikṣvākuvaṁśaḥ —]
bharahassa paḍhamaputtō, āiccajasō tti nāma vikkhāō
tassa ya sīhajasō cciya, puttō tassēva balabhaddō // PaumaCa.3

vasubala mahābalō ciya, amiyabalō cēva hōi nāyabō
jāō subhaddanāmō, sāyarabhaddō ya ravitēō // PaumaCa.4

sasipaha pabhūyatēō, tēyassī tāvaṇō payāvī ya
aïviriō ya narindō, tassa ya puttō mahāviriō // PaumaCa.5

uiyaparakkamanāmō, tassa vi ya mahindavikkamō puttō
sūrō indajuiṇṇō, mahaï mahāindaī rāyā // PaumaCa.6

tattō pabhū bibhū vi ya, aridamaṇō cēva vasahakēū ya
rāyā vi ya garuḍakō, taha ya miyaṅkō samuppannō // PaumaCa.7

ētē naravaravasahā, puhaïṁ dāūṇa niyayaputtāṇaṁ
nikkhantā khāyajasā, sivamayalamaṇuttaraṁ pattā // PaumaCa.8

ēsō tē parikahiō, āicca sāisaṁbhavō vaṁsō
ēttō suṇāhi naravara! uppattī sōmavaṁsassa // PaumaCa.9

[sōmavaṁśa: —]
usabhassa bīyaputtō, bāhubalī nāma āsi vikkhāō
tassa ya mahappabhāvō, puttō sōmappabhō nāma // PaumaCa.10

ēttō mahābalō ciya, subalō bāhubali ēvamāīyā
sōmappahassa vaṁsē, uppannā naravaī bahusō // PaumaCa.11

kēēttha gayā mōkkhaṁ, pavajaṁ gihiūṇa dhuyakammā
avarē puṇa dēvattaṁ, pattā tava-saṁjamabalēṇaṁ // PaumaCa.12

ēvaṁ tu sōmavaṁsō, naravaï! kahiō maē samāsēṇaṁ
vijjāharāṇa vaṁsaṁ, bhaṇāmi ēttō nisāmēhi // PaumaCa.13

[vidyādharavaṁśaḥ —]
nāmēṇa rayaṇamālī, namirāyasuō mahābalasamiddhō
tassa vi ya rayaṇavajjō, rayaṇarahō cēva uppannō // PaumaCa.14


[p. 39]
jāō ya rayaṇacittō, candarahō vajjasaṅghanāggē ya
sēṇō ya vajadattō, rāyā vajjaddhaō jāō // PaumaCa.15

vajjāuhō ya vajō, suvajja vajaṁgharō mahāsattō
vajjābha vajjabāhū, vajjaṅkō nāma vikkhāō // PaumaCa.16

aha vajjasundarō vi ya, vajjāsō vajapāṇirāyā ya
uppannō ya naravaī, vajjasujaṇhū ya vajjō ya // PaumaCa.17

vijūmuhō suvayaṇō, rāyā taha vijudattanāmō ya
vijū ya vijutēō, taḍivēō bijudāḍhō ya // PaumaCa.18

ēē khēyaravasahā, vijjā-bala-siddhisārasaṁpuṇṇā
dāūṇa rāyalacchī, suēsu kālēṇa vōlīṇā // PaumaCa.19

aha annayā kayāī, dōsu vi sēḍhīsu sāmiō rāyā
nāmēṇa vijjudāḍhō, avaravidēhaṁ gaō sahasā // PaumaCa.20

diṭṭhō ya saṁjayantō, tēṇa bhamantēṇa saṁjamārūḍhō
ghēttūṇa pāvaguruṇā, ihāṇiō pañcasaṁgamayaṁ // PaumaCa.21

ṭhaviūṇa girivarindē, pattharapaharēhi khēyarasamaggō
āhaṇaï niraṇukampō, taha vi ya jōgaṁ na chaḍḍa i // PaumaCa.22

uvasaggammi bahuvihē, tassa sahantassa jōgajuttassa
samacittassa bhagavaō, uppannaṁ kēvalaṁ nāṇaṁ // PaumaCa.23

ēyammi dēsa kālē, dharaṇindō āgaō muṇisayāsa
namiūṇa tassa calaṇē, vijākōsaṁ taō haraï // PaumaCa.24

jiṇabhavaṇa-muṇivarāṇaṁ, uvariṁ gacchējja jō balummattō
sō vijjāparibhaṭṭō, hōhī vijjāharō niyamā // PaumaCa.25

kāuṇa samayamēyaṁ, vijjāō samappiūṇa dharaṇindō
pucchaï muṇivaravasahaṁ, ghōruvasaggassa saṁbandhaṁ // PaumaCa.26

aha bhaṇaī saṁjayantō, caügaïvitthiṇṇadīhasaṁsārē
gāmē u sayaḍanāmē, kaha vi bhamantō samuppannō // PaumaCa.27

vaṇiyakulammi hiyakarō, nāmēṇa ahaṁ susāhupaḍisēvī
ajjava-maddavajuttō, jāō pariṇāmajōgēṇaṁ // PaumaCa.28

kālaṁ kāūṇa taō, kusumāvaïsāmiō samuppannō
sirivaddhaṇō tti nāmaṁ, jāō haṁ naravaī taïyā // PaumaCa.29


[p. 40]
tatthēva āsi gāmē, vippō sō kucchiyaṁ tavaṁ kāuṁ
kālagaō suralōē, dēvō apṣiḍḍiō jāō // PaumaCa.30

tattō cuō samāṇō, jalaṇasihō bambhaṇō samuppannō
sirivaddhaṇassa taïyā, purōhiō sañcavāī sō // PaumaCa.31

vaṇiyassa tēṇa dabaṁ, avalattaṁ tattha niyamadattassa
gaṇiyāe taō vippō, nāmāmudaṁ niō jūē // PaumaCa.32

gantūṇa tassa gēhaṁ, nāmāmuddacchalēṇa rayaṇāī
cēḍīē āṇiūṇaṁ, samappiyāiṁ ca vaṇiyassa // PaumaCa.33

ghēttūṇa ya sabassa, vippō nivāsiō puravarāu
vēraggasamāvannō, kāūṇa tavaṁ samāḍhattō // PaumaCa.34

mariūṇa ya māhindē, dēvō hōūṇa varavimāṇammi
tattō cuō samāṇō, uppannō vijudāḍhō tti // PaumaCa.35

sidivaddhaṇō vi ya tavaṁ, kāuṁ dēvattaṇāu caviūṇaṁ
avaravidēhammi taō, jāō haṁ saṁjayantamuṇī // PaumaCa.36

tēṇāṇubandhajaṇiō, kōvaggī darisaṇindhaṇāiṇṇō
vijjāharassa ēṇhi, uvasagganihēṇa pajjaliō // PaumaCa.37

jō āsi niyamadattō, sō vihu dhammaṁ puṇō samajjēuṁ
mariūṇa tumaṁ ēsō, dharaṇindattē samuppannō // PaumaCa.38

sōūṇa pagayamēyaṁ, khāmēūṇaṁ muṇiṁ sadharaṇindaṁ
paricayaï visayasōkkhaṁ, dikkhābhimuhō nivō jāō // PaumaCa.39

dharaṇindō muṇivasahaṁ, kāūṇa payāhiṇaṁ ca tikkhuttō
sabaparivārasahiō, niyayaṭṭhāṇaṁ gaō sahasā // PaumaCa.40

aha tattha vijudāḍhassa nandaṇō daḍharahō tti nāmēṇaṁ
tassa vi ya paṭṭabandhaṁ, kāūṇa tavaṁ gaō mōkkhaṁ // PaumaCa.41

tattō ya āsadhammō, jāō assāyarō kumāravarō
āsaddhaō narindō, paümanihō paümamālī ya // PaumaCa.42

paümaraha sīhavāhō, mayadhammō mēhasīha saṁbhūō
sīhaddhaō sasaṅkō, candakō candasiharō ya // PaumaCa.43

indarahō candarahō, sasaṅkadhammō ya āuhō cēva
rattaṭṭhō haricandō, puracandō puṇṇacandō ya // PaumaCa.44

vālinda candacūḍō, gayaṇindu durāṇaṇō naravarindu
rāyā ya ēkacūḍō, dōcūḍa ticūḍa caücūḍō // PaumaCa.45

jāō ya vajacūḍō, bahucūḍō sōhacūḍanāmō ya
jalaṇajaḍi akkatēō, ēvaṁ vijjāharā bahusō // PaumaCa.46


[p. 41]
kēēttha gayā mōkkhaṁ, annē puṇa varavimāṇavāsēsa
uvavannā guṇapuṇṇā, jiṇavaradhammāṇubhāvēṇaṁ // PaumaCa.47

[ajitajinacaritam —]
ēvaṁ tē parikahiō, vaṁsō vijjāharāṇa saṁkhēvaṁ
ēttō suṇasu narāhiva, bīyajiṇindassa uppattī // PaumaCa.48

usabhajiṇajammasamaē, jē suhayarā lōē
ōsariūṇa pavattā, āu-balussēha-tava-niyamā // PaumaCa.49

paraṁparāē, samaïkvantēsu puhaïṣālēsu
sāēyapuravarīē, dharaṇidharō naravarō jāō // PaumaCa.50

tassa ya guṇāṇurūvō, puttō tiyasaṁjaō samuppannō
tassa vi ya indalēhā, bhajjā puttō ya jiyasattū // PaumaCa.51

pōyaṇapurammi rāyā, āṇandō tassa kamalamāla tti
mahilā rūvapaḍāgā, vijayā ya suyā varakumārī // PaumaCa.52

pariṇīyā guṇapuṇṇā, jiyasattunarāhivēṇa kayapuṇṇā
tiyasaṁjaō vi siddhiṁ, kaïlāsagirimmi saṁpattō // PaumaCa.53

aha annayā kayāī, jāō titthaṁkarō ajiyasāmī
dēvēhiṁ tassa sahasā, ahisēyāī kayaṁ sarva // PaumaCa.54

rajaṁ kāūṇa taō, ujjāṇē juvaïparimiō dacha
paṅkayavaṇaṁ milāṇaṁ, vēraggamaṇō vicintēi // PaumaCa.55

jaha ēvaṁ paümasaraṁ, mayaranduddāmakusumariddhilaṁ
hōūṇa puṇō nihaṇaṁ, vaccaï taha māṇusattaṁ pi // PaumaCa.56

āpucchiūṇa ēttō, māyā-pii-putta-pariyaṇaṁ sarva
pubavihāṇēṇa jiṇō, pavajjamuvāgaō dhīrō // PaumaCa.57

dasa ya sahassā taha patthivāṇa mōttūṇa rāyariddhīō
nigganthā pavaïyā, jiṇēṇa samayaṁ mahāsattā // PaumaCa.58

chaṭṭōvavāsaniyamē, sāēyapurammi bambhadattēṇaṁ
dinnaṁ phāsuyadāṇaṁ, vihiṇā bahubhēyasaṁjuttaṁ // PaumaCa.59

aha bārasamē varisē, kēvalanāṇaṁ taō samuppannaṁ
cōttīsaṁ ca aïsayā, aṭṭha mahāpāḍihērā ya // PaumaCa.60


[p. 42]
uppannā ya gaṇaharā, navaī samaṇā navōṇayaṁ lakkhaṁ
saṁjama-sīladharāṇaṁ, guṇariddhivisēsapattāṇaṁ // PaumaCa.61

[sagaracakricaritam —]
tiyasaṁjayassa puttō, bīō cciya vijayasāyarō nāmaṁ
tassa vi ya hōi bhajjā, sumaṅgalā rūvasaṁpannā // PaumaCa.62

tīē gabbhammi suō, jāō sagarō tti nāma vikkhāō
cōddasarayaṇāhivaī, saṁpattō cakkavaṭṭittaṁ // PaumaCa.63

ēyantarammi sēṇiya! jaṁ vattaṁ taṁ suṇēhi ēgamaṇō
atthi ihaṁ vēyaḍḍē, rahanēuracakkavālapuraṁ // PaumaCa.64

vijāharāṇa rāyā, puṇṇaghaṇō nāma tattha vikkhāō
aha mēghavāhaṇō sē, puttō guṇarūvasaṁpannō // PaumaCa.65

uttarasēḍhīe ṭhiyaṁ, nayaraṁ ciya gayaṇavallahaṁ nāma
parivasaï tattha rāyā, sulōyaṇō khēyarāhibaī // PaumaCa.66

tassa ya sahassanayaṇō, puttō dhūyā ya rūvasaṁpannā
taṁ cēva pavarakannaṁ, puṇṇaghaṇō maggaē payaō // PaumaCa.67

bahusō jāijjantī, na ya dinnā tēṇa tassa sā kannā
nēmittiyavayaṇēṇaṁ, sagaranarindassa uddiṭṭhā ॥ // PaumaCa.68

kannānimittahēṭha, puṇṇaghaṇa-sulōyaṇāṇa ābhiṭṭa
jujhaṁ mahantaghōraṁ rahavara-gaya-turaya-pāikkaṁ // PaumaCa.69

jāva ya paharasamiddhaṁ, dōṇha vi jujhaṁ uiṇṇasēṇṇāṇaṁ
tāva ya sahassanayaṇō, ghēttūṇa sahōyarīṁ naṭṭhō // PaumaCa.70

hantūṇa samaramajhē, sulōyaṇaṁ pavisiūṇa nayarammi
kannaṁ apēcchasāṇō, puṇṇaghaṇō āgaō sapuraṁ // PaumaCa.71

tāva ya sahassaṇayaṇō, apahuppantō balēṇa parihīṇō
acchaï araṇṇamajjhē, kālakkhēvaṁ paḍikkhantō // PaumaCa.72

tāva ya āsēṇa hiō, cakkaharō āṇiō tamuddēsaṁ
tassa ciya niyayabhaïṇī, sahassanayaṇēṇa sē dinnā // PaumaCa.73

mahilārayaṇa maṇaharaṁ, daṭṭhūṇa narāhivō suparituṭṭō
vijjāharassa niyayaṁ, dēi samiddhaṁ mahārajaṁ // PaumaCa.74


[p. 43]
aha cakkavālanayaraṁ, sahassanayaṇēṇa vēḍhiyaṁ sabaṁ
niṣphiḍaï savaḍahuttō, puṇṇaghaṇō sāhaṇasamaggō // PaumaCa.75

saṁgāmammi pavattē, bahulōhiyakaddamē paramaghōrē
gāḍhapahāraṣaraddhō, puṇṇaghaṇō pāviō nihaṇaṁ // PaumaCa.76

ghaṇavāhaṇō vi tāhē, vēriyavittāsiō palāyantō
bhayajaṇiyaturiyavēgō, ajiyajiṇindaṁ gaō saraṇaṁ // PaumaCa.77

indēṇa pucchiō sō, kīsa tumaṁ bhayapavēiyasarīrō
tēṇa vi ya tassa siṭuṁ, vēranimittaṁ jahāvattaṁ // PaumaCa.78

aha tassa maggalaggō, sahassanayaṇō ravi va pajjaliō
pēcchaï tamatimiraharaṁ, jiṇassa bhāmaṇḍalaṁ divaṁ // PaumaCa.79

mōttūṇa niyayagavaṁ, thōūṇa jiṇaṁ parāe bhattīē
tatthēva sanniviṭṭhō, naccāsannē samōsaraṇē // PaumaCa.80

dōṇha vi piūṇa cariyaṁ, vijjāharapatthivāṇa puvabhavaṁ
pucchaï gaṇaharavasahō, kēvalanāṇī parikahēi // PaumaCa.81

[puṇyaghanatrilōcanayōḥ pūrvabhavaḥ —]
atthēttha bharahavāsē, āiccaṣabhē purē maṇabhirāmē
caükōḍidhaṇasamiddhō, vāṇiyaō bhāvaṇō nāmaṁ // PaumaCa.82

kittimaï tti surūvā, mahilā puttō ya tassa haridāsō
dhaṇalōbhēṇa ya caliō, pōēṇa ya bhāvaṇō taïyā // PaumaCa.83

niyayaṁ dava-gharasiriṁ, dāūṇa suyassa vivihaüvaēsaṁ
tō niggaō gharāō, suhanakkhattē karaṇajuttē // PaumaCa.84

aha sō jūēṇa jiō, haridāsō cōriyaṁ suraṅgāē
kāūṇa samāḍhattō, rāyagharaṁ patthiō taïyā // PaumaCa.85

jattaṁ kāūṇa taō, saṁpattō bhāyaṇō niyayagēhaṁ
na ya pēcchaï haridāsaṁ, pucchaḍ mahilaṁ payattēṇaṁ // PaumaCa.86

tīē vi tassa siṭṭa, haridāsō cōriyaṁ suraṅgāē
dabassa kāraṇaṭṭhā, rāyaharaṁ patthiō navaraṁ // PaumaCa.87

sō tassa maraṇabhīō, jāva ya santō karēi ēgamaṇō
tāva cciya saṁpattō, haridāsō appaṇō gēhaṁ // PaumaCa.88

paricintiūṇa ēttō, kō vi mahaṁ vēriō samallīṇō
āhaṇaï pāvakammō, khaggapahārēṇa sē sīsaṁ // PaumaCa.89


[p. 44]
mārēūṇa ya piyaraṁ, kāūṇa ya tassa pēyakaraṇijjaṁ
puhaīyalaṁ bhamantō, sō vi hu maraṇaṁ samaṇupattō // PaumaCa.90

jō bhāvaṇō tti nāma, puṇṇaghaṇō sō ihaṁ samuppannō
jō vi hu tassā''si suō, sulōyaṇō sō vi nāyavō // PaumaCa.91

ēvaṁ pubabhavagayaṁ, vēraṁ vijjāharāṇa sōūṇaṁ
mā hōha kalusahiyayā, vēraṁ dūrēṇa vajaha // PaumaCa.92

aha bhaṇaï cakkavaṭṭī, puṇṇaghaṇa-sulōyaṇāṇa jaṁ vattaṁ
cariyaṁ suyaṁ mahāyasa! kahēha ēttō suyāṇaṁ pi // PaumaCa.93

[sahasranayanamēghavāhanayōḥ pūrvabhavaḥ —]
jambuddīvē bharahē, paümapurē rambhakō tti nāmēṇaṁ
tassā''si paramasīsā, sasī ya āvaliyanāmō ya // PaumaCa.94

āvaliṇā gantūṇaṁ, kīyā gōdhēṇu gōulē pavarā
mōla jāva na dijjaï, tāva sasī tattha saṁpattō // PaumaCa.95

sigcha ciya tēṇa kaō, dōṇha vi bhēō susatthakusalēṇaṁ
gōvālaēṇa samayaṁ, kāūṇaṁ kūḍamantaṇayaṁ // PaumaCa.96

gōdhēṇu tēṇa gahiyā, nāyaṁ iyarēṇa jujjhamāvannaṁ
pahaō āvalināmō, maō ya mēcchō samuppannō // PaumaCa.97

sasi mullatthaṁ ca tayā, vikkēūṇaṁ jahāṇusārēṇaṁ
avibhinnamuhacchāō, līlāe samāgaō gēhaṁ // PaumaCa.98

aha annayā kayāī, gacchantō tāmalittinayaraṁ sō
sasiō mēcchēṇa haō, maō ya vasahō samuppannō // PaumaCa.99

tattō vi pāvaguruṇā, vasahō mēcchēṇa māriuṁ khaddhō
uppannō majjārō, mēcchō vi hu mūsaō jāō // PaumaCa.10

annōnnamāraṇaṁ tē, kāūṇaṁ naraya-tiriyajōṇīsu
saṁbhamadēvassa taō, dōṇṇi vi dāsā samuppannā // PaumaCa.101

dāsā sahōyarā tē, jāyā nāmēṇa kūḍa-kāvaḍiyā
jiṇaharaniōgakaraṇē, tē ya niuttā u inbhēṇaṁ // PaumaCa.102

kālaṁ kāūṇa taō, dōṇi vi bhūyāhivā samuppannā
paḍhamō rūvāṇandō, surūvanāmō bhavē bīō // PaumaCa.103


[p. 45]
sasiō cuō samāṇō, kulaṁdharō rāyavali samuppannō
avarō ttha 'pussabhūī, tatthēva purōhiō jāō // PaumaCa.104

mittā hōūṇa taō, pīī chēttūṇa saïriṇīe kaē
aha 'pussabhūi ēttō, icchada ya kulaṁdharaṁ hantuṁ // PaumaCa.105

tarumūlagayassa tahā, dhammaṁ sōūṇa sāhupāsambhi
naravaïparikkhiō sō, uvasantō puṇṇajōēṇa // PaumaCa.106

daṭṭha ṇa pussabhūī, vibhavaṁ dhammassa gahiyavaya-niyamō
kālaṁ kāūṇa taō, saṇaṁkumārē samuppannō // PaumaCa.107

kāūṇa jiṇavaratavaṁ, tatthēva kulaṁdharō vi āyāō
tē dō vi cuyasamāṇā, dhāyaïsaṇḍē samuppannā // PaumaCa.108

nayarē ariṁjayapurē, jayāvaīkucchisaṁbhavā jāyā
kūrā-'maradhaṇunāmā, bhiccā usahassa rāyāṇō // PaumaCa.109

aha naravaīṇa samayaṁ pavajjaṁ gēṇhiūṇa kālagayā
parinibuō narindō, tē sahasārē samuppannā // PaumaCa.110

sasi paḍhamaṁ tattha cuō, jāō cciya mēhavāhaṇō ēsō
āvaliō vi hu ēttō, sahassanayaṇō samuppannō // PaumaCa.111

[sagaracakri-sahasranayanayōḥ sambandhaḥ —]
tō bhaṇaï cakkavaṭṭī, sahassanayaṇē vibhū! 'parikahēhi
pīī mē ahiyayarā, kēṇa nimittēṇa uppannā? // PaumaCa.112

aha sāhiuṁ pavattō, titthayarō pubajammasaṁbandhaṁ
bhikkhādāṇaphalēṇaṁ, dēvattaṁ rambhaō pattō // PaumaCa.113

sōhammāu cavittā, candapurē naravaïssa bhajjāē
varakittināmadhēō, pavajaṁ gēṇhiūṇa maō // PaumaCa.114

dēvō hōūṇa cuō, avaravidēhē taō samuppannō
candamaï-mahāghōsassa nandaṇō rayaṇasaṁcapurē // PaumaCa.115


[p. 46]
ēttō payāvalō sō, ṣavajaṁ gēṇhiūṇa kālagaō
dēvō pāṇayakappē, hōūṇa cuō bharahavāsē // PaumaCa.116

puhaīpurammi jāō, jasaharaputtō jayāe jasakittī
nikkhamiya piusagāsē, vijayavimāṇē samuppannō // PaumaCa.117

tattō cuō samāṇō, jāō sagarō tti cakkavaṭṭi tumaṁ
cōddasarayaṇāhivaī, samattabharahāhivō sūrō // PaumaCa.118

jēṇa'ntarēṇa daïō, āvaliō rambhakassa āsi purā
tēṇa'ntarēṇa tujhaṁ, sahassanayaṇē ahiyanēhō // PaumaCa.119

sōūṇa cariyamēyaṁ, niyayaṁ piusantiyaṁ harisiyacchō
thōūṇa samāḍhattō, sabbhūyaguṇēhi titthayaraṁ // PaumaCa.120

ētthaṁ tu aṇāhāṇaṁ, sattāṇaṁ nāha! kāraṇēṇa viṇā
uvayāraparō si tuma, kiṇṇa mahacchērayaṁ ēyaṁ? // PaumaCa.121

nāha! tuma bambhāṇō, tilōyaṇō saṁkarō sayaṁbuddhō
nārāyaṇō aṇantō, tilōyapujjārihō aruhō // PaumaCa.122

bhaṇiō rakkhasavaïṇā, bhīmēṇaṁ mēhavāhaṇō tāhē
sāhu kayaṁ tē supurisa! jaṁ si jiṇaṁ āgaō saraṇaṁ // PaumaCa.123

tō suṇasu majjha vayaṇaṁ bhaya-sōgaviṇāsaṇaṁ hiyakaraṁ ca
pacchā ya hōi pacchaṁ, kālammi ya nibuī kuṇaï // PaumaCa.124

atthēttha tujjha sattū , vēyaḍḍē khēyarā balasamiddhā
tēhi samaṁ ciya kālaṁ, kaha nēhisi suyaṇa! vīsatthō? // PaumaCa.125

[laṅkāpurī —]
nisuṇēsu sāyaravarē, vidruma-maṇi-rayaṇakiraṇapajjaliē
kāṇaṇavaṇēhi rammō, rakkhasadīvō tti nāmēṇaṁ // PaumaCa.126

sattēva jōyaṇasayā, vitthiṇṇō sabaō samantēṇaṁ
tassa vi ya majjhadēsē, atthi tikūḍō tti varasēlō // PaumaCa.127

nava jōyaṇāṇi tuṅgō, pannāsaṁ sabaō ya vitthiṇṇō
siharaṁ tassa virāyaï, ubbhāsēntaṁ dasa disāō // PaumaCa.128

siharassa tassa hē?, jambūṇayakaṇagacittapāyārā
laṅkāpuri tti nāmaṁ, nayarī surasaṁpayasamiddhā // PaumaCa.129


[p. 47]
bandhavajaṇēṇa samayaṁ, sigghaṁ gantūṇa tattha vīsatthō
bhaya-sōgavippamukkō, abhiṇandantō sayā vasasu // PaumaCa.130

ēvaṁ bhaṇiūṇa tēṇaṁ, rakkhasavaïṇā jalantamaṇikiraṇō
vijjāhi samaṁ dinnō, hārō dēvēhi parigahiō // PaumaCa.131

pāyālaṁkārapura, dharaṇiyalantaragayaṁ ca sē dinnaṁ
chajjōyaṇamavagāḍhaṁ, vitthiṇṇaṁ 'bārasa'ddhaddhaṁ // PaumaCa.132

ēvaṁ rakkhasavaïṇā, bhaṇiō ghaṇavāhaṇō suparituṭṭhō
namiūṇa jiṇavarindaṁ, tēṇa samaṁ patthiō lakaṁ // PaumaCa.133

pēcchaï ya tuṅgatōraṇa-dhavalaṭṭālayavicittapāgāraṁ
ujjāṇa-dīhiyāhi ya, cēiya-bhavaṇēhi aïrammaṁ // PaumaCa.134

bandhavajaṇēṇa sahiō, jayasadugghuṭṭakalayalārāvō
laṅkāpuriṁ paviṭṭhō, jiṇabhavaṇaṁ āgaō rāyā // PaumaCa.135

bhāvēṇa viṇayaṣaṇaō, kāūṇa payāhiṇaṁ tiparivāraṁ
thōūṇa siddhapaḍimā, rāyagihaṁ patthiō tāhē // PaumaCa.136

laṅkāpurīe sāmī, bhīmēṇaṁ mēhavāhaṇō ṭhaviō
vijjāharasusamiddhaṁ, bhuñjaï rajjaṁ surindō va // PaumaCa.137

kinnaragīyapuravarē, bhāṇuvaīgabbhasaṁbhavā kannā
ghaṇavāhaṇassa bhajjā, nāmēṇa ya suppabhā jāyā // PaumaCa.138

amarindarūvasarisō, puttō ghaṇavāhaṇassa uppannō
suppabhadēvītaṇaō, sō ya mahārakkhasō nāmaṁ // PaumaCa.139

ēvaṁ gayavaï kālē, bhattīrāēṇa cōiō santō
ghaṇavāhaṇō vi ajiyaṁ, vandaṇahēuṁ samaṇupattō // PaumaCa.140

sīhāsaṇōvaviṭṭhō, diṭṭhō titthaṁkarō vimaladēhō
najjaï sa(sā)rayasamaē, nahassa majjhaṭṭhiō sūrō // PaumaCa.141

thōūṇa jiṇavarindaṁ, sabbhūyaguṇēhi maṅgalasaēhiṁ
tatthēva ya viṇiviṭṭhō, sura-naraparisāe majjhammi // PaumaCa.142

nāūṇa kahantarayaṁ, sagarō titthaṁkaraṁ paṇamiūṇaṁ
pucchaï jiṇavarasaṁkhā, samatīyā-'ṇāgayāṇaṁ ca // PaumaCa.143

kaï vā samaïkkantā, hōhinti ya kēttiyā mahāpurisā
tinthayara-cakkavaṭṭī, baladēvā vāsudēvā ya? // PaumaCa.144


[p. 48]
[tīrthaṅkarāḥ —]
bhaṇaï jiṇō vaïkantō, usabhō nāmēṇa paḍhamatitthayarō1
jēṇēttha bharahavāsē, lōgassa nidēsiō dhammō // PaumaCa.145

sō ṭhaviya suyaṁ rajjē pavajaṁ gēṇhiūṇa kālagaō
bīō ya vaṭṭamāṇō, ajiō haṁ tēṇa paḍitullō2 // PaumaCa.146

taha saṁbhavā3 'bhiṇandaṇa4 sumaī5 paümappahō6 supāsō7 ya
sasi8 pupphadanta9 sīyala10 vāsupujjō ya12 ॥ 147॥ // PaumaCa.147

vimala13maṇantaï 14 dhammō 15 santī16 kunthū17 arō18 ya mallī ya19
muṇisubaya20 nami21 nēmi22 pāsō23 vīrō24 ya titthayarō // PaumaCa.148

ēē bāvīsa jiṇā, hōhinti kamēṇa 'ṇāgaē kālē
tāṇaṁ tu cakkavaṭṭī, santī kunthū arō cēva // PaumaCa.149

uttamakulasaṁbhūyā, sabē khīrōyavāriahisittā
sabaï vi mōkkhagāmī, kēvalanāṇī bhavē savē // PaumaCa.150

ēē caüvīsa jiṇā, nāmēhi jaguttamā samakkhāyā
nisuṇēhi cakkavaṭṭī, jahakkama kittaïssāmi // PaumaCa.151

[cakriṇaḥ —]
bharahō ya cakkavaṭṭī1 samaīō saṁpayaṁ tuma sagarō2
avasēsā cakkaharā, hōhinti aṇāgaē kālē // PaumaCa.152

maghavaṁ3 saṇaṁkumārō4, santī5 kunthū6 arō7 subhūmō8 ya
paüma9 harisēṇanāmō10, jayasēṇō11 bambhadattō ya12 // PaumaCa.153

ayalō1 vijaōra bhaddō3, suppabha4 sudaṁsaṇō ya nāyabō5
āṇandō6 nandaṇō7 paümō 8 navamō rāmō ya9 baladēvō // PaumaCa.154

hōhī tiviṭṭha 1 duviṭhṭha2, sayaṁbhu3 purisōttamō4 purisasīhō5
purisavarapuṇḍarīō6. dattō7 nārāyaṇō 8 kaṇhō9 // PaumaCa.155

paḍhamō āsaggīvō1, tāragara mēraga3 nisumbha4 mahukēḍhō5
bali6 palhāō7 rāvaṇa 8 taha ya jarāsindhu9 paḍisattū // PaumaCa.156

ēē mahāṇubhāvā, purisā avasappiṇīe kālammi
ēttiyamēttā ya puṇō, havanti ūsappiṇīē vi // PaumaCa.157


[p. 49]
ēkaṁ jiṇavarasiṭuṁ, dhammaṁ kāūṇa paṁvarabhattīē
ēvaṁvihā maṇussā, hōūṇa sivaṁ paramuvēnti // PaumaCa.158

jē puṇa dhammavirahiyā, jīvā bahupāvakammapaḍibaddhā
tē caügaïvitthiṇṇē, bhamanti saṁsārakantārē // PaumaCa.159

ēvaṁ kālasabhāvaṁ, suṇiūṇaṁ mahaïpurisasaṁbandhaṁ
ghaṇavāhaṇō virāgaṁ, takkhaṇamēttēṇa saṁpattō // PaumaCa.160

pañcindiyavisayavimōhiēṇa kantāṣasattacittēṇaṁ
dhammō cciya nāhikaō, hā! kaṭuṁ vañciō appā // PaumaCa.161

indadhaṇusumiṇasarisē, vijjulayācavalacañcalē jīē
kō nāma karēja raī, jō hōja sacēyaṇō purisō? // PaumaCa.162

tā ujjhiūṇa raja, kantā puttā dhaṇaṁ ca dhaṇaṁ ca
gēṇhāmi paramabandhu', pārattabiijjayaṁ dhammaṁ // PaumaCa.163

ahisiñciūṇa rajjē, sō hu mahārakkhasaṁ paḍhamaputtaṁ
ummukkasavasaṅgō, pavajjamuvāgaō dhīrō // PaumaCa.164

laṅkāpurīe sāmī, ghaṇavāhaṇanandaṇō pahiyakittī
vijāharāṇa rāyā, bhuñjaï rajaṁ suravarō va // PaumaCa.165

bhajjā sē vimalābhā, tīē puttā kamēṇa uppannā
paḍhamō ya dēvarakkhō, uahī āiccarakkhō ya // PaumaCa.166

ajiyajiṇindō ya taō, dhammapahaṁ darisiūṇa lōyassa
sammēyasēlasiharē, sivamayalamaṇuttaraṁ pattō // PaumaCa.167

[sagaraputrāṇāmaṣṭāpadayātrā nāgēndraṇa dahanaṁ ca —]
sagarō vi cakkavaṭṭī, caüsaṭṭhisahassajuvaïkayavihavō
bhuñjaï ēgacchattaṁ, sayalasamatthaṁ imaṁ bharahaṁ // PaumaCa.168

amarindarūvasarisā, saṭṭhisahassā suyāṇa uppannā
aṭṭhāvayammi sēlē, vandaṇahēuṁ samaṇupattā // PaumaCa.169

vandaṇavihāṇapūyaṁ, kamēṇa kāūṇa siddhapaḍimāṇaṁ
aha tē kumārasīhā, cēiyabhavaṇē pasaṁsanti // PaumaCa.170


[p. 50]
mantīhi tāṇa siṭuṁ, ēyāī kāriyāim̐ bharahēṇaṁ
tumhēttha rakkhaṇatthaṁ, kiṁci uvāyaṁ lahuṁ kuṇaha // PaumaCa.171

daṇḍarayaṇēṇa ghāyaṁ, dāuṁ gaṅgānaīe majjhammi
sayarasuēṇa u tāhē, parikhēvō pavayassa kaō // PaumaCa.172

daṭṭhūṇa ya taṁ vivaraṁ, nāgindō kōhajalaṇapajjaliō
sabē vi sayaraputtē, takkhaṇamēttaṁ ḍahaï ruṭṭō // PaumaCa.173

na ya daḍḍhē 'dōṇṇi naṇē, tāṇaṁ majjhaṭṭhiē kumārāṇaṁ
kāūṇaṁ aṇukampaṁ, jiṇavaradhammappabhāvēṇaṁ // PaumaCa.174

datr̥̄ṇa maraṇamēyaṁ, sayarasuyāṇaṁ samattakhandhārō
bhaïrahi-bhīmēṇa samaṁ, sāēyapuriṁ samaṇupattō // PaumaCa.175

sayarassa nivēyantā, suyamaraṇaṁ bhīma-bhagirahī sahasā
nayasatthapaṇḍiēhiṁ, nivāriyā tē amaccēhiṁ // PaumaCa.176

tē tattha pavaramantī, gantūṇa ya ṣaṇamiūṇa cakkaharaṁ
dinnāsaṇōvaviṭṭhā, kayasannā jaṁpiu payattā // PaumaCa.177

iha pēccha naravaï! tumaṁ, lōyassa aṇiccayā asārattaṁ
kō ēttha kuṇaï sōyaṁ, jō purisō paṇḍiō lōē? // PaumaCa.178

āsi purā cakkaharō, bharahō nāmēṇa tujjha samavibhavō
chakkhaṇḍā jēṇa imā, dāsi va vasīkayā puhaī // PaumaCa.179

tassā''si paḍhamaputtō, āiccajasō tti nāma vikkhāō
jassa ya nāmapasiddhō, vaṁsō iha vaṭṭaē lōē // PaumaCa.180

ēttha naravaī, vaṁsē bala-riddhi-kittisaṁpannē
kāūṇa mahārajjaṁ, vōlīṇā dīhakālēṇaṁ // PaumaCa.181

acchantu tāva maṇuyā, jē vi ya tē suravaī mahiḍḍīyā
vibhavēṇa pajjalēuṁ, vijjhāṇā huyavahaṁ cēva // PaumaCa.182

jē vi ya jiṇavaravasahā, samatthatēlōkkanamiyapayavīḍhā
āurakkhayammi pattē, tē vi ya muñcanti sasarīraṁ // PaumaCa.183

jaha ēkkammi taruvarē, vasiūṇaṁ pakkhiṇō pabhāyammi
vacanti dasa disāō, ēkkuḍambammi taha jīvā // PaumaCa.184

indadhaṇuphēṇasuviṇaya-vijulayākusumabubbuyasaricchā
iṭhṭhajaṇasaṁpaōgā, vibhavā dēhā ya jīvāṇaṁ // PaumaCa.185

sōsanti jē vi udahi, mēruṁ bhañjanti muṭṭhiṣaharēhiṁ
kālēṇa tē vi purisā, kayantavayaṇaṁ ciya paviṭṭhā // PaumaCa.186


[p. 51]
baliyāṇa jīvalōē, sabāṇa vi hōi aïbalō maccū
nihaṇaṁ jēṇa aṇantā, cakkaharāī ihaṁ nīyā // PaumaCa.187

ēvaṁ maccuvasagaē, sasurā-'sura-māṇusammi lōyammi
ummukkakammakalusā, navaraṁ ciya sutthiyā siddhā // PaumaCa.188

uttamakulubbhavāṇaṁ, ēyāṇaṁ guṇasahassanilayāṇaṁ
cariē sumarijjantē, kaha cēva na phuṭṭaē hiyayaṁ? // PaumaCa.189

jaha tē kālēṇa nivā, iha maṇuyabhavē khayaṁ samaṇupattā
taha amhē vi ya sabē, vaccīhāmō niruttēṇaṁ // PaumaCa.19

annaṁ pi suṇasu sāmiya! dīṇamuhā bhīma-bhagirahī dō vi
ētthā''gayāṇa pēcchasi, nūṇaṁ sēsā khayaṁ pattā // PaumaCa.191

tē pēcchiūṇa rāyā, taṁ ciya sōūṇa niyayasuyamaraṇaṁ
ghaṇasōyasalliyaṅgō, mucchāvasavēmbhalō paḍiō // PaumaCa.192

candaṇajalōlliyaṅgō, paḍibuddhō puttamaraṇadukkhattō
aha vilaviuṁ payattō, nayaṇēsu ya mukkasalilōhō // PaumaCa.193

hā! sukumālasarīrā, puttā maha surakumārasamarūvā
kēṇa vihayā ayaṇḍē, avirāhiyaduṭṭhavērīṇa? // PaumaCa.194

hā! guṇasahassanilayā, hā! uttamarūva sōmasasivayaṇā
hā! nigghiṇēṇa vihiṇā, vahiyā mē niraṇukampēṇaṁ // PaumaCa.195

kiṁ tujjha natthi puttā, pāvavihī! bālayā hiyayaïṭṭhā
jēṇa maha mārasi ihaṁ, suyāṇa saḍhi sahassāiṁ // PaumaCa.196

ēyāṇi ya annāṇi ya, cakkaharō vilaviūṇa bahuyāī
paḍibuddhō bhaṇaï taō, vayaṇāī jāyasaṁvēgō // PaumaCa.197

hā! kaṭuṁ visayavimōhiēṇa suyaṇēharajjubaddhēṇaṁ
dhammō maē na ciṇṇō, taruṇattē mandabhaggēṇaṁ // PaumaCa.198

kiṁ majjha vasumaīē?, navahi nihīhi va rayaṇasahiēhiṁ!
jaṁ dullahaladdhāṇaṁ, puttāṇa muhaṁ na pēcchāmi // PaumaCa.199

dhannā tē sappurisā, bharahāī jē mahiṁ payahiūṇaṁ
niviṇṇakāmabhōgā, nissaṅgā cēva pavaïyā // PaumaCa.20

aha sō jaṇhaviputtaṁ, ahisiñcēūṇa bhagirahiṁ rajē
bhīmarahēṇa samāṇaṁ, pavaïō jiṇavarasayāsē // PaumaCa.201


[p. 52]
kāūṇa tavamuyāraṁ, uppāḍiya kēvalaṁ saha suēṇaṁ
āukkhaē mahappā, sagarō siddhiṁ samaṇupattō // PaumaCa.202

aha bhagirahī vi rajjaṁ, kuṇaï mahābhaḍasamūhaparikiṇṇō
sāēyapuravarīē, indō jaha dēvanayarīē // PaumaCa.203

[bhagīrathapūrvabhavaḥ —]
aha bhagirahī kayāī, gantūṇa ya paṇamiūṇa muṇivasahaṁ
tatthēva sanniviṭṭhō, naccāsannē suṇiya dhammaṁ // PaumaCa.204

suyasāgaramaṇagāraṁ, pucchaï taṁ bhagirahī kumāravarō
kēṇēva kāraṇēṇaṁ, tāṇaṁ majhē duvē na mayā? // PaumaCa.205

aha bhaṇaï muṇivarō sō, gacchō sammēyapavayaṁ caliō
saṇiyaṁ viharantō cciya, saṁpattō antimaṁ gāmaṁ // PaumaCa.206

dahṇa samaṇasaṅgha, gāmajaṇō tassa kuṇaï uvasaggaṁ
kumbhārēṇa nisiddhō, nindantō pharusavayaṇēhiṁ // PaumaCa.207

cōrattaṁ paḍivannō, tatthēgō gāmavāsiō purisō
tassa'varāhanimittaṁ, gāmō daḍḍō narindēṇaṁ // PaumaCa.208

kumbhārō vi ya annaṁ, gāmaṁ āmantiō gaō taïyā
sō tattha navari ēkkō, na ya daḍḍō kammajōēṇaṁ // PaumaCa.209

mariūṇa kumbhayārō, vaṇiō jāō mahādhaṇasamiddhō
vārāḍayammi ēttō, gāmō jāō samaṁ tēṇaṁ // PaumaCa.210

tattō vi kariya kālaṁ, vaṇiō sō naravaī samuppannō
gāmā vi māivāhā, jāyā hatthīṇa parimaliyā // PaumaCa.211

jāō naravaï samaṇō, dēvō hōūṇa varavimāṇammi
tattō cuō samāṇō, bhagirahirāyā tuma jāō // PaumaCa.212

jō vi hu sō gāmajaṇō, kālaṁ kāūṇa vivihajāīsu
kammāṇubhāvajaṇiyā, sagarassa suyā samuppannā // PaumaCa.213

saṅghassa nindaṇaṁ kuṇaï jō narō rāga-dōsapaḍibaddhō
sō bhavasahassaghōrē, puṇaruttaṁ bhamaï saṁsārē // PaumaCa.214

suṇiūṇa niyayacariyaṁ, bhavapariyaṭṭaṁ ca sayaraputtāṇaṁ
samaṇō hōūṇa ciraṁ, bhagīrahī siddhimaṇupattō // PaumaCa.215

ēyaṁ tē parikahiyaṁ, cariyaṁ sayarassa patthavuppannaṁ
ēttō magahanarāhiva!, jaṁ patthuya taṁ ca vō suṇasu // PaumaCa.216


[p. 53]
[mahārākṣasasya vaïrāgyaṁ pūrvabhavaśva —]
jō tattha sō mahappā, laṅkāpurisāmiō mahārakkhō
nikkaṇṭayamaṇukūlaṁ, bhuñjaï rajaṁ mahābhōgaṁ // PaumaCa.217

sō annayā kayāī, juvaījaṇaparimiō varujjāṇē
ramiūṇa vāvisalilē, pēcchaï bhamaraṁ paümamajjhē // PaumaCa.218

jaha paümagandhaluddhō, naṭṭhō cciya mahuyarō avinnāṇō
taha juvaïvayaṇakamalē, āsattō cēva naṭṭhō haṁ // PaumaCa.219

suibuddhiṇā vihūṇā, niyamēṇaṁ mahuyarā viṇassanti
kusalō vi jaṁ viṇaṭṭhō, ahayaṁ taṁ mōhadullaliyaṁ // PaumaCa.220

gandhēṇa rasēṇa imō, jaï ēvaṁ mahuyarō khayaṁ pattō
paḍhamaṁ cēva viṇaṭṭhō, pañcindiyavasagaō jō haṁ // PaumaCa.221

bhōttūṇa visayasōkkhaṁ, purisō dhammēṇa virahiō santō
paribhamaï cāurantaṁ, puṇaruttaṁ dīhasaṁsāraṁ // PaumaCa.222

jāva ya virattabhāvō, acchaï laṅkāhivō parigaṇantō
tāva ya saṅghaparivuḍō, pattō suyasāyarō samaṇō // PaumaCa.223

tasa-pāṇa-janturahiē, ujjāṇē phāsuē silāvaṭṭē
tatthēva sanniviṭṭhō, samaṇēhi samaṁ kayaniōgō // PaumaCa.224

ujjāṇapālaēhi, siṭṭē samaṇāgamē taō rāyā
gantūṇa payayamaṇasō, paṇamaï suyasāyaraṁ sāhuṁ // PaumaCa.225

sēsaṁ ca samaṇasaṅgha, jahakkamaṁ paṇamiūṇa uvaviṭhṭhō
pucchaï bhavapariyaṭṭē, niyayaṁ rāyā muṇivarindaṁ // PaumaCa.226

aha sāhiuṁ payattō, samaṇō chaübhatthanāṇavisaēṇaṁ
bharahēttha pōyaṇapurē, vasaï narō hiyakarō nāmaṁ // PaumaCa.227

bhajjā ya māhavī sē, puttō pōiṁkarō tuma tēsiṁ
jiṇavaradhammuppannō, hēmarahō naravaī tattha // PaumaCa.228

sō annayā kayāī, cēiyapūrya raïttu bhāvēṇaṁ
paḍupaḍaha-saṅkhasahiyaṁ, jayasadaṁ jiṇavarē kuṇaï // PaumaCa.229


[p. 54]
uṭṭhiyamēttō si tuma, sadaṁ sōūṇa haṭṭatuṭṭhamaṇō
aha ghōsiuṁ payattō, jiṇassa thuimaṅgalavihāṇaṁ // PaumaCa.230

kālaṁ kāūṇa taō, jakkhō jāō mahiḍḍisaṁpannō
avaravidēhē pēcchaï, kañcaṇanayarē muṇivarassa // PaumaCa.231

uvasaggaṁ kīrantaṁ, vārēūṇa ya riū sasattīē
rakkhaï muṇivaradēhaṁ, jakkhō puṇṇaṁ samajjēi // PaumaCa.232

tattō cuō samāṇō, taḍiyaṅgayakhēyarassa vēyaḍḍhē
siriṣabhadēvītaṇaō, jāō uiō varakumārō // PaumaCa.233

tō vandaṇāe jantaṁ, aha cāraṇavikkama palōēuṁ
vijjāharāhirāyā, kuṇaï niyāṇaṁ taō mūḍhō // PaumaCa.234

kāūṇa tavamuyāraṁ, īsāṇē suravarō ttha hōūṇaṁ
ghaṇavāhaṇassa puttō, jāō si tumaṁ mahārakkhō // PaumaCa.235

surabhōgēsu na tittī, jō si tumaṁ na ya gaō sucirakālaṁ
kaha parituṭṭhō hōhisi, diyahāṇaṁ sōlasaddhēṇaṁ? // PaumaCa.236

sōūṇa vayaṇamēyaṁ, gaō visāyaṁ taō mahārakkhō
āsannamaraṇabhāvō, bhaṇaï narindō imaṁ vayaṇaṁ // PaumaCa.237

visayavisamōhiēṇaṁ, mahilānēhāṇurāgarattēṇaṁ
kālō cciya na ya nāō, kēttiyamēttō vi vōlīṇō // PaumaCa.238

na ya gēhammi palittē, kūvō khammaï sutūramāṇēhiṁ
dhāhāviē ṇa dammaï, āsō cciya takkhaṇaṁ cēva // PaumaCa.239

abhisiñciūṇa rajjē, puttaṁ ciya dēvarakkhasaṁ rāyā
taha bhāṇurakkhasaṁ pi ya, juvarajjē ṭhaviya nikkhantō // PaumaCa.240

vōsiriyasabasaṅgō, caïūṇaṁ caüvihaṁ ca āhāraṁ
ārāhaṇāe kālaṁ, kāūṇa suruttamō jāō // PaumaCa.241

aha kinnaragīyapurē, siridharavijjāharassa varaduhiyā
raïvēganāmadhēyā, sā mahilā dēvarakkhassa // PaumaCa.242

gandhavagīyanayarē, surasannibharāyanāmadhēyassa
jāyā gandhārisuyā, gandhavā bhāṇurakkhassa // PaumaCa.243

dasa dēvarakkhasasuyā, jāyā cha ccēva varakumārīō
taha bhāṇurakkhasassa vi, tāvaïyā cēva uppannā // PaumaCa.244


[p. 55]
amarapurasannibhāī, sanāmasarisāim̐ paṭṭaṇavarāī
rakkhasasuēhi sigdhaṁ, kayāim̐ bahusannivēsāī // PaumaCa.245

saṁjhāyāla1suvēlō2, maṇapalhāō3 maṇōharō4 cēva
haṁsaddīvō5 harijō6, dhannō7 kaṇaō8 samuddō ya9 // PaumaCa.246

nāmēṇa addhasaggō10, ēva nivēsā mahāguṇasamiddhā
uppāiyā samatthā, mahaïmahārakkhasasuēhiṁ // PaumaCa.247

āvattaviyaḍamēhā, ukkaḍaphuḍaduggahā mahābhāgā
tavaṇāyavaliyarayaṇā, kayā ya ravirakkhasasuēhiṁ // PaumaCa.248

varabhavaṇa-tuṅgatōraṇa-nāṇāvihamaṇimaūhapajjaliyā
sōhanti sannivēsā, rakkhasaputtāṇa kīlaṇayā // PaumaCa.249

rāyā u dēvarakkhō, bīō puṇa bhāṇurakkhasanarindō
ghēttūṇa pavaradikkhaṁ, abābāhaṁ samaṇupattō // PaumaCa.250

[rākṣasavaṁśaḥ —]
ēvaṁ tu mahāvaṁsē, vōlīṇē mēhavāhaṇō jāō
rakkhasasuō mahappā, maṇavēgāē samuppannō // PaumaCa.251

tassa ya nāmēṇa imō, rakkhasavaṁsō jayammi vikkhāō
tassa vi āiccagaī, mahantakittī ya uppannō // PaumaCa.252

supṣabhadēvītaṇayā, ravi-candasamappabhā kumāravarā
samaṇō hōūṇa ciraṁ, piyā ya tēsiṁ gaō saggaṁ // PaumaCa.253

nāmēṇa mayaṇapaümā, āiccagaïssa vallabhā bhajjā
āuṇahanāmadhēyā, mahilā u mahantakittissa // PaumaCa.254

āiccagaïssa suō, bhīmarahō nāma naravaī jāō
tassā''si mahiliyāṇaṁ, sahassamēgaṁ varavahūṇaṁ // PaumaCa.255

aṭṭhattaraṁ sayaṁ ciya, puttāṇaṁ amararūvasarisāṇaṁ
ghēttūṇa ya pabajaṁ, bhīmarahō patthiō siddhiṁ // PaumaCa.256

rakkhanti rakkhasā khalu, dīvā puṇṇēṇa rakkhiyā jēṇa
tēṇaṁ ciya khayarāṇaṁ, rakkhasanāmaṁ kayaṁ lōē // PaumaCa.257


[p. 56]
ēsō tē parikahiō, rakkhasaksassa ubbhavō tujjha
sēṇiya! suṇāhi ēttō, vaṁsē purisā samāsēṇa // PaumaCa.258

bhīmappahassa puttō, paḍhamō pūyārahō samuppannō
pabaïō khāyajasō, rajē ṭhaviūṇa jiyabhāṇuṁ // PaumaCa.259

jiyabhāṇussa vi puttō, saṁparikittī visālavacchayalō
suggīvō tassa suō, tassa vi ya bhavē hariggīvō // PaumaCa.260

siriṁgīvō sumuhō vi ya, suvantō amiyavēganāmō ya
āiccagaïkumārō, indappabha indamēhō ya // PaumaCa.261

jāō mayāridamaṇō, pahiō indaï subhāṇudhammō ya
ēttō surāri tijaḍō, mahaṇō aṅgāraō ya ravī // PaumaCa.262

cakkāra vajjamajhō, pamōya varasīhavāhaṇō sūrō
cāuṇḍarāvaṇō vi ya, bhīmō bhayavāha riumahaṇō // PaumaCa.263

nibāṇabhattimantō uggasirī aruhabhattimantō ya
taha ya pavaṇuttaragaī, uttama aṇilō ya caṇḍō ya // PaumaCa.264

laṅkāsōga maūhō, mahabāhu maṇōramō ya ravitēō
mahagaï mahakantajasō, arisaṁtāsō ya rāyāṇō // PaumaCa.265

candavayaṇō ya maharavō, mēhajjhāṇō tahēva gahakhōbhō
nakkhattadamaṇamāī, ēvaṁ vijjāharā nēyā // PaumaCa.266

kōḍīṇa sayasahassā, ēvaṁ vijāharā balasamiddhā
laṅkāpurīe sāmī, bōlīṇā dīhakālēṇaṁ // PaumaCa.267

puttāṇa niyayarajjaṁ, dāūṇa paraṁparāe nikkhantā
dēvattaṁ sivasōkkhaṁ, kēi sasattīe saṁpattā // PaumaCa.268

ēvaṁ gaēsu niyamā, mahayāpurisēsu paümagabbhāē
mēhappabhassa puttō, kittīdhavalō samuppannō // PaumaCa.269

vijjāharēhi samayaṁ, āṇāissariyavivihaguṇapuṇṇō
laṅkāpurīe rajjaṁ, kuṇaï jahicchaṁ surindō va // PaumaCa.270

ēvaṁ bhavantarakaēṇa tavōbalēṇaṁ, pāvanti dēva-maṇuēsu mahantasōkkhaṁ
kēēttha daḍḍanīsēsakasāya-mōhā, siddhā bhavanti vimalā-'malapaṅkamukkā // PaumaCa.271


iti paümacariē rakkhasavaṁsāhiyārē pañcamuddēsaō samattō
