[dasarahapañcajjā-rāmaniggamaṇa-bharaharajjavihāṇaṁ]

aha tattha jiṇāyayaṇē, nidaṁ gamiūṇa aḍḍarattammi
lōgē suttapasuttē, nīsaṁcārē vigayasaddē // PaumaCa.1

ghēttu dhaṇuvararayaṇaṁ, sīyāsahiyā jiṇaṁ namaṁsittā
saṇiyaṁ viṇiggayā tē, dō cēva jaṇaṁ palōyantā // PaumaCa.2

kō vēttha surayakhīṇō, gāḍhaṁ uvagūhiuṁ suvaï kantaṁ
puvaṁ kayāvarāhō, annō mahilaṁ pasāēi // PaumaCa.3

paragēhaṁ, gantūṇaṁ kucciēsu aṅgēsu
uvāsaï majjāra, jālagavakkhantarē dhuttō // PaumaCa.4

annō sunnāyayaṇē, saṁkēyayadinnakannasabbhāvō
ahiyaṁ ākuliyamaṇō, kuṇaï niviṭuṭṭhiyaṁ purisō // PaumaCa.5

ēyaṁ ciya suṇamāṇā, pēcchantā jaṇavayassa viṇiōgaṁ
aha niggayā purīō, saṇiyaṁ tē gūḍhadārēṇaṁ // PaumaCa.6

avaradisaṁ vaccantā, diṭṭhā suhaḍēhi maggamāṇēhiṁ
gantūṇa paṇamiyā tē, bhāvēṇa sasēnnasahiēhiṁ // PaumaCa.7

sīhā sahāvamantharagaīe, saṇiyaṁ tu tattha naravasahā
gāūyamēttaṭhāṇaṁ, vaccanti suhaṁ balasamaggā // PaumaCa.8

gāmēsu paṭṭaṇēsu ya, pūijjantā jaṇēṇa bahuēṇaṁ
pēcchanti vaccamāṇā, khēḍa-maḍambā-''garaṁ vasuhaṁ // PaumaCa.9


[p. 256]
aha tē kamēṇa pattā, hari-gaya-ruru-camara-sarahasaddālaṁ
ghaṇapāyavasaṁchannaṁ, aḍaviṁ ciya pāriyattassa // PaumaCa.10

pēcchanti tattha bhīmā, bahugāhasamāulā jalasamiddhā
gambhīrā nāma nadī, kallōlucchaliyasaṁghāyā // PaumaCa.11

tō rāghavēṇa bhaṇiyā, suhaḍā sabaï vi sāhaṇasamaggā
tumhē niyattiyavaṁ, ēyaṁ raṇaṁ mahābhīmaṁ // PaumaCa.12

tāēṇa bharahasāmī, ṭhaviō rajjammi sayalapuhaīē
gacchāmi dāhiṇapahaṁ, avassa tubbhē niyattēha // PaumaCa.13

aha tē bhaṇanti suhaḍā, sāmi! tamē virahiyāṇa kiṁ amhaṁ
rajjēṇa sāhaṇēṇa ya, vivihēṇa ya dēhasōkkhēṇaṁ? // PaumaCa.14

sīha-'cchabhalla-cittaya-ghaṇapāyava-girivarāulē raṇē
samayaṁ tumē vasāmō, kuṇasu dayaṁ asaraṇāṇa'mhaṁ // PaumaCa.15

āucchiūṇa suhaḍē, sīyaṁ bhuyāvagr̥hiyaṁ kāuṁ
rāmō uttaraï naïṁ, gambhīraṁ lakkhaṇasamaggō // PaumaCa.16

rāmaṁ salakkhaṇaṁ tē, paratīrāvaṭṭhiyaṁ palōēuṁ
hāhāravaṁ karēntā, sabaï vi bhaḍā paḍiniyattā // PaumaCa.17

tēhi niyattēhi tahiṁ, di8 ciya jiṇaharaṁ mahātuṅgaṁ
samaṇēhi saṁparivuḍaṁ, tattha paviṭṭhā suhaḍasīhā // PaumaCa.18

kāūṇa namōkkāraṁ, jiṇapaḍimāṇaṁ visuddhabhāvēṇaṁ
paṇamanti muṇivarindē, aṇuparivāḍīe tivihēṇaṁ // PaumaCa.19

pucchanti sāhavaṁ tē, bhayavaṁ! saṁsārasāyaraṁ bhīmaṁ
uttārēhi mahājasa! amhē jiṇadhammapōēṇaṁ // PaumaCa.20

tō sāhavēṇa dhammō, kahiō saṁkhēvaō jiṇuṭṭhiō
jaha takkhaṇēṇa jāyā, saṁvēgaparāyaṇā bahavē // PaumaCa.21

niddaḍḍō vijaō vi ya, mēhakumārō tahēva raṇalōlō
nāgadamaṇō ya bīrō, saḍhō ya sattūdamadharō ya // PaumaCa.22

taha kakaḍō viṇōō, sabō piyavaddhaṇō kaḍhōrō ya
ēvaṁvihā narindā, nigganthasirī samaṇupattā // PaumaCa.23

annē puṇa gihadhamma, ghēttūṇa narāhivā visayahuttā
pattā sāēyapurī, bharahassa phuḍaṁ nivēēnti // PaumaCa.24

sīyā-lakkhaṇasahiō, na niyattō rāghavō gaō raṇṇaṁ
sōūṇa vayaṇamēyaṁ, bharahō aïdukkhiō jāō // PaumaCa.25


[p. 257]
tō dasarahō vi rāyā, puttaviōē aīvasaṁviggō
ṭhāvēi takkhaṇaṁ ciya, visaē rajjāhivaṁ bharahaṁ // PaumaCa.26

saṁvēgajaṇiyakaraṇō, bhaḍāṇa bāvattarīe samasahiō
dikkhaṁ gaō narindō, pāsē cciya bhūyasaraṇassa // PaumaCa.27

[daśarathapravrajyā —]
tattha vi ēgavihārī, aṇaraṇṇasuō tavaṁ pakuvantō
maṇasā dūmiyahiyaō, puttasiṇēhaṁ samubahaï // PaumaCa.28

aha annayō kayāī, dhīrō āruhiya suhayaraṁ jhāṇaṁ
cintēi tō maṇēṇaṁ, nēhō cciya bandhaṇaṁ gāḍhaṁ // PaumaCa.29

dhaṇa-sayaṇa-putta-dārā, jē annabhavēsu āsi ṇēgavihā
tē kattha gayā'ṇāīsaṁsārē paribhamantassa // PaumaCa.30

paribhuttaṁ visayasuhaṁ, suralōē varabimāṇavasahīsu
narayāṇaladāhā ciya, saṁpattā bhōgahēummi // PaumaCa.31

annōnnabhakkhaṇaṁ puṇa, tirikkhajōṇīsu samaṇubhūyaṁ mē
puḍhavi-jala-jalaṇa-māruya bhamiō ya vaṇassaīsu ciraṁ // PaumaCa.32

maṇuyattaṇē vi bhōgā, bhuttā saṁjōya-vippaōgā ya
bahurōga-sōgamāī, bandhavanēhāṇurattēṇaṁ // PaumaCa.33

tamhā puttasiṇēhaṁ, ēyaṁ chaḍḍēmi dōsaāmūlaṁ
muṇivaradiṭēṇa puṇō, jhāṇēṇa maṇaṁ visōhēmi // PaumaCa.34

vivihaṁ tavaṁ karēntō, ahiyāsēntō parīsahē savē
dasarahamuṇī mahappā, viharaï ēgantadēsēsu // PaumaCa.35

puttēsu para viēsa, gaēsu avarāiyā ya sōmittī
bhattārē pavaïē, sōyasamuddammi paḍiyāō // PaumaCa.36

suyasōgadukkhiyāō, tāō daṭṭhaṇa kēgaī dēvī
tō bhaṇaï niyayaputtaṁ, vayaṇamiṇaṁ mē nisāmēhi // PaumaCa.37

nikkaṇṭayamaṇukūlaṁ, putta! tumē pāviyaṁ mahārajaṁ
paümēṇa lakkhaṇēṇa ya, rahiyaṁ na ya sōhaē ēyaṁ // PaumaCa.38

tāṇaṁ ciya jaṇaṇīō, puttaviōgammi jāyadukkhāō
kāhinti mā hu kālaṁ, āṇēhi lahuṁ varakumārē // PaumaCa.39

jaṇaṇīe vayaṇamēyaṁ, suṇiūṇa turaṁgamaṁ samārūḍhō
tūrantō cciya bharahō, tāṇaṁ aṇumaggaō laggō // PaumaCa.40

iya diṭṭhā vi ya samayaṁ, mahilāē tē kumāravarasīhā
pucchantō pahiyajaṇaṁ, baccaï bharahō pavaṇavēgō // PaumaCa.41


[p. 258]
aha tē naīe tīrē, vīsamamāṇā mahāvaṇē bhīmē
sīyāe samaṁ pēcchaï, bharahō pāsatthavaradhaṇuyā // PaumaCa.42

bahuyadivasēsu dēsō, jō vōlīṇō kumārasīhēhiṁ
sō bharahēṇa pavannō, diyahēhiṁ chahi ayattēṇaṁ // PaumaCa.43

sō cakkhugōyarāō, turayaṁ mōttaṇa kēgaīputtō
calaṇēsu paümaṇāhaṁ, paṇamiya mucchaṁ samaṇupattō // PaumaCa.44

paḍibōhiō ya bharahō, rāmēṇāliṅgiō siṇēhēṇaṁ
sīyāe lakkhaṇēṇa ya, bāḍhaṁ saṁbhāsiō vihiṇā // PaumaCa.45

bharahō namiyasarīrō, kāūṇa sirañjaliṁ bhaṇaï rāmaṁ
rajaṁ karēhi supurisa! sayalaṁ āṇāguṇavisālaṁ // PaumaCa.46

ahayaṁ dharēmi chattaṁ, cāmaradhārō ya havaï sattuṁ jō
lacchīharō ya mantī, tujjha'nnaṁ suvihiyaṁ kiṁ vā? // PaumaCa.47

jāva imō ālāvō, vaṭṭaï tāvaṁ rahēṇa turantīṁ
taṁ cēva samuddēsaṁ, saṁpattā kēgaī dēvī // PaumaCa.48

ōyariya rahavarāō, paümaṁ āliṅgiūṇa rōvantī
saṁbhāsēi kamēṇaṁ, sīyāsahiyaṁ ca sōmittiṁ // PaumaCa.49

tō kēgaī pavuttā, putta,! viṇīyāpurimmi vaccāmō
rajjaṁ karēhi niyayaṁ, bharahō vi ya sikkhaṇīō tē // PaumaCa.50

mahilā sahāvacavalā, adīhapēhī sahāvamāillā
taṁ mē khamāhi puttaya! jaṁ paḍikūlaṁ kayaṁ tujjha // PaumaCa.51

tō bhaṇaï paümaṇāhō, ammō! kiṁ khattiyā aliyavāī
hōnti mahākulajāyā? tamhā bharahō kuṇaü rajaṁ // PaumaCa.52

tatthēva kāṇaṇavaṇē, paccakkhaṁ sabanaravarindāṇaṁ
bharahaṁ ṭhavēi rajē, rāmō sōmittiṇā sahiō // PaumaCa.53

namiūṇa kēgaīē, bhuyāsu uvagūhiuṁ bharahasāmi
aha tē sīyāsahiyā, saṁbhāsiya sabasāmantē // PaumaCa.54

dakkhiṇadēsābhimuhā, caliyā bharahō vi niyayapurahuttō
pattō karēi rajaṁ, indō jaha dēvanayarīē // PaumaCa.55

sō ērisammi rajjē, na karēi dhiī khaṇaṁ pi sōēṇaṁ
navaraṁ puṇa aṅgasuhaṁ, havaï cciya jiṇapaṇāmēṇaṁ // PaumaCa.56

bharahō jiṇindabhavaṇaṁ, vandaṇahēuṁ gaō saparivārō
thōūṇa pēcchaï muṇī, nāmēṇa juī saha gaṇēṇaṁ // PaumaCa.57


[p. 259]
bharahō namiūṇa muṇī, tassa ya puraō abhiggahaṁ dhīrō
gēṇhaï rāmadarisaṇē, pavajjā haṁ karissāmi // PaumaCa.58

bharahēṇa dhammanihasaṁ, samaṇō paripucchiō bhaṇaï ēvaṁ
jāva ya na ēi rāmō, tāva gihatthō kuṇasu dhammaṁ // PaumaCa.59

[vividhavrataniyamajinapūjādānādīnāṁ phalam —]
añcantaduddharadharā, cariyā nigganthamaharisīṇaṁ tu
parikammavisuddhassa u, hōhī suhasāhaṇā niyamā // PaumaCa.60

rayaṇaddīvammi gaō, gēṇhaï ēka pi jō mahārayaṇaṁ
taṁ tassa ihāṇīyaṁ, mahagghamōllaṁ havaï lōē // PaumaCa.61

jiṇadhammarayaṇadīvē, jaï niyamamaṇiṁ laēi ēka pi
taṁ tassa aṇagvēyaṁ, hōhī puṇṇaṁ parabhavammi // PaumaCa.62

paḍhamamahiṁsārayaṇaṁ, gēṇhēuṁ jō jiṇaṁ samancēi
sō bhuñjaï suralōē, iṇdiyasōkkhaṁ aṇōvamiyaṁ // PaumaCa.63

saccabayaniyamadharō, jō pūyaï jiṇavaraṁ payattēṇaṁ
sō hōi mahuravayaṇō bhuñjaï ya paraṁparasuhāiṁ // PaumaCa.64

parihariūṇa adattaṁ, jō jiṇanāhassa kuṇaï varapūyaṁ
sō navanihīṇa sāmī, hōhī maṇi-rayaṇapuṇṇāṇaṁ // PaumaCa.65

paranārīsu pasaṅgaṁ, na kuṇaï jō jiṇamayāsiō purisō
sō pāvaï sōhaggaṁ, nayaṇāṇandō varataṇūṇaṁ // PaumaCa.66

saṁtōsavayāmūlaṁ, dhāraï ya jiṇindavayaṇakayabhāvō
sō vivihadhaṇasamiddhō, hōi narō sabajaṇapujjō // PaumaCa.67

āhārapayāṇēṇaṁ, jāyaï bhōgassa ālaō niyayaṁ
jaï vi ya jāi viēsaṁ, tahavi ya sōkkhaṁ havaï tassa // PaumaCa.68

abhayaṣayāṇēṇa narō, jāyaï bhayavajiō nirōgō ya
nāṇassa payāṇēṇaṁ, sabakalāpāraō hōi // PaumaCa.69

āhāravajjaṇaṁ jō, karēi rayaṇīsu jiṇamayābhimuhō
ārambhapavattō vi ya, lahaï narō sō vi sugaïpahaṁ // PaumaCa.70

arahantanamōkkāraṁ, tiṇṇi vi kālē karēi jō purisō
tassa bahuyaṁ pi pāvaṁ, nāsaï varasuddhabhāvassa // PaumaCa.71

jala-thalayasurahinimmalakusumēsu ya jō jiṇaṁ samaccēi
sō divavimāṇaṭhiō, kīlaï pavaraccharāhi samaṁ // PaumaCa.72


[p. 260]
bhāvakusumēsu niyayaṁ, vimalēsu jiṇaṁ samaccaē jō u
sō hōi sundarataṇū , lōē pūyārihō purisō // PaumaCa.73

dhūyaṁ agaru-turukkaṁ, kuṁkuma-varacandaṇaṁ jiṇavarassa
jō dēi bhāviyamaī, sō surahisurō samubbhavaï // PaumaCa.74

jō jiṇabhavaṇē dīvaṁ, dēi narō tivabhāvasaṁjuttō
sō diṇayarasamatēō, dēvō uppajjaï vimāṇē // PaumaCa.75

chattaṁ camara-pēḍāyā, dappaṇa-lambūsayā viyāṇaṁ ca
jō dēi jiṇāyayaṇē, sō paramasiriṁ samubahaï // PaumaCa.76

gandhēhi jiṇavarataṇū , jō hu samālabhaï bhāviyamaīō
sō surabhigandhapaürē, ramaï vimāṇē sucirakālaṁ // PaumaCa.77

kāūṇa jiṇavarāṇaṁ, abhisēyaṁ surahigandhasalilēṇaṁ
sō pāvaï abhisēyaṁ, uppajjaï jattha jattha narō // PaumaCa.78

khīrēṇa nō'bhisēyaṁ, kuṇaï jiṇindassa bhattirāēṇaṁ
sō khīravimaladhavalē, ramaï vimāṇē sucirakālaṁ // PaumaCa.77

dahikumbhēsu jiṇaṁ jō, ēhavēi dahikōṭṭimē suravimāṇē
uppajjaï lacchidharō, dēvō divēṇa rūvēṇaṁ // PaumaCa.80

ēttō ghiyābhisēyaṁ, jō kuṇaï jiṇēsarassa payayamaṇō
sō hōi surahidēhō, surapavarō varavimāṇammi // PaumaCa.81

abhisēyapabhāvēṇaṁ, bahavē suvanti'ṇantaviriyāī
laddhāhisēyariddhī, suravarasōkkhaṁ aṇuhavanti // PaumaCa.82

bhattīe nivēyaṇayaṁ, baliṁ ca jō jiṇaharē paüñjēi
paramavibhūī pāvaī, ārōggaṁ cēva sō purisō // PaumaCa.83

gandhava-tūra-naṭaṁ, jō kuṇaï mahussavaṁ jiṇāyayaṇē
sō varavimāṇavāsē, pāvaï paramussavaṁ dēvō // PaumaCa.84

jō jiṇavarāṇa bhavaṇaṁ, kuṇaï jahāvihavasārasaṁjuttaṁ
sō pāvaï paramasuha, suragaṇaahiṇandiō suiraṁ // PaumaCa.85

jiṇapaḍimā kuṇaï narō, jō daḍhadhammō aṇannadiṭṭhīō
sō sura-māṇusabhōgē, bhōttūṇa sivaṁ pi pāvihii // PaumaCa.86

kāūṇa ēvamāī, dhammaṁ jiṇadēsiyaṁ suravimāṇē
uppajjiūṇa caviō, cakkaharattaṁ puṇō lahaï // PaumaCa.87


[p. 261]
puṇaravi kāūṇa tavaṁ, pāvaï siddhiṁ vimukkakammaraō
ēttō suṇasu vibhatti, jiṇavandaṇabhattirāyassa // PaumaCa.88

maṇasā hōi caütthaṁ, chaṭhṭhaphalaṁ uṭhṭhiyassa saṁbhavaï
gamaṇassa u ārambhē, havaï phalaṁ aṭṭhamōvāsē // PaumaCa.89

gamaṇē dasamaṁ tu bhavē, taha cēva duvālasaṁ gaē kiṁci
majjhē pakkhōvāsaṁ, māsōvāsaṁ tu didvēṇaṁ // PaumaCa.90

saṁpattō jiṇabhavaṇaṁ, lahaī chammāsiyaṁ phalaṁ purisō
saṁvacchariyaṁ tu phalaṁ dāruddēsē ṭhiō lahaï // PaumaCa.91

pāyakkhiṇṇē lahaï ya, varisasayaphalaṁ jiṇē taō diḍhē
pāvaï varisasahassaṁ, aṇantapuṇṇaṁ jiṇathuīē // PaumaCa.92

jiṇavandaṇabhattīē, na hu annō asthi uttamō dhammō
tamhā karēhi bhattī, bharaha! tumaṁ jiṇavarindāṇaṁ // PaumaCa.93

pacchā niggantharisī, bhaviūṇa sivaṁ pi jāhisi kayatthō
bharahō muṇissa pāsē, sāyāraṁ gēṇhaī dhammaṁ // PaumaCa.94

darisaṇavisuddhabhāvō, sāhupayāṇujjaō viṇīō ya
juyaïsayaddhēṇa samaṁ, karēi rajjaṁ guṇavisālaṁ // PaumaCa.95

ēvaṁvihē vi rajjē, niyaēṇa uvēi bhōgamaṇubandhaṁ
cintēi taggayamaṇō, phajhyā dikkhaṁ pavajjē haṁ? // PaumaCa.96

ēvaṁ tu rāyā bharahō viṇīō, jiṇindanigganthakahāhi sattō
sakammaviddhaṁsaṇahēubhūyaṁ, karēi cittaṁ vimalaṁ visuddhaṁ // PaumaCa.97


iya paümacariē dasarahapavvajārāmaniggamaṇabharaharajjavihāṇō nāma battīsaïmō uddēsaō samattō

[vajjayaṇṇaüvakkhāṇaṁ]

tattō tē dō vi jaṇā, sōyāsahiyā kamēṇa vaccantā
pattā ya tāvasakulaṁ, vakkala-jaḍadhāriṇō jantha // PaumaCa.1

nāṇāsaṁgahiyaphalaṁ, akiṭṭhadhaṇṇēṇa ruddhapahamaggaṁ
umbara-phaṇasa-vaḍāṇaṁ, samihāsaṁghāyakayapuñja // PaumaCa.2


[p. 262]
pavisanti tāvasakulaṁ, āsaṇa-viṇaōvayārakusalēhiṁ
saṁbhāsiyā ya payayā, sabēhiṁ tāvasagaṇēhiṁ // PaumaCa.3

vasiūṇa tattha rayaṇī, puṇaravi vaccanti aḍavipahamaggaṁ
dūrunnayasiharōhaṁ, pēcchanti u cittakūḍaṁ tē // PaumaCa.4

nāṇāvihadumachannaṁ, nāṇāvihasāvayāṇa āvāsaṁ
nāṇāpakkhisamiddhaṁ, girinaïyāruddhasaṁcāraṁ // PaumaCa.5

katthaï sīhaviyāriya-gayavararuhiracchaḍāruṇaṁ bhīmaṁ
katthaï sarabhuttāsiya–hatthiulavibhaggatarunivahaṁ // PaumaCa.6

katthaï varāha-kēsaridaḍhadappāvaḍiyajujjhasaṁgha
katthaï kaḍhiṇōratthala vagghacavēḍāhayaṁ mahisaṁ // PaumaCa.7

vāṇarabukkāraravaṁ, katthaï kilikilikilantapakkhigaṇaṁ
katthaï sīhabhayaduya-hariṇapalāyantasaṁghāyaṁ // PaumaCa.8

katthaï mattamahāgaya–gaṇḍālīṇāligumagumāyantaṁ
ēyārisaviṇiōgaṁ, pēcchanti ya cittakūḍaṁ tē // PaumaCa.9

nāṇātarubbhavāiṁ, nāṇāvihasurahigandhakaliyāī
khāyanti jahicchāē, phalāiṁ varasāyakaliyāī // PaumaCa.10

līlāe vaccamāṇā, caüsu vi māsēsu sāirēgēsu
pattā avantivisayaṁ, kāṇaṇa-vaṇamaṇḍiyaṁ rammaṁ // PaumaCa.11

jaṇa-dhaṇasamāulaṁ tē, kēttiyamēttaṁ pi vōliyā visayaṁ
annaṁ puṇa uddēsaṁ, pēcchanti jaṇujjhiyaṁ sahasā // PaumaCa.12

vaḍapāyavassa hēṭṭē, uvaviṭṭhā''sāsiyā ya vīsantā
bhaṇiō ya rāghavēṇaṁ, lakkhaṇa! dēsō imō vijaṇō // PaumaCa.13

sāsā akiṭṭhajāyā, ujjāṇadumā ya phalabharōṇa miyā
puṇḍucchavāḍapaürā, gāmā vi ya paṭṭaṇāyārā // PaumaCa.14

dīsanti sarā viulā, achinnapaümuppalā ya pakkhīsu
sayaḍēsu bhaṇḍaēsu ya, bhaggēsu visaṁṭhulā panthā // PaumaCa.15

caṇaya-tila-mugga-māsā, vikkhiriyā tandulā ya ṇēgavihā
dīsanti bahuddēsē, jiṇṇā ya jaraggavō paḍiyā // PaumaCa.16

bhaṇiō ya rāghavēṇaṁ, sōmittī paṭṭaṇaṁ va gāma vā
lakkhēhi samabbhāsē, parisamiyā dāruṇaṁ sīyā // PaumaCa.17


[p. 263]
tō lakkhaṇō valaggō, naggōhaṁ dīhaviḍavavitthāraṁ
rāmēṇa pucchiō sō, kiṁ pēcchasi ēttha sōmitti!? // PaumaCa.18

sō bhaṇaï dēva viyarḍa, rūvaṁ pēcchāmi pavayasaricchaṁ
sattataladhavalaēsu ya, pāsāyasaēsu parikiṇaṁ // PaumaCa.19

ārāmujjāṇēhi ya, talāyasahasēhi vēḍhiyaṁ sayalaṁ
dhaṇa-jaṇavayaparihīṇaṁ, dīsaï nayaraṁ imaṁ viyaḍaṁ // PaumaCa.20

ēka pēcchāmi pahū! purisaṁ aïcavalaturiyagaïgamaṇaṁ
bhaṇiō ya rāghavēṇaṁ, āṇēhi imaṁ maha samīvē // PaumaCa.21

ōyariya pāyavāō, sōmittī tēṇa āṇiō purisō
rāmassa calaṇajuyalaṁ, namiūṇa ṭhiō samabbhāsē // PaumaCa.22

taṁ bhaṇaï ṣaümaṇāhō, bhada! kaō āgaō si? kiṁ dēsō
vijaṇō dhaṇēṇa rahiō? sāhasu ēyaṁ phuḍaṁ majhaṁ // PaumaCa.23

sō bhaṇaï sirīguttō, ahayaṁ tu kuḍḍumbiō ya vaïēsō
ētthāgaō mahājasa! bhaṇāmi jaṁ taṁ nisāmēhi // PaumaCa.24

sīhōdarō ti nāmaṁ, ujjēṇīsāmiō naravarindō
tassa iha vajjayaṇṇō, dasaüranayarāhivō bhiccō // PaumaCa.25

mōttūṇa tihuyaṇaguruṁ, nigganthā sāhavō ya nāṇadharā
annassa namōkkāraṁ, na kuṇaï sō cēva purisassa // PaumaCa.26

nigganthapasāēṇaṁ, sammattaṁ vajjayaṇṇanaravaïṇā
pattaṁ jagavikkhāyaṁ, kiṁ na suyaṁ dēva! tumhēhiṁ? // PaumaCa.27

bhaṇiō ya lakkhaṇēṇaṁ, kēṇōvāraṇa tēṇa sammatta
laddhaṁ? kahēhi ēttō, jāyaṁ mē kōuyaṁ paramaṁ // PaumaCa.28

[vajrakarṇarājakathā —]
ēttō kahēi pahiō, dēva! nisāmēhi tassa sāhūṇaṁ
dinnō jahōvaēsō, paḍhamaṁ sammattara hiyassa // PaumaCa.29

aha vajjayaṇṇarāyā, pāraddhīphandiō paribhamantō
pēcchaï mandāraṇṇē, nigganthaṁ sāhavaṁ ēka // PaumaCa.30

gimhē silāyalatthō, sūrāyavasōsiēsu aṅgēsu
sīhō va bhayavimukkō, samattaniyamō daḍhadhiīō // PaumaCa.31

varaturayasamārūḍhō, kayantasarisō aṇāimicchattō
gantūṇa bhaṇaī sāhu, kiṁ ētthaṁ kuṇasi āraṇṇē? // PaumaCa.32


[p. 264]
tō bhaṇaï samaṇasīhō, ēttha hiyaṁ attaṇō vicintēntō
acchāmi raṇṇamajjhē, dukkhavimōkkhaṁ ca kuṇamāṇō // PaumaCa.33

puṇaravi bhaṇaï narindō, ēyāvatthassa bhōgarahiyassa
thōvaṁ pi natthi sōkkhaṁ, kiṁ appahiyaṁ tumaṁ sāhū!? // PaumaCa.34

visayapasaṅgābhimuhaṁ, nāūṇa subhāsiyaṁ bhaṇaï sāhū
jaṁ pucchasi appahiyaṁ, taṁ tē sarva nivēēmi // PaumaCa.35

jē visaēsu pasattā, tē appasuhēṇa vañciyā mūḍhā
bhamihinti bhavasamuddē, dukkhasahassāiṁ pāvantā // PaumaCa.36

hantūṇa vivihasattē, imassa dēhassa pōsaṇaṭṭāē
āyasapiṇḍō va jalē, jāhisi naraē nirabhirāmē // PaumaCa.37

nūṇaṁ tumē narāhiva! na ya vinnāyāō satta puḍhavīō
bahunarayasaṁkulāō, ghōrāṇalapajjalantīō // PaumaCa.38

duggandhā duppharisā, narayā sasi-sūravajjiyā niccaṁ
puḍapāya-kūḍasāmali-karavatta'sivattajantāī // PaumaCa.39

ēēsu pāvakammā, pakkhittā jīvahiṁsayā dīṇā
cakkhunimisaṁ pi sōkkhaṁ, na lahanti labhanti dukkhāī // PaumaCa.40

tē ērisaṁ mahantaṁ, dukkhaṁ pāvanti visayasuhalōlā
tāṇaṁ ciya appahiyaṁ, kērisayaṁ hōi purisāṇaṁ? // PaumaCa.41

kimpāgaphalasaricchaṁ, visayasuhaṁ appasōkkha-bahudukkhaṁ
ahiyaṁ vajjēhi imaṁ, karēhi jaṁ tujjha appahiyaṁ // PaumaCa.42

tēhi kayaṁ appahiyaṁ, jēhi u gahiyā mahatvayā pañca
ahavā'ṇuvayanirayā, sēsā dukkhāṇi pāvanti // PaumaCa.43

dhamma kāūṇa ihaṁ, pāvihisi surālaē paramasōkkhaṁ
dukkhaṁ aṇuhavasi ciraṁ, narayammi gaō ahammēṇaṁ // PaumaCa.44

ēē mayā aṇāhā, nicubiggā bhaüdyā raṇē
mā haṇasu rasāsattō, hiṁsaṁ tivihēṇa vajjēhi // PaumaCa.45

ēēsu ya annēsu ya, uvaēsasaēsu bōhiō jāhē
tāhē turaṅgamāō, ōyariuṁ paṇamaī sāhuṁ // PaumaCa.46


[p. 265]
tō bhaṇaï kayatthō'haṁ, vimukkapāvō na ēttha saṁdēhō
jō sura-narasaṁpujaṁ, sāhussa samāgamaṁ pattō // PaumaCa.47

nigganthāṇa mahāyasa! dukkaracariyā ahaṁ puṇa asattō
pañcāṇuvayadhārī, gihatthadhammē abhiramāmō // PaumaCa.48

ēvaṁ gihatthadhammaṁ, ghēttūṇa narāhivō samullavaï
jiṇasāhavē pamōttuṁ, annassa siraṁ na nāmēmi // PaumaCa.49

aha pīivaddhaṇaṁ sō, sāī pūēi paramabhāvēṇaṁ
uvavāsaṁ ciya giṇhaï, rāyā ullasiyarōmañcō // PaumaCa.50

uvavāsiyassa sāhū, kahēi paramaṁ hiyaṁ niyayakālaṁ
jaṁ kāūṇa gihatthā, bhaviyā muñcanti dukkhāṇaṁ // PaumaCa.51

sāgāra-nirāgāraṁ, cārittaṁ duvihamēva uvaï8
sālambaṇaṁ gihatthā, karanti sāhū nirālambaṁ // PaumaCa.52

pañca ya aṇuvayāī, sikkhāō taha ya hōnti cattāri
tiṇṇi ya guṇabayāī, jiṇindapūyā ya uvaïṭṭā // PaumaCa.53

tō vajjayaṇṇarāyā, jiṇadhammaṁ gēṇhiūṇa bhāvēṇaṁ
pavisaraï niyayanayaraṁ, bahujaṇaparivāriō tuṭṭhō // PaumaCa.54

gamiūṇa syaṇisamaya, majjiyajimiō maṇēṇa cintēi
sīhōyarassa viṇayaṁ, kaha tassa phuḍaṁ karissē haïṁ? // PaumaCa.55

cintēūṇa sumariuṁ, kaṇayamayaṁ muddiyaṁ iha 'ṅguḍhē
kārēmi rayaṇacittaṁ, suvayajiṇabimbasannihiyaṁ // PaumaCa.56

sā naravaīṇa muddā, kārāvēūṇa dāhiṇaṅguṭṭē
āviddhā rāēṇaṁ, harisasamullasiyagattēṇaṁ // PaumaCa.57

sīhōyarassa puraō, kāūṇa 'ṅguṭṭhayaṁ niyayasīsē
paṇamaï jiṇindapaḍimaṁ, sasaṁbhamō lōgamajjhammi // PaumaCa.58

parisuṇiya kāraṇēṇaṁ, kēṇaï vaïrīṇa sāhiē santē
dasaüravaïssa ruṭṭhō, gāḍhaṁ sīhōyarō rāyā // PaumaCa.59

tō sababalasamaggō, māṇī sannaddhabaddhatōṇīrō
caliō dasaüranayaraṁ, uvariṁ ciya vajjayaṇṇassa // PaumaCa.60

tāva ciya turiyagaī, vēṇulayāgahiyakarayalō purisō
gantūṇa vajjayaṇaṁ, bhaṇaï taō mē nisāmēhi // PaumaCa.61

aṇamōkkārassa pahū! ruṭṭhō sīhōyarō saha balēṇaṁ
āgacchaï turantō, tujjha vahatthaṁ savaḍahuttō // PaumaCa.62


[p. 266]
ēvaṁ narāhivō sō, kēṇa vi tuha vēriēṇa akkhāē
avasēṇa ihā''gacchaï, karēhi hiyaïcchiyaṁ jaṁ tē // PaumaCa.63

tō bhaṇaï vajjayaṇṇō, kō si tumaṁ? kattha dēsavatthabō?
kaha vā narindamantō, ēsō tē jāṇiō? bhaṇaha // PaumaCa.64

sō bhaṇaï kundanayarē, nāmēṇaṁ saddasaṁgamō vaṇiō
jaüṇā tassa varataṇū , puttō vi ya vijjuyaṅgō haṁ // PaumaCa.65

pattō ya jōbaṇasirī, ujjēṇī āgaō vaṇijjēṇaṁ
daṭṭa ṇa aṇaṅgalayā, vēsā āyallayaṁ pattō // PaumaCa.66

vasiō ya ēgaratti, tīe samaṁ tibanēharāēṇaṁ
kaḍhiṇayaraṁ ciya baddhō, hariṇō jaha vāurāē va // PaumaCa.67

jaṇaēṇa majjha niyayaṁ, samajjiyaṁ jaṁ dhaṇaṁ asaṁkhējaṁ
taṁ chammāsēṇa pahū! viṇāsiyaṁ mē duputtēṇaṁ // PaumaCa.68

jaha kamalē cha mahuyarō, āsattō taha ya kāmagayacittō
mahilāṇurāgarattō, kiṁ na kuṇaï sāhasaṁ purisō? // PaumaCa.69

aha sā sahīe puraō, nindantī niyayakuṇḍalaṁ muṇiyā
ēēṇa asārēṇaṁ, kiṁ kōraï kaṇṇabhārēṇaṁ? // PaumaCa.70

bhaṇaï ya ahō! kayatthā, dhannā sā siridharā mahādēvī
uttamarayaṇāiddhaṁ, sōhaï maṇikuṇḍalaṁ kaṇṇē // PaumaCa.71

ahayaṁ kuṇḍalacōrō, rāyaharaṁ patthiō nisi paōsē
sīhōyaraṁ suyā mē, pucchantī siriharā dēvī // PaumaCa.72

naravaï! na lahasi nidaṁ, kiṁ ubimgō si dāruṇaṁ ajaṁ?
sō bhaṇaï majjha niddā, kattō cintāulamaṇassa? // PaumaCa.73

maha viṇayaparāhuttō, na māriō jāva sundarī! duṭṭhō
dasaüranayarāhivaī, tāva kaō mē havaï niddā? // PaumaCa.74

suṇiūṇa vayaṇamēyaṁ, tō haṁ mōttūṇa cōriyaṁ turiō
ētthā''gaō narāhiva! tujjha rahassaṁ parikahēuṁ // PaumaCa.75

jāva cciya ullāvō, ēsō vaṭṭaï sabhāē majjhammi
tāva cciya balasahiō, pattō sīhōyarō rāyā // PaumaCa.76

sō gēhiuṁ asattō, taṁ nayaraṁ visamadugga-pāyāraṁ
parivēḍhiūṇa sayalaṁ, purisaṁ pēsēi tūrantaṁ // PaumaCa.77


[p. 267]
gantūṇa vajjayaṇṇaṁ, suṇiṭhuraṁ bhaṇaï sāmivayaṇēṇaṁ
muṇiucchāhiyahiyayō, jiṇavaragavaṁ samubahasi // PaumaCa.78

dinnaṁ maē pahuttaṁ, bhuñjasi visayaṁ jiṇaṁ namasēsi
māyāe vavaharantō, kaha ma nibuī kuṇasi? // PaumaCa.79

jaï majjha calaṇajuyalaṁ, na namasi rē vajjayaṇṇa! āgantuṁ
tō nicchaēṇa tujhaṁ, na ya jīyaṁ nēya rajaṁ tē // PaumaCa.80

tō bhaṇaï vajjayaṇṇō, maha visayaṁ sāhaṇaṁ puraṁ kōsaṁ
sabaṁ ca gēṇhaü ima, dhammadāraṁ ca mē dēu // PaumaCa.81

ēsā maē païnnā, ārūḍhā sāhusalliyāsammi
ēyaṁ tē parikahiyaṁ, amaō haṁ na ya vimuccāmi // PaumaCa.82

gantūṇa tattha dūō, sabaṁ sīhōyarassa sāhēi
ruṭṭhō rōhēi puraṁ, visayaṁ ca imaṁ viṇāsēi // PaumaCa.83

ēvaṁ tē parikahiyaṁ, dēsaviṇāsassa kāraṇaṁ sabaṁ
ēttō gacchāmi ahaṁ, sunnāgāraṁ imaṁ gāmaṁ // PaumaCa.84

ḍajjhantammi ya visaē, majjha vi niyayaṁ kuḍīrayaṁ daḍḍē
bhajjāe pēsiō haṁ, ghaḍapiḍharāṇaṁ ihaṁ dēva! // PaumaCa.85

ēvaṁ ciya parikahiē, daṭṭhaṇa'idukkhiyaṁ dayāvannō
paümō dēi mahagdhaṁ, niyayaṁ kaḍisuttayaṁ tassa // PaumaCa.86

paṇivaïūṇa gaō sō, niyayagharaṁ dēsiō aïturantō
paümō vi bhaṇaï ēttō, lakkhaṇa! vayaṇaṁ suṇasu majjhaṁ // PaumaCa.87

jāva cciya na ya sūrō, sudussahō hōi gimhakālammi
tāva imassa samīvaṁ, purassa bhūmiṁ pagacchāmō // PaumaCa.88

aha tē kamēṇa pattā, dasaṅganayarassa bāhirudēsē
candappahassa bhavaṇaṁ, thōūṇa avaṭṭhiyā tattha // PaumaCa.89

panthaparissamakhīṇā, sīyā daṭṭha ṇa lakkhaṇō sigdhaṁ
pavisaraï dasaüraṁ sō, aṇuṇāō dārapālēhiṁ // PaumaCa.90

diṭṭhō ya vajjayaṇṇō, tēṇa vi saṁbhāsiō niviṭṭhō ya
bhuñjāvēhi lahuṁ ciya, ēvaṁ bhaṇiō ya sūyārō // PaumaCa.91

tō jaṁpaï sōmittī, majjha gurū jiṇaharē saha piyāē
ciṭṭhaï tammi abhuttē, na ya haṁ bhuñjāmi āhāraṁ // PaumaCa.92

bhaṇiō sūyāravaī, naravaïṇā anna-pāṇamāīyaṁ
ēyassa tumaṁ niyayaṁ, dēhi turantō varāhāraṁ // PaumaCa.93


[p. 268]
taṁ lakkhaṇēṇa nīyaṁ, bhuttaṁ ciya bhōyaṇaṁ jahicchāē
sabaguṇēhi vi puṇṇaṁ, amayaṁ va taṇū suhāvēi // PaumaCa.94

tō bhaṇaï paümaṇāhō, pēcchasu sōmitti! vajjayaṇṇēṇaṁ
amuṇiyaguṇēṇa amhaṁ, vavahariyaṁ ērisaṁ kajjaṁ // PaumaCa.95

jiṇasāsaṇāṇurattō, aṇannadiṭṭhī dasaṅganayaravaī
jaï pāvihī viṇāsaṁ, dhiratthu tō amha jīēṇaṁ // PaumaCa.96

gantūṇa lakkhaṇa! tumaṁ, sīhōyarapatthivaṁ bhaṇasu ēvaṁ
'pīī karēhi sigdhaṁ, samayaṁ ciya vajjayaṇṇēṇaṁ // PaumaCa.97

jaṁ āṇavēsi bhaṇiūṇa lakkhaṇō aïgaō pavaṇavēgō
sibiraṁ ciya saṁpattō, kamēṇa pavisaraï rāyaharaṁ // PaumaCa.98

atthāṇimaṇḍavatthaṁ, jaṁpaï sīhōyaraṁ maïpagabbhō
bharahēṇa ahaṁ dūō, visajjiō tujjha pāsammi // PaumaCa.99

āṇavaï tumaṁ bharahō, samuddapērantavasumaīnāhō
jaha mā kuṇasu virōha, samayaṁ ciya vajjayaṇṇēṇaṁ // PaumaCa.100

sīhōyarō pavuttō, kiṁ guṇadōsē na yāṇaī bharahō
jaï viṇayamaïgayāṇaṁ, bhiccāṇa ṣahū pasajjanti // PaumaCa.101

maha ēsa vajjayaṇṇō, viṇayaparāhuttamāṇiō muiō
ēyassa paramuvāyaṁ, karēmi kiṁ tujjha tattīē? // PaumaCa.102

bhaṇaï taō sōmittī, kiṁ tē bahuēhi jaṁpiyavēhiṁ?
ēyassa khamasu sabaṁ, sīhōyara! majjha vayaṇēṇaṁ // PaumaCa.103

sōūṇa vayaṇamēyaṁ, bhaṇaï ya sīhōyarō paramaruṭṭhō
jō tassa vahaï pakkhaṁ, sō vi maē cēva hantabō // PaumaCa.104

puṇaravi bhaṇaï kumārō, maha vayaṇaṁ suṇasu savasaṁkhēvaṁ
saṁdhiṁ va kuṇasu ajaṁ, maraṇaṁ va lahum̐ paḍicchāhi // PaumaCa.105

bhaṇiyamēttē, saṁkhuhiyā sayalapatthivatthāṇī
nāṇācēṭṭāuliyā, nāṇādubayaṇakallōlā // PaumaCa.106

kēi bhaḍā sahasa tti ya, ukkaḍḍhēūṇa tattha churiyāō
sigghaṁ ciya saṁpattā, tassa vahatthujjayamaīyā // PaumaCa.107

saṁvēḍhiuṁ pavattā, masagā iva pavayaṁ samantēṇaṁ
aha sō bhaüjjhiyamaṇō, jujjhēi samaṁ riubhaḍēhiṁ // PaumaCa.108

karayalaghāyāhi bhaḍā, kēētthā''haṇaï calaṇapaharēhiṁ
jaṅghābalēṇa kēī, kēī pāḍaï bhuyabalēṇaṁ // PaumaCa.109


[p. 269]
jōhēṇa haṇaï jōhaṁ, paṇhipahārēṇa kuṇaï nijīvaṁ
annaṁ vidinnapaṭṭi, vajjaï ya ahōmuhaṁ paḍiyaṁ // PaumaCa.110

ēvaṁ sā bhaḍaparisā, bhaggā daṭṭha ṇa uḍhiō rāyā
sīhōyarō turantō, mattamahāgayavarārūḍhō // PaumaCa.111

turaya-raha-kuñjarēsu ya, annēsu bhaḍēsu baddhakavaēsu
vēḍhēi lakkhaṇaṁ sō, mēhō va raviṁ jalayakālē // PaumaCa.112

daṭṭaṇa āvayantaṁ, riusēnnaṁ sabaō samantēṇaṁ
sōmittī gayakhambha, ummūlēūṇa abhiṭṭō // PaumaCa.113

gaya-turaya-dappiyabhaḍē, pahaṇaï parihatthadacchaücchāhō
cakaṁ va samāiddhaṁ, taṁ riusēnnaṁ bhamāḍēi // PaumaCa.114

hayamāṇavahayajōhaṁ, bhaggaṁ taṁ riubalaṁ palōēi
dasaüranayarāhivaī, jaṇasahiō gōuraniviṭṭhō // PaumaCa.115

sāhu tti sāhu lōgō, jaṁpaï ēkvēṇimēṇa vīrēṇaṁ
bhaggaṁ suhaḍāṇīyaṁ, sīhēṇa va mayakulaṁ sayalaṁ // PaumaCa.116

bhaggā bhaṇanti suhaḍā, kiṁ ēsō dāṇavō surō kālō?
ēkkō jōhēi balaṁ, samarasamatthō mahāpurisō // PaumaCa.117

bhayavihalavēviyaṅgaṁ, gantuṁ sīhōyaraṁ rahārūḍhaṁ
uppaïūṇā''yaḍḍaï, dharaṇiyalatthaṁ kuṇaï vīrō // PaumaCa.118

niyayaṁsuyagalagahiyaṁ, puraō kāūṇa jaha ya balibaī
paümassa sanniyāsaṁ, sōmittī nēi turantō // PaumaCa.119

sīhōyaramahilāō, jaṁpanti vimukkanayaṇasalilāō
païbhikkhaṁ dēhi pahū! amhaṁ saraṇaṁ asaraṇāṇaṁ // PaumaCa.120

sō bhaṇaï rukkhasaṇḍa, jaṁ pēcchaha amha suviulaṁ puraō
ullambēmi haṇēuṁ, ēyaṁ sīhōyaraṁ sigdhaṁ // PaumaCa.121

sō tāṇa ruyantīṇaṁ, nōō sīhōyarō gurusamīvaṁ
kahiō ya lakkhaṇēṇaṁ, ēsa pahū! vajjayaṇṇariū // PaumaCa.122

sīhōyarō paṇāmaṁ, kāūṇaṁ bhaṇaï paümaṇāhaṁ sō
na yahaṁ jāṇāmi phuḍaṁ, kō si tumaṁ dēva! ētthā''ō? // PaumaCa.123

jaṁ āṇavēsi sāmiya! sarva pi karēmi tujjha bhiccō haṁ
bhaṇiō ya kuṇasu-saṁdhi, samayaṁ ciya vajjayaṇṇēṇaṁ // PaumaCa.124


[p. 270]
tāva ciya āhūō, hiēṇa purisēṇa dasaürāhivaī
sigdhaṁ ca samaṇupattō, payāhiṇaṁ kuṇaï jiṇabhavaṇē // PaumaCa.125

candappahassa paḍima, thōūṇaṁ rāghavaṁ suhāsīṇaṁ
saṁbhāsēi pahaṭhṭhō, sīyaṁ ca sasaṁbhamasiṇēhaṁ // PaumaCa.126

dēhāikusalapuvaṁ, paripucchēūṇa tattha uvaviṭhṭhō
kusalēṇa bhadda! tujjhaṁ, amha vi kusalaṁ bhaṇaï rāmō // PaumaCa.127

vaṭṭaï jāvullāvō, samāgaō tāva vijuyaṅgō vi
paümaṁ sīyāe samaṁ, paṇamiya tatthēva uvaviṭṭhō // PaumaCa.128

rāmēṇa vajjayaṇṇō, bhaṇiō sāhu tti jiṇamaē diṭṭhī
girirāyacūliyā iva, na kampiyā kusuivāēṇaṁ // PaumaCa.129

namiūṇa jiṇavarindaṁ, bhavōhamahaṇaṁ tilōyaparimahiyaṁ
kaha annō paṇamijjaï, imēṇa varaüttimaṅgēṇaṁ? // PaumaCa.130

tō bhaṇaï vajjayaṇṇō, avasīyantassa vasaṇapaḍiyassa
puṇṇēhi majjha supurisa! jāō ciya bandhavō tuhayaṁ // PaumaCa.131

bhaṇiō ya vajayaṇṇō, rāmakaṇidvēṇa jaṁ tumē i8
taṁ ajja bhaṇasu sigdhaṁ, sabaṁ saṁpāyaïssāmi // PaumaCa.132

tō bhaṇaï taṇāīṇa vi, pīḍaṁ nēcchāmi sabajīvāṇaṁ
maha vayaṇēṇa mahājasa! muñcasu sīhōyaraṁ ēyaṁ // PaumaCa.133

ēvaṁ bhaṇiē jaṇēṇaṁ, ugghuṭuṁ sāhu sāhu sāhu tti
sīhōyarō ya mukkō, vayaṇēṇaṁ vajjayaṇṇassa // PaumaCa.134

pīī kayā ya dōṇha vi, samayasamāvannapaṇayapamuhāṇaṁ
niyayanayarīe addhaṁ, tassa ya sīhōyarō dēi // PaumaCa.135

āsāṇa gayavarāṇaṁ, kuṇaï hiraṇṇassa samavibhāgēṇaṁ
sīhōyarō ya tuṭṭhō, dēi ciya vajjayaṇṇassa // PaumaCa.136

jiṇadhammapabhāvēṇaṁ, tattha gayāṇaṁ ca kuṇḍalaṁ divaṁ
sīhōyarēṇa dinnaṁ, tuṭēṇaṁ vijuyaṅgassa // PaumaCa.137

tō dasaürāhivēṇaṁ, duhiyāō tāṇa aṭṭha dinnāō
ābharaṇabhūsiyāō, sigdhaṁ puraō ya ṭhaviyāō // PaumaCa.138

sīhōyaramāīhiṁ, annēhi vi patthivēhi kannāṇaṁ
thaṇajahaṇasāliṇīṇaṁ, sayāṇi tiṇṇēva dinnāiṁ // PaumaCa.139

tō lakkhaṇō pavuttō, na ya mahilāsaṁgahēṇa mē kajaṁ
jāva ya na bhuyabalēṇaṁ, samajjiyaṁ attaṇō rajaṁ // PaumaCa.140


[p. 271]
bharahassa sayaladēsaṁ, mōttūṇaṁ malayapabaē amhē
kāūṇa païṭṭhāṇaṁ, niyayapuraṁ āgamissāmō // PaumaCa.141

ēyāṇa ahaṁ taïyā, pāṇiggahaṇaṁ karēmi kannāṇaṁ
bhaṇiyaṁ ca ēvamēyaṁ, sabēhi vi naravarindēhiṁ // PaumaCa.142

suṇiūṇa vayaṇamēyaṁ, tattha visaṇṇāō rāyadhūyāō
ghaṇavirahajalāvattē, sōgasamuddammi paḍiyāō // PaumaCa.143

ēvaṁ tē naravasabhā, vimaṇāō gēṇhiūṇa dhūyāō
niyayagharāṇi uvagayā, dasarahaputtē paṇamiūṇaṁ // PaumaCa.144

tatthēva jiṇaharē tē, rattiṁ gamiūṇa aruṇavēlāē
puṇaravi pahaṁ pavannā, vacanti suhaṁ jahicchāē // PaumaCa.145

cēiyaharaṁ pabhāē, sunnaṁ daṭṭha ṇa jaṇavaō sabō
gharavāvāravimukkō, jāō cciya tāṇa sōgēṇaṁ // PaumaCa.146

vajjasamaṇēṇa samayaṁ, jāyā sīhōyarassa varapīī
sammāṇa-dāṇa-gamaṇāiēsu parivaḍḍiyasiṇēhā // PaumaCa.147

ēvaṁ tē mandamandā dasarahataṇayā mēiṇī saṁcarantā, nāṇāgandhāipuṇṇē taruṇataruphalē bhuñjamāṇā pabhūē
pattā tē kūvavadaṁ bahubhavaṇa-mahāvappa-vāvīsamiddhaṁ, ujjāṇē sanniviṭṭhā vimalakusumiē mattabhiṅgāṇugīē // PaumaCa.148


iya paümacariē vajjayaṇṇaüvakkhāṇō nāma tēttīsaïmō uddēsaō samattō


---------------------------------------------------------------------
[sīhōdara-ruddabhūi-vālikhillōvakkhāṇāṇi]

tāṇaṁ ciya ujjāṇē, acchantāṇaṁ tisābhibhūyāṇaṁ
salilatthī tūrantō, sōmittī saravaraṁ pattō // PaumaCa.1

tāva ciya nayarāō, rāyasuō āgaō saravaraṁ taṁ
kīlaï jaṇēṇa samayaṁ, nāma kallāṇamālō tti // PaumaCa.2

pēcchaï tōrāvatthaṁ, sarassa sō lakkhaṇaṁ laliyarūvaṁ
pēsēi tassa purisaṁ, vammahasaratāḍiyasarīrō // PaumaCa.3

gantūṇa paṇamiūṇa ya, bhaṇaï pahū! ēha aṇuvarōhēṇaṁ
tuha darisaṇussavasuhaṁ, narindaputtō ihaṁ mahaï // PaumaCa.4


[p. 272]
paricintiūṁ ṇa kō vi hu, dōsō saṁpatthiō ya sōmittī
kōmalakaraggagahiō, bhavaṇaṁ ciya pēsiō tēṇaṁ // PaumaCa.5

ēkkāsaṇē niviṭṭhō, pucchaï sō lakkhaṇaṁ kaō si tumaṁ
ētthā''gaō mahājasa!?, kiṁ nāmaṁ tē parikahēhi? // PaumaCa.6

sō bhaṇaï vippaüttō, maha bhāyā ciṭṭhaē varujjāṇē
jōva na tassa udaṁ taṁ, vaccāmi taō kahissē haïṁ // PaumaCa.7

tō bhaṇaï narāhivaī, ētthaṁ ciya bhōyaṇaṁ bahuviyappaṁ
uvasāhiyaṁ maṇōjjaṁ, āṇijjaü sō ihaṁ cēva // PaumaCa.8

vīsajjiō turantō, paḍihārō kāṇaṇē suhaniviṭṭha
daṭū ṇa paümanāhaṁ, kuṇaï paṇāmaṁ sasīyassa // PaumaCa.9

bhaṇaï ya tō paḍihārō, sahōyarō dēva! tujjha varabhavaṇē
ciṭṭhaï visajjiō haṁ, nayarāhivaīṇa pāsaṁ tē // PaumaCa.10

sāmiya! kuṇasu pasāyaṁ, pavisarasu narāhivassa varabhavaṇaṁ
vayaṇēṇa tassa caliō, sīyāe samaṁ paümanāhō // PaumaCa.11

abbhuṭṭhiō ya ēntō, lacchīnilaēṇa jaṇasamaggēṇaṁ
dinnāsaṇōvaviṭṭhō, rāmō sōyāe sāhīṇō // PaumaCa.12

sabammi supaḍiuttē, kāuṁ majjaṇaya-bhōyaṇāīyaṁ
paümō lakkhaṇasahiō, pavēsiō tēṇa varabhavaṇaṁ // PaumaCa.13

pāēsu paṇamiūṇaṁ, jaṁpaï tāraṇa pēsiō dūō
maha suṇasu dēva! tubbhē, paramatthaṁ sārasabbhāvaṁ // PaumaCa.14

tō ujjhiūṇa lajjā, ōiṁdhaï kañcayaṁ sarīrāō
surajuvaï va maṇaharā, najjaï saggāu pabbhaṭṭhā // PaumaCa.15

diṭṭhā varakannā sā, jōvaṇa-lāyaṇṇa-kantipaḍipuṇṇā
lacchi va kamalarahiyā, bhavaṇasirī cēva pañcakkhā // PaumaCa.16

taṁ bhaṇaï paümanāhō, bhaddē! kiṁ ērisēṇa vēsēṇa
kīlasi varataṇuyaṅgī, kannē! niyayammi rajjammi? // PaumaCa.17

lajjōṇaüttimaṅgī, bhaṇaï ya nisuṇēhi dēva! vittantaṁ
nāmēṇa vālikhillō, iha purisāmī naravarindō // PaumaCa.18

tassa puhaï tti mahilā, sā gurubhārā kayāi saṁpannā
mēcchāhivēṇa jujjhē, baddhō sō naravaī taïyā // PaumaCa.19


[p. 273]
suṇiūṇa vālikhillaṁ, baddhaṁ sīhōyarō bhaṇaï sāmī
jō iha gabbhuppannō, hōhī puttō ya sō rajjē // PaumaCa.20

tattō ya ahaṁ jāyā, mantīṇa subuddhināmadhēēṇaṁ
sīhōyarassa siṭuṁ, sāmiya! puttō samuppannō // PaumaCa.21

bālattaṇammi raïyaṁ, nāma kallāṇamāliṇī majhaṁ
navaraṁ ciya sabbhāvaṁ, mantī jaṇaṇī ya jāṇanti // PaumaCa.22

kāūṇa purisavēsaṁ, gurūhi rajjāhivō pariṭṭhaviō
ahayaṁ tu pāvakammā, mahilā tumhaṁ samakkhāyaṁ // PaumaCa.23

tō kuṇaha pasāyaṁ mē, tāyaṁ mōēha mēcchapaḍibaddhaṁ
gurusōyajalaṇataviyaṁ, imaṁ sarīraṁ suhāvēha // PaumaCa.24

sīhōyarō vi rāyā, na ya tassa vimōyaṇaṁ pahū! kuṇaï
jaṁ ēttha visayadavaṁ, niyayaṁ pēsēmi mēcchāṇaṁ // PaumaCa.25

nayaṇaṁsuē muyantī, rāmēṇā''sāsiyā sasīēṇaṁ
bhaṇiyā ya lakkhaṇēṇaṁ, maha vayaṇaṁ suṇasu taṇuyaṅgī! // PaumaCa.26

rajaṁ karēhi sundari!, imēṇa vēsēṇa tāva bhayarahiyā
mōēmi nāva tujhaṁ, piyaraṁ kaïēsu diyahēsu // PaumaCa.27

ēvabhaṇiyammi tōsaṁ, jaṇaē va vimōiē gayā bālā
ullasiyarōmakūvā, sahasa tti samujjalā jāyā // PaumaCa.28

divasāṇi tiṇṇi vasiuṁ, tatthujjāṇē maṇōharē rammē
sīyāe samaṁ dōṇi vi, viṇiggayā suhaṣasuttajaṇē // PaumaCa.29

aha vimalammi pahāē, sā kannā tē tahiṁ apēcchantī
rōyaï kaluṇaṁ mayacchī, sōgāvannēṇa hiyaēṇaṁ // PaumaCa.30

ēvaṁ ujjāṇāō, niyayapuraṁ pavisiūṇa sā kannā
rajaṁ karēi nayarē, tēṇaṁ ciya purisavēsēṇaṁ // PaumaCa.31

aha tē kamēṇa pattā, vimalajalaṁ nammayaṁ suvitthiṇṇaṁ
cakkāya-haṁsa-sārasa-kala mahuruggīyasaddālaṁ // PaumaCa.32

saṁkhubhiyamayara-kacchava-macchasamucchaliyaviluliyāvattaṁ
taralataraṅgubbhāsiya-jalahatthivimukkasikkāraṁ // PaumaCa.33

sīyāe samaṁ dōṣṇi vi, līlāē nammayaṁ samuttiṇṇā
vijhāḍavi pavannā, ghaṇataruvara-sāvayāiṇṇaṁ // PaumaCa.34


[p. 274]
panthēṇa saṁcarantā, vārijjantā va gōvapahiēhiṁ
varavasabhalīlagāmī, kiṁcuddēsaṁ vaïkvantā // PaumaCa.35

aha bhaṇaï jaṇayataṇayā, vāmadisāvaṭṭhiō kaḍuyarukkhē
vāharaï imō riṭṭhō, sāmiya! kalahaṁ nivēēi // PaumaCa.36

annō ya khīrarukkhē, vāharamāṇō jayaṁ parikahēi
bhaṇiyaṁ mahānimittē, hōi muhuttantarē kalahō // PaumaCa.37

thōvantaraṁ niviṭṭhā, puṇaravi vaccanti aḍavipahahuttā
puraō mēcchāṇa balaṁ, tāva ya pēcchanti masivaṇṇaṁ // PaumaCa.38

mēcchāṇa samāvaḍiyā, dōṇṇi vi saravarasayāṇi muñcantā
taha jujjhiuṁ pavattā, jaha bhaggā'ṇāriyā sabē // PaumaCa.39

aha tē bhaüdyamaṇā, gantūṇa kahēnti niyayasāmissa
mahayā balēṇa sō vi.ya, puraō ya uvaṭṭhiō tāṇaṁ // PaumaCa.40

micchā kāgōṇandā, vikkhāyā mahiyalammi tē sūrā
jē sayalapatthivēsu vi, na ya saṁgāmammi bhañjanti // PaumaCa.41

daṭṭhaṇa uccharantaṁ, mēcchabalaṁ pāusē va ghaṇavandraṁ
lacchīharēṇa ēttō, ruṭēṇaṁ valaïyaṁ dhaṇuyaṁ // PaumaCa.42

apphāliyaṁ sarōsaṁ, cāvaṁ lacchīharēṇa sahasa ti
jēṇaṁ taṁ mēcchabalaṁ, bhīyaṁ āgampiyaṁ sahasā // PaumaCa.43

daṭṭha ṇa niyayasēnnaṁ, saṁbhantaṁ bhayapaḍantadhaṇu-khaggaṁ
ōyariya rahavarāō, paṇamaï tō micchasāmantō // PaumaCa.44

jaṁpaï kōsambīē, vippō vēsāṇalō tti nāmēṇaṁ
bhajjā sē païbhattā, tīē haṁ kucchisaṁbhūō // PaumaCa.45

nāmēṇa ruddabhūī, bālapabhūīe duṭṭhakammakarō
gahiō ya cōriyāē, sūlāe nirōviō bhēttuṁ // PaumaCa.46

kāruṇṇamuvagaēṇaṁ, vaṇiēṇa vimōiō tahiṁ santō
ētthā''gaō bhamantō, kāgōnandāhivō jāō // PaumaCa.47

iha ēttiyammi kālē, balavantā jaï vi patthivā bahavē
maha diṭṭigōyaraṁ tē, asamatthā raṇamuhē dhariuṁ // PaumaCa.48

sō haṁ nirāṇukampō, darisaṇamēttēṇa tumha bhayabhīō
calaṇēsu ēsa paḍiō, bhaṇaha lahuṁ kiṁ karēmi? tti // PaumaCa.49


[p. 275]
paümēṇa taō bhaṇiō, kivāluṇā jaï karēha maha vayaṇaṁ
mōēhi bandhaṇāō, narāhivaṁ vālikhillaṁ taṁ // PaumaCa.50

naṁ āṇavēsi sāmiya!, ēvaṁ bhaṇiūṇa vālikhillaṁ sō
mōēi bandhaṇāō, sammāṇaṁ sē paraṁ kuṇaï // PaumaCa.51

nīō paümasayāsaṁ, paṇamaï ya puṇō puṇō pasaṁsantō
jē bandhaṇāu mukkō, ahayaṁ tumhēṁ pasāēṇaṁ // PaumaCa.52

bhaṇiō ya rāghavēṇaṁ, iṭṭhajaṇasamāgamaṁ lahasu sigdhaṁ
jāṇihisi sabamēyaṁ, niyayapuri patthiō santō // PaumaCa.53

caliō ya vālikhillō, paṇaïṁ kāūṇa ruddabhūī ya
paümō mēcchāhivaī, ṭhaviya vasē vaccaï pahēṇaṁ // PaumaCa.54

rāyā vi vālikhillō, saṁpattō ruddabhūiṇā samayaṁ
pavisaraï kūvavaī, bandijaṇugghuṭṭhajayasaddō // PaumaCa.55

ciravippaōgaduhiyā, paṇamaï kallāṇamāliṇī piyaraṁ
tēṇa vi ya uttamaṅgē, dhūyā paricumbiyā tayaṇu // PaumaCa.56

puhavī vi mahādēvī, parituṭhṭhā pulaïēsu aṅgēsu
saṁbhāsiyā saṇēhaṁ, bhiccā ya sanāyarā savē // PaumaCa.57

bahāō mahārahasuō, samayaṁ ciya ruddabhūiṇā ēttō
āharaṇa-rayaṇa-kaṇayāiēsu pūēi mēcchavaī // PaumaCa.58

saṁpūiō payaṭṭō, āucchēūṇa mēcchasāmantō
saṁpattō niyayapura, ramaï suhaṁ vālikhillō vi // PaumaCa.59

sōūṇa dhīrassa vicēṭṭhiyaṁ tē, sīhōdarāī bahavē narindā
pasaṁsamāṇā vimalaṁ nasōhaṁ, jāyā sasaṅkā paümassa niccaṁ // PaumaCa.60


iya paümacariē vālikhillaüvakkhāṇaṁ nāma caütīsaïmō uddēsaō samattō

[kavilōvakkhāṇaṁ]

aha tē kamēṇa vijhaṁ, aïkkamēūṇa pāviyā visayaṁ
majjhēṇa vahaï tāvī, jassa naī nimmalajalōhā // PaumaCa.1

vacantāṇuhēsō, jāō jalavajjiō araṇṇammi
tāva ciya aïgāḍhaṁ, sīyā taṇhaṁ samubahaï // PaumaCa.2


[p. 276]
bhaṇaï paümaṁ vi sīyā, sūsaï kaṇṭhō mahaṁ aïtisāē
parisamajaṇiyaṁ ca taṇū , tamhā udayaṁ samāṇēha // PaumaCa.3

hatthāvalambiyakarā, bhaṇiyā rāmēṇa pēccha āsannē
gāmaṁ tuṅgavaragharaṁ, ēttha tuma pāṇiyaṁ piyasu // PaumaCa.4

ēva bhaṇiūṇa saṇiyaṁ, saṇiyaṁ saṁpatthiyā'ruṇaggāmē
gēhammi ya uvaviṭhṭhā, kavilassa u āhiyaggissa // PaumaCa.5

taṁ babhaṇīe dinnaṁ, pīyaṁ sīyāe sīyalaṁ salilaṁ
tāva ciya raṇṇāō, saṁpattō takkhaṇaṁ kavilō // PaumaCa.6

taruphala-samihakkantō, kamaṇḍaluggahiyaüṁchavittīō
aïkōhaṇō visīlō, uluyamuhō kakkaḍacchīō // PaumaCa.7

tē tattha sanniviṭṭhā, daṭṭhaṇaṁ bambhaṇī bhaṇaï ruṭṭhō
ēyāṇa gharapavēsō, kiṁ tē dinnō mahāpāvē? // PaumaCa.8

paharēṇumaïlacalaṇā, mā mē uvahaṇaha aggihōttagharaṁ
tubbhē niṣphiḍaha lahuṁ, kiṁ acchaha ēttha nillajjā? // PaumaCa.9

tō bhaṇaï jaṇayadhūyā, imēṇa duvayaṇaagginivahēṇaṁ
daḍḍhē sarīrayaṁ mē, raṇṇaṁ va jahā vaṇadavēṇaṁ // PaumaCa.10

aḍavīsu varaṁ vāsō, samayaṁ hariṇēsu jattha sacchandō
na ya ērisāṇi sāmiya!, suvanti jahiṁ duvayaṇāiṁ // PaumaCa.11

lōēṇa tattha baḍuō, vārijantō vi gāmavāsīṇaṁ
na ṣasajjaï duṭṭhappā, bhaṇaï ya gēhāō nipphiḍaha // PaumaCa.12

āruṭṭhō sōmittī, gāḍhaṁ dubayaṇapharusaghāēhiṁ
calaṇēsu gēṇhiūṇaṁ, ahōmuhaṁ bhāmaī viṣpaṁ // PaumaCa.13

bhaṇiō ya rāghavēṇaṁ, lakkhaṇa! na ya ērisaṁ havaï juttaṁ
mēllēhi imaṁ vippaṁ, pāvaṁ ayasassa āmūlaṁ // PaumaCa.14

samaṇā ya bambhaṇā vi ya, gō pasu itthī ya bālayā vuḍḍā
jaï vi hu kuṇanti dōsaṁ, taha vi ya ēē na hantabā // PaumaCa.15

mōttūṇa bambhaṇaṁ taṁ, sōmittī rāghavō saha piyāē
aha niggaō gharāō, puṇaravi ya pahēṇa vaccanti // PaumaCa.16

kūlēsu girinaīṇaṁ, nivasāmi varaṁ araṇṇavāsammi
na ya khalayaṇassa gēhaṁ, pavisāmi puṇō bhaṇaï rāmō // PaumaCa.17


[p. 277]
tāva ciya ghaṇakālō, samāgaō gajiyāisaddālō
cañcalataḍicchaḍālō, dhārāsaṁbhinnapahamaggō // PaumaCa.18

andhāriyaṁ samatthaṁ, gayaṇaṁ ravikiraṇavavagayālōyaṁ
varisantēṇa palōṭṭā, jaha puhaī bhariyakūva-sarā // PaumaCa.19

salilēṇa timmamāṇā, pattā niggōhaṣāyavaṁ viulaṁ
ghaṇaviyaḍapattabahalaṁ, najaï gēhaṁ va aïrammaṁ // PaumaCa.20

sō tattha dumāhivaī, ibhakaṇṇō nāma sāmiyaṁ gantuṁ
bhaṇaï karēhi parittaṁ, gihāu uvāsiō ahayaṁ // PaumaCa.21

avahivisaēṇa nāuṁ, halahara-nārāyaṇā turiyavēgā
tatthēva āgaō sō, viṇāyagō pūyaṇō nāmaṁ // PaumaCa.22

tāṇa pabhāvēṇa lahuṁ, vacchallēṇa ya visālapāyārā
jaṇa-dhaṇa-rayaṇa-samiddhā, tēṇa tahiṁ nimmiyā nayarī // PaumaCa.23

tatthēva suhaṣasuttā, pāhāuyagīya maṅgalaravēṇaṁ
pēcchanti navaviuddhā, bhavaṇaṁ tūlīnisaṇṇaṅgā // PaumaCa.24

pāsāya-tuṅgatōraṇa-haya-gaya-sāmanta-pariyaṇāiṇṇā
dēhuvagaraṇasamiddhā, dhaṇayapurī cēva paccakkhā // PaumaCa.25

nakkhāhivēṇa sahasā, rāmassa viṇimmiyā purī jēṇaṁ
tēṇaṁ sā rāmapurī, jāyā puhaīe vikkhāyā // PaumaCa.26

tō bhaṇaï gaṇāhivaī, sēṇiya! nisuṇēhi tattha sō vippō
sūruggamē ṣayaṭṭō, dabbhayahatthō araṇṇammi // PaumaCa.27

tēṇa bhamantēṇa tahi, divā nayarī gharā-''vaṇasamiddhā
uvavaṇa-talāya-jaṇa-dhaṇa-samāulā tuṅgapāyārā // PaumaCa.28

cintēi bambhaṇō sō, kiṁ suralōgāu āgayā ēsā
nayarī maṇābhirāmā, kasya vi puṇṇāṇubhāvēṇaṁ? // PaumaCa.29

kiṁ hōjja maē sumiṇō?, diṭṭhō māyā va kēṇaï paüttā?
pittāhiyaṁ va cak?, hōja va maraṇaṁ samāsannaṁ 1 // PaumaCa.30

ēyāṇi ya annāṇi ya, paricintantēṇa mahiliyā divā
bhaṇiyā ya kassa bhaddē!, ēsa purī dēvanayari va? // PaumaCa.31

sābhaṇaï kiṁ na yāṇasi?, ēsa purī bhadda! paümanāhassa
sīyā jassa mahiliyā, havaï ya lacchīharō bhāyā // PaumaCa.32


[p. 278]
annaṁ ṣi vippa! nisuṇasu, paümō davaṁ jahicchiyaṁ dēi
tēṇa vi sā paḍibhaṇiyā, kahēhi taddarisaṇōvāyaṁ // PaumaCa.33

sā jakkhiṇī sunāmā, bhaṇaï ya bhō vippa! suṇasu maha vayaṇaṁ
sāhēmi taṁ uvāyaṁ, jēṇa tumaṁ pēcchasī paümaṁ // PaumaCa.34

gayavara-sīhamuhēhiṁ, vēyālabihīsiēhi bahuēhiṁ
nayarīe tiṇṇi dārā, rakkhijjantē ya purisēhiṁ // PaumaCa.35

pubaddārassa bahiṁ jaṁ pēcchasi dhaya-baḍāyakayasōhaṁ
taṁ jiṇaharaṁ mahantaṁ, jattha susāhū parivasanti // PaumaCa.36

jō kuṇaï namōkkāra, arahantāṇaṁ visuddhabhāvēṇaṁ
sō pavisaï nivigdhaṁ, lahaï vaha jō u vivarīō // PaumaCa.37

jō puṇa aṇuvayadharō, jiṇadhagmujjayamaṇō susīlō ya
sō puijjaï purisō, paümēṇa aṇēgadavēṇaṁ // PaumaCa.38

suṇiūṇa vayaṇamēyaṁ, vaccaï vippō thuī paüñjantō
saṁpattō jiṇabhavaṇaṁ, paṇamaï ya tahiṁ jiṇavarindaṁ // PaumaCa.39

taṁ paṇamiūṇa sāhū, pucchaï arahantadēsiyaṁ dhammaṁ
samaṇō vi aparisēsaṁ, sāhēi aṇubayāmūlaṁ // PaumaCa.40

taṁ sōūṇa diyavarō, dharma gēṇhaï gihatthamaṇuciṇṇaṁ
jāō visuddhabhāvō, aṇannadiṭṭhī paramatuṭṭhō // PaumaCa.41

asaṇāiēṇa bhattaṁ, laddhaṁ aha pāṇiyaṁ ca tisiēṇaṁ
taha tujjha pasāēṇaṁ, sāhava! dhammō maē laddhō // PaumaCa.42

ēva bhaṇiūṇa samaṇaṁ, paṇamiya sabāyarēṇa parituṭṭhō
pariōsajaṇiyahiyaō, niyayagharaṁ patthiō vippō // PaumaCa.43

bhaṇaï pahiṭhṭhō kavilō, sundari! sāhēmi jaṁ maē ajaṁ
di8 adiṭṭhapuvaṁ, suyaṁ ca gurudhammasabassaṁ // PaumaCa.44

samihāhēuṁ saṁpatthiēṇa, diṭṭhā purī maē raṇṇē
mahilā ya sundaraṅgī, nūṇaṁ sā dēvayā kā vi // PaumaCa.45

paripucchiyāe siṭuṁ, tīē maha ēsa vippa? rāmapurī
sāvayajaṇassa paümō, dēi kilāṇantayaṁ davvaṁ // PaumaCa.46

samaṇassa sanniyāsē, dhammaṁ suṇiūṇa sāvaō jāō
parituṭṭhō haṁ sundari?, dullahalambhō maē laddhō // PaumaCa.47


[p. 279]
sā bambhaṇī susammā, bhaṇaï paī jō tumē muṇisayāsē
gahiō jiṇavaradhammō, sō hu maē cēva paḍivannō // PaumaCa.48

savāyarēṇa sundari!, phāsuyadāṇaṁ muṇīṇa dāyavaṁ
arahantō sayakālaṁ, namaṁsiyavō ṣayattēṇaṁ // PaumaCa.49

tō bhuñjiūṇa sōkkhaṁ, uttarakuravāibhōgabhūmīsu
labhihisi paramparāē, nivāṇamaṇuttaraṁ ṭhāṇaṁ // PaumaCa.50

sāgāradhammaniraō, kavilō taṁ bambhaṇī bhaṇaï ēvaṁ
paümaṁ paümadalacchī!, gantūṇa puriṁ ca pēcchāmō // PaumaCa.51

davēṇa vippamukkaṁ, purisaṁ dāriddasāgarē paḍiyaṁ
uttārēi niruttaṁ, rāmō aṇukampamāvannō // PaumaCa.52

tō niggaō gharāō, puraō kāūṇa bambhaṇī vippō
kusumakaraṇḍayahatthō uccaliō rāmapurihattō // PaumaCa.53

sō tattha vaccamāṇō, pēcchaī nāgē phaḍāvisālillē
vēyālē ya bahuvihē, dāḍhāvigarālabīhaṇaē // PaumaCa.54

ēyāṇi ya annāṇi ya, rūvāṇi bahuppayāraghōrāṇi
kantāe samaṁ vippō, ghōsēi mahānamōkkāraṁ // PaumaCa.55

mōttūṇa lōgadhamma, ahiyaṁ jiṇasāsaṇujjaō ahayaṁ
jāō namō jiṇāṇaṁ, saṁpaï'tīē bhavissāṇaṁ // PaumaCa.56

pañcasu pañcasu pañcasu, bharahē ēravaēsu ya taha vidēhēsu
ēēsu ya jāyāṇaṁ, namō jiṇāṇaṁ jiyabhayāṇaṁ // PaumaCa.57

jiṇadhammanicchiyamaṇō, ēvaṁ tu bihīsiyāu vōlēuṁ
pattō rāmapurī sō, kantāsahiō maṇabhirāmaṁ // PaumaCa.58

abbhantaraṁ paviṭhṭhō, dāvēntō mahiliyāe bhavaṇavarē
rāyaṅgaṇaṁ ca pattō, ālōbaī lakkhaṇaṁ vippō // PaumaCa.59

pēcchantēṇa sumariō, ēsō sō rūva-kantipaḍipuṇṇō
jō kaḍuya-kakkasēhiṁ, taïyā vayaṇēhi mē sattō // PaumaCa.60

tassa bhaēṇaṁ turiō, mōttūṇaṁ bambhaṇī palāyantō
lacchīharēṇa diṭṭhō, sigdhaṁ sahāviō vippō // PaumaCa.61

vāhariō ya niyattō, da₹ṇaṁ dō vi tē mahāpurisē
satthiṁ karēi kavilō, muñcaï pupphañjalī puraō // PaumaCa.62

paümēṇa bambhaṇō sō, bhaṇiō kattō si āgaō tuhayaṁ?
tō bhaṇaï āgaō haṁ, aruṇaggāmāu tuha pāsaṁ // PaumaCa.63


[p. 280]
kavilō nāmēṇāhaṁ, havaï susammā ya rōhiṇī ēsā
taïyā maē na nāō, pacchannamahēsarō si tumaṁ // PaumaCa.64

jaï vi ya sartha narindō, paravisayagaō havēja ēgāgaü
taha vi ya parihavaṭhāṇaṁ, pāvaï lōē ṭhiī ēsā // PaumaCa.65

jassa'tthō tassa suhaṁ, jassa'tthō paṇḍiō ya sō lōē
jassa'tthō sō guruō, atthavihūṇō ya lahuō u // PaumaCa.66

tassa mahatthō ya jasō, dhammō vi ya tassa hōi sāhōṇō
dhammō vi sō samatthō, jassa ahiṁsā samuddiṭṭhā // PaumaCa.67

ahavā kiṁ na suyaṁ tē?, saṇaṁkumārō samantabharahavaī
rūvassa darisaṇaṭē, jassa surā āgayā ihaī // PaumaCa.68

saṁvēgajaṇiyakaruṇō, pavajaṁ gēṇhiuṁ paribhamantō
bhikkhaṁ ca alabhamāṇō, vijayapuraṁ pāviō kamasō // PaumaCa.69

paḍilāhiō mahappā, kayāi dāriddasamabhibhūyāē
ṣaḍiyā ya rayaṇavuṭṭhī, gandhōdaya-ghupphavarisaṁ ca // PaumaCa.70

ēvaṁvihā vi samaṇā, sura-naramahiya-'cciyā daḍhacarittā
paravisayaṁ viharantā, paribhūyā duṭṭhalōēṇaṁ // PaumaCa.71

pharusāṇi aṇiṭṭhāṇi ya, jaṁ bhaṇiyā rāga-dōsa-mūḍhēṇaṁ
taṁ khamaha aviṇayaṁ mē, jō tumha pahū! kaō taïyā // PaumaCa.72

kavilaṁ ēva ruyantaṁ, saṁthāvaï rāghavō mahurabhāsī
sīyā vi susamma saṁbhamēṇa parinivuī kuṇaï // PaumaCa.73

kaṇayakalasēsu kavilō, kiṁkarapurisēhi paümaāṇāē
sādhammiō tti kāuṁ, kantāe samaṁ taō ṇhaviō // PaumaCa.74

bhuñjāviō vicittaṁ, āhāraṁ, bhūsiō ya rayaṇēhiṁ
dinnaṁ ca dhaṇaṁ bahuyaṁ, tāhē gēhaṁ gaō vippō // PaumaCa.75

ājammadhaṇavihīṇō, pattō jaṇavimhayaṁ mahābhōgaṁ
taha vi ya na karēi dhiī, sammāṇaparāhayasarīrō // PaumaCa.76

puvaṁ vihaḍiya-paḍiyaṁ, majjha gharaṁ āsi vibhavaparihīṇaṁ
rāmassa pasāēṇaṁ, jāyaṁ dhaṇa-rayaṇaparipuṇṇaṁ // PaumaCa.77

hā! ka8 sappurisā, jaṁ mē nibhacchiyā alajjēṇaṁ
taṁ mē dahaï sarīraṁ, sallaṁ ca avaṭṭhiyaṁ hiyaē // PaumaCa.78


[p. 281]
aṭṭhārasa ya sahassā, ghēṇaṁ taṁ ca gēhiṇī' mōttuṁ
nandajaïssa sayāsē, kavilō dikkhaṁ samaṇupattō // PaumaCa.79

bārasavihaṁ tavaṁ sō, kuṇamāṇō māruō va nīsaṅgō
viharaï muṇī mahappā, gāmā-''garamaṇḍiyaṁ vasuhaṁ // PaumaCa.80

jō kavilassa imaṁ tu payatthaṁ, ēkkamaṇō nisuṇēi maṇussō
sō uvavāsasahassavihāyaṁ, bhuñjaï divasuhaṁ vimalaṅgō // PaumaCa.81


iya paümacariē kavilōvakkhāṇaṁ nāma pañcatīsaïmō uddēsō samattō
