ēēla caünikāyā, dēvā kōlanti pariyaṇasamamgā
raïsāgarōvagāḍhā, na saranti niē vi hu vimāṇē // PaumaCa.14

ēyāṇa ubavaṇāṇaṁ, ṭhiyāī majjhammi cēhayagharāī
tavaṇijapijharāī, bahuvihasurasaṅghanamiyāī // PaumaCa.15

vavaïṇṇō pakṇasuō, tattha kmiāṇāu pariyaṇasamaggō
pāyakkhiṇaṁ karēuṁ, pavisaraï tō niṇāgāraṁ // PaumaCa.16

dahūṇa siddhapaḍimā, bahulakkhaṇasaṁjuyā diṇayarāmā
paṇamaï pahaṭṭhamaṇasō, kantāhi samaṁ pavaṇaputtō // PaumaCa.17

maṇa-nagaṇahāriṇōō, haṇukssa piyāu kaṇayakamalēhiṁ
pūēnti siddhapaḍimā, annēhiṁ vi divakusumēhi // PaumaCa.18

sayamēva pavaṇaputtō, paḍimāō kuṅkumēṇa achēuṁ
dēi varasurahidhūyaṁ, baliṁ ca tivāṇurāēṇaṁ // PaumaCa.19

ēttō vāṇaramaülī, arahantaṁ jhāiūṇa bhāvēṇaṁ
thuṇaï thuimālēhiṁ, vivihēhiṁ pāvamahaṇēhiṁ // PaumaCa.20


[p. 566]
thuṇimaṇa ahicchāē, viṇimgamō jiṇaharāu haṇuvantō
pāyakkhiṇēi mēru, vandantō siddhabhavaṇāī // PaumaCa.21

bharahaṁ ēntassa taō, kamēṇa atyaṁgaō diyaṁsanāhō
haṇuvassa sayalasēnnaṁ, ṭhiyaṁ ca suradunduhigirimma // PaumaCa.22

sō tattha bahulapakkhē, gayaṇayalaṁ māruī palōyantō
pēcchaha ghaṇajhaṇanihaṁ, tārāma samantabhō chana // PaumaCa.23

cintēi tō maṇēṇaṁ, maha ēvaṁ candavirahiyaṁ gayaṇaṁ
na ya sōhaha kulagayaṇaṁ, tahā viṇā purisacandēṇaṁ // PaumaCa.24

taṁ nasthi naē sayalē, ṭhāṇaṁ tilatusatibhāgamētaṁ pi
jattha na kōlaha maccha, sacchandō suravarēhiṁ pi // PaumaCa.25

naï dēvāṇa vi ēsā, cavaṇāvatyā u havaï savāṇaṁ
amhārisāṇa saṁpada, kā ētya kahā maṇusāṇaṁ! // PaumaCa.26

vumanti jatya hatthī, mattā girisiharasanihā galyā
tō ēttha kiṁ va bhaṇṇaï!, paḍhama ciya avahiyā sasayā // PaumaCa.27

annāṇamōhiēṇaṁ, paścindiyavasagaēṇa jīvēṇaṁ
taṁ nasthi mahādukkhēṁ, jaṁ na'ṇuhūrya bhamantēṇaṁ // PaumaCa.28

mahilākarēṇuyāṇaṁ, luddhō gharavāriniyalapaḍibaddhō
aṇuhavaï tattha dukkhaṁ, purisagaō vammahāsattō // PaumaCa.29

pāsēṇa pañjarēṇa ya, bajjhanti caüppayā ya pakkhī ya
iha juvaïpañjarēṇaṁ, baddhā purisā kilissanti // PaumaCa.30

kiṁpāgaphalasaricchā, bhōgā pamuhē havanti gulamahurā
tē cēva u pariṇāmē, nāyanti ya visamavisasarisā // PaumaCa.31

taṁ nāṇiūṇa ēvaṁ, asāsayaṁ addhvaṁ calaṁ nīyaṁ
avahatthiūṇa bhōgē, pabajaṁ gihimō ajaṁ // PaumaCa.32

ēyāṇi ya annāṇi ya, paricintēntassa pavaṇaputtassa
rayaṇī kamēṇa jhīṇā, pabhāsayantō ravī uiō // PaumaCa.33

paḍibuddhō pavaṇasuō, bhaṇaï taō pariyaṇaṁ piyāō ya
dhammābhimuhassa mahaṁ, nisuṇēha paripphuḍaṁ vayaṇaṁ // PaumaCa.34

vasiūṇa suirakālaṁ, māṇusanammammi bandhavēhiṁ samēṁ
avasēṇa vippaōgō, havaï ya mā addhiī kuṇaha // PaumaCa.35

tāhē bhaṇanti haṇuvaṁ, mahilāō mahuramammaṇagirāō
mā muñcasu nāha! tuma, amhē ētthaṁ asaraṇāō // PaumaCa.36


[p. 567]
bhaṇaï taō haṇuvantō, parihiṇḍantassa majjha saṁsārē
mahilāṇa sahassāī, gayāī kālēṇa bahuyāī // PaumaCa.37

na ya māyā nēva piyā, na putadārā ihaṁ marantassa
purisassa paricāṇa, na kuṇanti bahā kuṇaï dhammō // PaumaCa.38

taṁ ēva aṇuhavēḍaṁ, nasyatirikkhēsu dāruṇaṁ dukkhaṁ
kaha puṇa nāṇantō haṁ, karēmi mahilāsu saha nēhaṁ // PaumaCa.39

saṁsārammi aṇantē, bhōō haï jāiyava-maraṇāṇaṁ
saṁpaï laēmi dikvaṁ, marisaha mē aviṇayaṁ sarva // PaumaCa.40

mēruṁ piva thiragaruyaṁ, hiyayaṁ nāūṇa tassa mahilāō
tāhē kuṇanti paramaṁ, akandaṁ lōlanayaṇāō // PaumaCa.41

āsāsiūṇa dhīrō, jubaīō ṭhāviu surya rajjē
niṣphiḍaï vimāṇāō, vijāharasuhaḍaparikiṇṇō // PaumaCa.42

māruhiya purisanāṇaṁ, nāṇāviharayaṇakiraṇapajjaliyaṁ
saṁpatthiō kamēṇaṁ, ujjāṇatyaṁ jiṇāyayaṇaṁ // PaumaCa.43

'kāūṇaṁ vandaṇaya, jiṇabhavaṇē sāhavaṁ suhaniviṭēṁ
nāmēṇa dhammarayaṇaṁ, taṁ paṇamaï māruī tuṭṭhō // PaumaCa.44

kāūṇa ya kihakarma, haṇuvō tō bhaṇaï muṇivaraṁ ēttō
bhayavaṁ! hōhi gurū mē, vihēhi saṁkhēvō dikkha // PaumaCa.45

aṇumaniō gurūṇaṁ, tāhē maüḍaṁ sakuṇḍalāharaṇaṁ
dēi suyassa narindō, saṁjamamaggē kaücchāhō // PaumaCa.46

paricattakāmabhōgō, kuṇaï sirē māruī tō lōyaṁ
haṇuvantō pabaïō, pāsē muṇidhammarayaṇassa // PaumaCa.47

pannāsā satta sayā, saṁvēgaparāyaṇā ya naravaïṇō
pavaïyā khāyanasā, cāraṇasamaṇaṁ paṇamiūṇaṁ // PaumaCa.48

haṇuyassa mahiliyāō, sabāō daïyasōgaduhiyāō
lacchīmaīe sayāsē, bāyāō cēva samaṇīō // PaumaCa.49

sirisēlō kammavaṇaṁ, sabaṁ jhāṇāṇalēṇa dahiūṇa taō
kēvalaladdhāisaō, saṁpattō vimalanimmalaṁ paramapayaṁ // PaumaCa.50


iha paümacariē haṇunivvāṇagamaṇa nāma aṭhuttarasayaṁ pavvaṁ samattaṁ


---------------------------------------------------------------------

[p. 568]
[sakasakahāvihāṇapa]

aha tatya kumārāṇaṁ, haṇuyassa ya nisuṇiūṇa pavaja
bhaṇaï paümō hasantō, kaha bhōgāṇaṁ viracā tē // PaumaCa.1

santē vi ya paricahaüm̐, bhōgē giṇhanti jē hu pabajja
nūṇaṁ tē gahagahiyā, vāūṇa vilahiyā purisā // PaumaCa.2

ahavā tāṇa na vijjā, asthi sahōṇā paōgamahakusalā
jēṇujhiūṇa bhōgā, ṭhiyā ya tava-saṁjamābhimuhā // PaumaCa.3

ēvaṁ bhōgasamuhē, tassa nimaggassa rāmadēvassa
buddhī āsi bhaïnaḍā, sēṇiya! udaēṇa kammassa // PaumaCa.4

aha annayā surindō, sahāe sīhāsaṇē suhaniviṭṭhō
ciṭṭhaï mahidvijuttō, dēvasahassēhiṁ parikiyō // PaumaCa.5

nāṇālaṁkāradharō, ghīrō bala-viriya-tēyasaṁpannō
aha saṁkahāgayaṁ sō, vayaṇaṁ ciya bhaṇaï dēvindō // PaumaCa.6

dēvattaṁ indattaṁ, jassa pasāēṇa pavarasiddhattaṁ
labbhaï taṁ namaha sayā, sasurāsuravandiyaṁ araha // PaumaCa.7

jēṇa imō nissārō, saṁsārarivū jagē ajiyapuchō
saṁnamasaṁgāmamuhē, pāvō nāṇāsiṇā nihaō // PaumaCa.8

kandappataranāda, kasāyagāhāulaṁ bhavāvarta
saṁsārasalilanāhaṁ, uttāraï jō aṇaṁ bhaviyaṁ // PaumaCa.9

jāyassa jassa taïyā, sumērusiharē surēhiṁ sabēhiṁ
jaṇiō ściya ahisēō, khīrōyahivārikalasēhiṁ // PaumaCa.10

mōhamalapaḍalachannaṁ, pāsaṇḍavivajiyaṁ nayavihīṇaṁ
nāṇakiraṇēhi sabaṁ, payāsiya jēṇa tēlōkaṁ // PaumaCa.11

sō jiṇavarō sababhū, bhāṇu sivō saṁkarō mahādēvō
viṇhū hiraṇṇagabbhō, mahēsarō īsarō ruddō // PaumaCa.12

jō ēvamāiēhiṁ, thubaï nāmēhiṁ dēva-maṇuēhiṁ
sō usahō jagabandhū, saṁsārucchēyaṇaṁ kuṇaï // PaumaCa.13

baha icchaha aṇuhaviuṁ, kallāṇaparaṁpara niravasēsaṁ
tō paṇamaha usahajiṇaṁ, sura-asuranamaṁsiyaṁ bhayavaṁ // PaumaCa.14


[p. 569]
jīvō aṇāinihaṇō, sakammapavaṇāhaō paribhamantō
kaha kaha vi māṇusataṁ, pattō na kuṇēi jiṇaghamaṁ // PaumaCa.15

micchādasaṇacariya, kāmarṇa jaï vi lahaï dēvattaṁ
taha vi ya cuō samāṇō', mujhē iha māṇusē jammē // PaumaCa.16

nindaï jiṇavaradhamma, micchatō nāṇa-dasaṇavihūṇō
sō hiṇḍaï saṁsārē, dukkhasahassāī aṇuhōntō // PaumaCa.17

pēcchaha mahiḍḍiyassa vi, sunāṇajuttassa māṇusē nammē
dulahā u havaï bōhī, kiṁ puṇa annāṇajuttassa? // PaumaCa.18

indō bhaṇaï kayā haï, bōhiṁ ladrūṇa māṇusē jammē
kammaṭṭavippamukkō, paramapayaṁ cēva pāvisaṁ? // PaumaCa.19

taṁ bhaṇaï surō ēkō, jaï tujha vi ērisī havaï buddhī
amhārisāṇa niyamā, māṇusajammē vimujjhihii // PaumaCa.20

indaṁ mahiḍḍijuttaṁ, bambhavimāṇē suraṁ cuyasamāṇaṁ
rāmaṁ kiṁ ca na pēcchaha, māṇusabhōgēsu aïmūḍhaṁ? // PaumaCa.21

tō bhaṇaï dēvarāyā, savāṇa vi bandhaṇāṇa dūrēṇaṁ
kaḍhiṇō u nēhabandhō, saṁsāratthāṇa sattāṇaṁ // PaumaCa.22

niyalēhi pūriō ciya, vaccaï purisō jahicchiya dēsaṁ
ēka pi aṅgulamiṇaṁ, na jāi ghaṇanēhapaḍibaddhō // PaumaCa.23

rāmassa niyayakālaṁ, sōmittō ghaṇasiṇēhamaṇurattō
sō vi ya tassa viōgē, muñcaï jōyaṁ aïsamatthō // PaumaCa.24

sō ta lacchinikēyaṁ, paümō na ya muyaï nēhapaḍibaddhō
kammassa ya udaēṇaṁ, kālaṁ ciya nēi maïmūḍhō // PaumaCa.25

suravaïmaṇiyaṁ naṁ taccamaggāṇurattaṁ, jiṇavaraguṇagahaṇaṁ suppasatthaṁ pavitaṁ
suṇiya vibuhasaṅghā taṁ ca indaṁ namēuṁ, aïvimalasarōrā janti saṁ saṁ nikēyaṁ // PaumaCa.26


ii paümacariē sakasakahāvihāṇaṁ nāma navuttarasayaṁ pavyaṁ samattaṁ


---------------------------------------------------------------------

[p. 570]
[lavaṇa-ṅkuisavayōvaṇapavēsavihāṇapavvaṁ]

aha tattha dōṇṇi dēvā, kuūhalī rayaṇacūla-maṇicūlā
nēhaparikkhaṇahēḍaṁ, samāgayā rāma-kēsōṇaṁ // PaumaCa.1

rāmaṁ sōūṇa mayaṁ, karisiyaṁ kuṇaï lakkhaṇō cēhūṁ?
rūsaï kiṁ vā gacchaï?, kiṁ vā paribhāsaē vayaṇaṁ? // PaumaCa.2

ahavā sōgāuliyaṁ, pēcchāmō lakkhaṇassa muhayandaṁ
tē ēva kayālāvā, sāēyapuri aha paviṭṭhā // PaumaCa.3

dēvā rāmassa gharē, kuṇanti māyāviṇimmiyaṁ sadaṁ
paümō maō maō tti ya, varajuvaīṇaṁ ciya vilāvaṁ // PaumaCa.4

rāmassa maraṇasaī, sōuṁ akandiyaṁ ca jubaīhiṁ
lacchīharō visaṇṇō, jaṁpaï tāhē imaṁ vayaṇaṁ // PaumaCa.5

hā kiṁ va imaṁ vattaṁ, ēva bhaṇantassa tassa sayarāhaṁ
vāyāe, samaṁ jīya, viṇiggaya lacchinilayassa // PaumaCa.6

kañcaṇathambhanisannō, aṇimōliyalōyaṇō tahāvatthō
lakkhijjaï cakkaharō, lēppamaō iva viṇimmaviō // PaumaCa.7

daṭṭaṇa vigayajīyaṁ, sōmittiṁ suravarā visaṇṇamaṇā
nindanti ya appāṇaṁ, dōṇṇi vi lajjāsamāvannā // PaumaCa.8

lakkhaṇamaraṇanihēṇaṁ, gāṇaṁ ēttha puravihiēṇaṁ
jāyaṁ paritāvayaraṁ, amhāṇa maṇaṁ tu appāṇaṁ // PaumaCa.9

pacchātātrumhaviyā, jīyaṁ dāūṇa tassa asamatthā
nindantā appāṇaṁ, sōhammaṁ patthiyā dēvā // PaumaCa.10

asamikkhiyakārīṇaṁ, purisāṇaṁ ēttha pāvahiyayāṇaṁ
sayamēva kayaṁ kammaṁ, paritāvayaraṁ havaï pacchā // PaumaCa.11

suravaramāyāe kayaṁ, kammaṁ avijāṇiūṇa jubaīō
paṇayakuviō ti kāuṁ, sabāu paī pasāēnti // PaumaCa.12

ēkkā bhaṇaï suṇiyā, jōvaṇamayagaviyāe pāvāē
sāmi! tumaṁ rōsaviō, kavaṇāē pāvabuddhōē // PaumaCa.13

paṇayakalahammi sāmiya!, bhaṇiō jaṁ aviṇayaṁ tuma tāē
taṁ amha khamasu saṁpaï, jaṁpasu mahurāe bāyāē // PaumaCa.14


[p. 571]
varakamalakōmalaṅgī, avagr̥haï kāvi nibharasiṇēhaṁ
calaṇēsu paḍaï annā, pattiya sāmī! kaüllāvā // PaumaCa.15

ghēttaṇa kāi vīṇaṁ, tassa ya guṇakittaṇaṁ mahurasaha
gāyaï varagandharva, daïyamsa pasāyajaṇaṇaṭuṁ // PaumaCa.16

avagūhiūṇa kāī, cumbaï gaṇḍatthalaṁ maṇabhirāmaṁ
jaṁpada puṇō puṇō ciya, amha pahū! dēhi ullāvaṁ // PaumaCa.17

saṁpuṇṇacandavayaṇā, kayanēvacchā kaḍakvavicchōhaṁ
naccaï kāvi maṇaharaṁ, piyassa puraō sasambhāvaṁ // PaumaCa.18

ēyāṇi ya annāṇi ya, tāṇa kuṇantīṇa cēṭṭiyasayāī
nāyaṁ niratyayaṁ taṁ, jōviyarahiyammi kantammi // PaumaCa.19

cāriyamuhāu suṇiuṁ, taṁ vittantaṁ sasaṁbhamō rāmō
taṁ lakkhaṇassa bhavaṇaṁ, tūrantō caṁba saṁpattō // PaumaCa.20

antēuraṁ paviṭṭhō, pacchaï vigayappamaṁ sirīrahiyaṁ
lacchīharassā bayaṇaṁ, pabhāyasasisannihāyāraṁ // PaumaCa.21

cintēi tō paümō, kēṇa vi kajjēṇa majjha cakaharō
ruṭṭō abbhuṭṭāṇaṁ, na dēi ciṭṭaï aviṇayaṅgō // PaumaCa.22

viralakkamēsu gantuṁ, agghāyaï matthā ghaṇasiṇēhaṁ
paümō bhagaï kaṇiṭuṁ, ki majjha na dēkhi ulāvaṁ? // PaumaCa.23

cindhēhi jāṇi ūṇa ya, gayanīyaṁ lakāvaṇaṁ nahāvanthaṁ
taha vi ya taṁ jīvantaṁ, sō mannaï nimbharasiṇēhō // PaumaCa.24

na ya hasaï nēva japaï, na cēva ussasaï cēṭṭhaparihīṇō
viṭṭhō ya tahāvatthī, sōmittī rāmadēvēṇaṁ // PaumaCa.25

mucchāgaō viuddhō, paramō parimusaï tamsa aṅgāī
nakkhakkhayaṁ pi ēkaṁ, na ya pēcchaï maggamāṇō vi // PaumaCa.26

ēyāvatthassa taō, vējjā saddāviūṇa paümābhō
kārāvēi tigicchaṁ, mantēhi tahōsahi pi // PaumaCa.27

vējagaṇēhiṁ jayā sō, mantōsahisaṁjupahiṁ vivihēhiṁ
na ya paḍivannō cēṭṭa, tō gaō rāhavō muccha // PaumaCa.28

kaha kaha vi samāsatthō, kuṇaï, palāvaṁ taō ya rōvantō
rāmō samunayaṇō, diṭṭhō jubaīhiṁ dīṇamudrō // PaumaCa.29

ēyantarammi tāō, sabāō lapavaṇassa mahilāō
rōvanti vihalavimbhalamaṇāō aṅga haṇantīō // PaumaCa.30


[p. 572]
hā nāha! hā mahājasa!, uddhēhi sasaṁbhamāṇa amhāṇaṁ
paṇivaïyavacchala! tuma, ullāvaṁ dēhi viyasantō // PaumaCa.31

hā dakkhiṇṇaguṇāyara, tujjha sayāsammi ciṭṭhaē paümō
ēyassa kiṁ va ruṭṭō, na ya uṭṭhasi āsaṇavarāō // PaumaCa.32

'asthāṇiyāgayāṇaṁ, suhāṇaṁ nāha! darisaṇamaṇāṇaṁ
hōūṇa sōmacittō, ālāvaṁ dēhi vimaṇāṇaṁ // PaumaCa.33

hā nāha! kiṁ na pēcchasi, ēvaṁ antēuraṁ vilavamāṇaṁ!
sōyāuraṁ ca lōya, kiṁ na nivārēsi dīṇamuhaṁ // PaumaCa.34

sōyāurāhiṁ ahiya, juvaīhiṁ tattha rōvamāṇīhiṁ
hiyayaṁ kassa na kaluṇaṁ, jāyaṁ ciya gaggaraṁ kaṇṭhaṁ? // PaumaCa.35

ēvaṁ rōvantīhiṁ, juvaīhiṁ hāra-kaḍayamāīyaṁ
khitujhiēhiṁ channā, sabā rāyaṅgaṇatthāṇī // PaumaCa.36

ēyantarammi sōuṁ, kālagayaṁ lakkhaṇaṁ susaṁviggā
lavaṇaṁ-'kusā virattā, bhōgāṇaṁ takkhaṇaṁ dhīrā // PaumaCa.37

cintēnti jō surēsu vi, saṁgāmē lakṣaṇō aniyapurō
bala-viriyasamatthō vihu, sō kaha kālāriṇā nihaō? // PaumaCa.38

kiṁ vā imēṇa kīraï, kayalīthambhō cha sārarahiēṇaṁ
dēhēṇa dukkha-dōggaïkarēṇa bhōgāhilāsīṇaṁ? // PaumaCa.39

ganbhavasahīe bhīyā, piyara namiūṇa paramasaṁvēgā
dōṇṇi bi mahindaüdaya, ujjāṇaṁ patthiyā dhīrā // PaumaCa.40

amayarasanāmadhēyaṁ, sāī paḍivajiūṇa tē saraṇaṁ
pabaïyā khāyajasā, uttamaguṇadhārayā jāyā // PaumaCa.41

ēkkattō suyavirahō, maraṇaṁ ca sahōyarassa annattō
ghaṇasōyamahāvatta, rāmō, dukkhaṇṇavē paḍiō // PaumaCa.42

rāmassa piyā puttā, puttāṇa u valahō ya sōmittī
virahē tassa narāhiva!, rāmō aïdukkhiō jāō // PaumaCa.43

ēvaṁ kammaniōgē, saṁpattē sabasaṁgaē bandhujaṇē
sōgaṁ vēraggasamaṁ, jāyantiha vimalacēṭṭhiyā sappurisā // PaumaCa.44


ii paramacariē lavaṇaṁ-'kusatavōvaṇapavēsavihāṇaṁ nāma dasuttarasayaṁ pavvaṁ samattaṁ


---------------------------------------------------------------------

[p. 573]
[rāmavippalāvavihāṇapavvaṁ]

aha kālagayasamāṇē, sēṇiya! nārāyaṇē jugapahāṇē
rāmēṇa sayalaraja, bandhavanēhēṇa paricattaṁ // PaumaCa.1

lacchōharassa dēha, surahisugandhaṁ sahāyaō maüyaṁ
jīēṇa vi parimukta, na muyaha paramō siṇēhēṇaṁ // PaumaCa.2

agghāyaï paricumbaï, ṭhavēi akē puṇō phusaï aṅgaṁ
ruyaï mahāsōgāṇalasaṁtattō rāhavō ahiyaṁ // PaumaCa.3

hā kaha mōttaṇa maē, ēkkāgi dukkhasāgaranimaggaṁ
ahilasasi vaccha! gantuṁ, siṇēharahiō iva nirutaṁ // PaumaCa.4

uṭhēhi dēva! turiyaṁ, tavōvaṇaṁ majjha patthiyā puttā
jāva na vi nanti dūra, tāva ya āṇēhi gantūṇaṁ // PaumaCa.5

dhīra! tumē rahiyāō, aïgāḍhaṁ dukkhiyāō mahilāō
lōlanti dharaṇivaṭē, kaluṇapalā kuṇantīō // PaumaCa.6

viyaliyakuṇḍalahāra, cūḍāmaṇimēhalāīyaṁ ēyaṁ
juvaïjaṇaṁ na nivārasi, vacchya! ahiyaṁ vilavamāṇaṁ // PaumaCa.7

uddēhi sayaṇavacchala!, vāyā mē dēhi vilavamāṇamsa
kiṁ va akāraṇakuviō, harasi muhaṁ dōsarahiyassa? // PaumaCa.8

na tahā dahaï nidāhō, divāyarō huyavahō va pajaliō
naha dahaï niravasēsa, dēhaṁ ēkōyaraviōgō // PaumaCa.9

kiṁ vā karēmi vacchaya!? kattō vaccāmi haï tumē rahiō?
ṭhāṇaṁ pēcchāmi na taṁ, nidhāṇaṁ jattha ra lahāmi // PaumaCa.10

hā vaccha! muścasu imaṁ, kōvaṁ sōmō ya hōhi saṁkhavaṁ
saṁpaï aṇagārāṇaṁ, vaṭṭaï vēlā maharisīṇaṁ // PaumaCa.11

atthāō divasayarō, lacchīhara! kiṁ na pēcchasi imāī
maülanti kuvalayāī, viyasanti ya kumuyasaṇḍāī? // PaumaCa.12

astharaha lahum̐ sējaṁ, kāūṇa bhuyantarammi sōmitti
sēvāmi jēṇa nidaṁ, parivajjiyasasavāvārō // PaumaCa.13

saṁpuṇṇacandasarisaṁ, āsi tumaṁ aïmaṇōharaṁ vayaṇaṁ
kajaṇa kaṁṇa supurisa!, saṁpaï vigayappabhaṁ nāyaṁ? // PaumaCa.14


[p. 574]
naṁ tujjha hiyayaïṭuṁ, davaṁ saṁpāyayāmi taṁ sarva
sabāvāramaṇaharaṁ, kāūṇa muha samullavasu // PaumaCa.15

muśca visāyaṁ supurisa!, amhaṁ ciya khēyarā aïviruddhā
sabē vi āgayā vi hu, ghēttumaṇā kōsalaṁ kuddhā // PaumaCa.16

mahayaṁ pi sattusēnnaṁ, jiṇayantō jō imēṇa cakkēṇaṁ
sō kaha sahasi paribhavaṁ, kayanta cakkassa dhīra tumaṁ // PaumaCa.17

sundara! vimuñca nidaṁ, vōlīṇā sabarī ravī uiō
dēhaṁ pasāhiūṇaṁ, cisu asthāṇamajhagaō // PaumaCa.18

sabō vi' ya puhaïnaṇō, samāgaō tujha sanniyāsammi
gurubhatta! mittavacchala!, ēyassa karēhi māṇatthaṁ // PaumaCa.19

niyayaṁ tu suppahāyaṁ, jiṇāṇa lōgāvalōgadarisīṇaṁ
bhaviyapaümāṇa vi puṇō, nāyaṁ muṇisubaō saraṇaṁ // PaumaCa.20

vaccha! tumē cirasaïē, siḍhilāyaï jiṇaharēsu saṁgīyaṁ
samaṇā jaṇēṇa samaya, saṁpattā cēva ubēyaṁ // PaumaCa.21

uṭhēhi sayaṇavacchala , dhīrēhi mamaṁ visāyapaḍivannaṁ

[baladēvaṇikkhamaṇapavvaṁ]

paralōganicchiyamaṇaṁ, sattugdhaṁ jāṇiūṇaṁ paümābhō

taṁ ṭhavaï kumāravaraṁ saṁmattavasuhāhivaṁ niyayarajjē

[p. 582]

chēttaṇa mōhaṁ pāsa, saṁcuṇṇēūṇa nēhaniyalāī
tāhē muñcaï paümō, maüḍāiṁ bhūsaṇavarāī // PaumaCa.13

kāūṇa tattha ghōrō, uvavāsaṁ kamalakōmalakarahiṁ
uppāḍaï niyayasirē, kēsē varakusumasusuyandhē // PaumaCa.14

vāmappāsaṭhiyassa u, saha syaharaṇēṇa dāu sāmaïyaṁ
pavāviō ya paümō, suṣayanāmēṇa samaṇēṇaṁ // PaumaCa.15

pañcamahatbayakaliō, pañcasu samiīsu cēva āuttō
guttīsu tīsu guttō, bārasatavadhāraō dhīrō // PaumaCa.16

mukkā ya kusumavuṭṭhī, dēvēhi ya dunduhī nahē pahayā
pavaṇō ya surahigandhō, paḍupaḍaharavō ya saṁjaṇiō // PaumaCa.17

mōttaṇa rāyalacchi, niyayapaē ṭhāviuṁ surya jēhūm̐
sattugyō pabaïō, indiyasattū niṇiya sabē // PaumaCa.18

rāyā bihīsaṇō vi ya, suggīvō naravaī nalō nīlō
candanahō gambhīrō, virāhiō cēva daḍhasattō // PaumaCa.19

ēē annē ya bahū, daṇuindā naravaī ya pavaïyā
rāmēṇa saha mahappā, saṁkhāē sōlasa sahassā // PaumaCa.20

jubaīṇa sahassāī, tīsaṁ sattuttarāī taddivasaṁ
pabajjamuvagayāī, sirimaïajjāe pāsammi // PaumaCa.21

kāūṇa ya pabajja, sahi vāsāī mubayasayāsē
tō kuṇaï muṇivarō sō, ēkllavihāraparikammaṁ // PaumaCa.22


[p. 583]
vivihābhimgahadhārī, pubaksuēṇa bhāviyamaīō
tavabhāvaṇāiyāō, bhāvēḍē bhāvaṇāō ya // PaumaCa.23

maha niggaō muṇī sō, gurūṇa aṇumōiō paümanāhō
paḍivanō ya vihāra, ēkkāī sattabhayarahiō // PaumaCa.24

girikandaraṭṭiyassa ya, rayaṇīē tōe tassa uppanna
paümamsa avahināṇa, sahasā jhāṇēkacittassa // PaumaCa.25

avahivisaraṇa tāhē, sumaraï lacchīharaṁ paümaṇāhō
aviyaṇhakāmabhōgaṁ, narayāvatthaṁ ca dukkhattaṁ // PaumaCa.26

saṁyamēga kumārattē, tiṣṇēva saṁyāṇi maṇḍalittē ya
cattālīsa ya vijaē, jassa u saṁvaccharō'tīyā // PaumaCa.27

ēkkārasa ya sahassī, pañcēva sayā tahēva sahijayā
varisāṇi mahārajē, jēṇa sayāsē ṭhiyā visayā // PaumaCa.28

bārasa cēva sahassā, havanti varisāṇaṁ sabasaṁkhāē
bhōttaṇa indiyasuha, gaō ya naraya animiyappā // PaumaCa.29

dēvāṇa kō va dōsō, parabhavajaṇiya samāgaya kamma
bandhavanēhanihēṇaṁ, maō gaō lakkhaṇō narayaṁ // PaumaCa.30

maha tassa nēhabandhō, vasudattāībhavēsu bahuēmuṁ
āsi purā maha jhīṇō, saṁpaï sabō mahāmōhō // PaumaCa.31

ēvaṁ jaṇō samatthō, bandhavanēhāṇurāyapaḍibaddhō
dhammaṁ asaddahantō, parihiṇḍaï dōhasaṁsārē // PaumaCa.32

ēvaṁ sō baladēvō, ēgāgī tattha kandaruddēsē
ciṭṭhaï sajjhāyaraō, dukkhavimōkkhaṁ vicintēntō // PaumaCa.33

ēvaṁ ciya nilamaṇaṁ, baladēvamuṇissa suṇiya ēyamaṇā
hōha jiṇadhammanirayā, "niccaṁ bhō vimalacēṭṭhiyā sappurisā // PaumaCa.34

[baladēvamaṇigōyarasaṁkhōmavihāṇapavvaṁ]

aha sō baladēvamuṇī, chaṭuvavāsē taō vaïkantē
pavisaraï sandaṇathaliṁ, mahāpuraṁ pāraṇadvāē // PaumaCa.1

mattagayalīlagāmī, sarayaravī cēva kantisaṁjuṇē
diṭṭhō nayarijaṇēṇaṁ, accanbhuyarūvasaṁṭhāṇō // PaumaCa.2

vēḍhēi paümaṇāī, sāhukāraṁ vimuścantō // PaumaCa.3

caṁpaï jaṇō samatthō, ahō hu tavasaṁjamēṇa rūvēṇaṁ
narasundarēṇa sayalaṁ, ēēṇa alaṁkiyaṁ bhuvaṇaṁ // PaumaCa.4

ābaddhapariyarā vi ya, kēi narā surabhigandhajalapuṇṇā
uvaṇēnti kaṇayakalasē, annōnnaṁ cēva lavantā // PaumaCa.11

[p. 585]

hatthī alāṇathambhē, bhattaṇa viṇiggayā bahavē // PaumaCa.14

nāyā khara-karahā viya, mahisa-baïllā ya bhayabhīyā // PaumaCa.15

tē jaṇavayassa saī, paḍiṇandī narabaī suṇēūṇaṁ
païsēi niyayabhiccē, kīsa imaṁ āulaṁ nayaraṁ! // PaumaCa.16

parimuṇiyakāraṇēhi, siṭē micēhiṁ naravaī tāhē

tassa gharammi mahāmuṇi!, sahāvamukkappiyaṁ varāhāraṁ
gēṇhasu nirāulamaṇā, ēhi pasāyaṁ kuṇasu amha // PaumaCa.19

bhikkhā samujjayāō, dāuṁ supasannabhāvāō // PaumaCa.20

[paümaṇibvāṇagamaṇapabvaṁ]

aha sō sīyāindō, narayatthaṁ lakkhaṇaṁ 'sumariūṇaṁ

ōyaraṇā-''ruhaṇāī, kārijantēttha bahuyāī // PaumaCa.5

jantēsu kēha chūḍhā, pīlijjantē purā akayapuṇṇā
kandūsu uddhapāyā, ḍajjhanti ahōmuhā annē // PaumaCa.6

asicakamōggarahayā, lōlantā kakkhaḍē dharaṇivaḍhē
khajanti ārasantā, cittaya-vaya-vaggha-sīhēhiṁ // PaumaCa.7

pāijjanti raḍantā, sutattatēvutambasannima salilaṁ
asipatavaṇagayā vi ya, annē chijanti satthēhiṁ // PaumaCa.8


[p. 591]
sō ēvamāiyāī, darcha dukkhāī narayavāsīṇaṁ
kāruṇṇamaṇiyahiyaō, sōyaï paramaṁ suravarindō // PaumaCa.9

sō aggikuṇḍamajjhāu nimgayaṁ lakkhaṇaṁ suravarindō
pēcchaï tālijjanta, bahuēhi ya nasyapālēhiṁ // PaumaCa.10

sō tēhi tassa puraō, karavatta-'sivatta-jantamādīhiṁ
bhayavihalavēviyanō, bāijjaï bāyaṇasaēhiṁ // PaumaCa.11

divō lāhivaī, surēṇa bhaṇiō ya tattha saṁbukō
rē pāva! puvajaṇiyaṁ, anja vi kōvaṁ na chaḍḍēsi // PaumaCa.12

tibakasāyavasagayā, aṇivāriyaïndiyā kivārahiyā
tē ēttha narayalōē, aṇuhunti aṇēyadukkhāī // PaumaCa.13

sōūṇa vi nēraïyaṁ, dukkhaṁ jīvassa jāyaï bhavōhē
kiṁ puṇa tujha na jāyaï, bhayaṁ ihaṁ visahamāṇassa: // PaumaCa.14

sōūṇa vayaṇamēyaṁ, saṁbukkō uvasamaṁ samaṇupattō
tāhē lāhivaī, lakkhaṇasahiyaṁ bhaṇaï dēvō // PaumaCa.15

mōttaṇa bhaübēya, maha vayaṇaṁ suṇaha tāva vīsatthā
tummē hi viraïrahiyā, saṁpattā ērisaṁ dukkhaṁ // PaumaCa.16

divavimāṇārūḍhaṁ, tē rāvaṇa-lakkhaṇā muraṁ 1
pucchanti sāhasu phuḍaṁ, kō si tuma āgaō ētya? // PaumaCa.17

sō tāṇa sāhaï surō, ēttō paümāiyaṁ jahāvattaṁ
paḍibōhakāraṇaṭē, niyayaṁ ca samāgamārambhaṁ // PaumaCa.18

niyaya ciya vittantaṁ, muṇiuṁ tē tattha dō vi paḍibuddhā
sōēnti dōṇavayaṇā, appāṇaṁ lajjiyamaīyā // PaumaCa.19

dhī! kiṁ na kō dhammō, taïyā amhēhiṁ māṇusē nammē?
jēṇēha duhāvasthā, saṁpacā dāruṇē naraē // PaumaCa.20

dhannō si tumaṁ suravara!, jō paricaïūṇa visayasōkkhāiṁ
niṇavaradhammāṇuraō, saṁpattō cēva dēviti // PaumaCa.21

tattō sō kāruṇiō, jaṁpaï mā bhāha dō vi tummē haïṁ
hakkhuviūṇa imāō, naragāō nēmi suralōyaṁ // PaumaCa.22

ābaddhapariyarō sō, hakkhuviūṇaṁ taō samāḍhattō
viliyanti aïdugējjhā, tē aṇalahaō va navanīō // PaumaCa.23

sabōvāēhi jayā, ghēttaṇa na cāiyā surindēṇaṁ
tāhē tē nēraïyā, bhaṇanti dēvaṁ muyasu ahaṁ // PaumaCa.24


[p. 592]
gacchasu tuma surāhiva!, sigdha ciya āraṇadhurya kappaṁ
amhēhiṁ pāvanaṇiya, aṇuhaviyaba mahādukkha // PaumaCa.25

visayāmisaluddhāṇaṁ, narayagāṇaṁ aīvadukkhāṇaṁ
niyaya parabasāṇaṁ, dēvā vi kuṇanti kiṁ tāṇaṁ! // PaumaCa.26

dēva! tumaṁ asamatthō, imassa dukkhassa mōium̐ amhē
taha kuṇasu maha na puṇarabi havaï maī narayagaïgamaṇē // PaumaCa.27

maṇaï surō a rahassaṁ, paramaṁ ciya uttama sivaṁ suddhaṁ
sammaīsaṇarayaṇaṁ, gēhaha paramēṇa viṇaṇaṁ // PaumaCa.28

ēvaṁ gaē vi saṁpaï, naï icchaha attaṇō dhurva sēyaṁ
tō gēhaha sammattaṁ, suddhaṁ nivāṇagamaṇaphalaṁ // PaumaCa.29

ēttō na uttaraṁ vi hu, na ya bhūyaṁ na ya bhavissaē annaṁ
mahamaṅgalaṁ pavittā tilōgasiharaṭṭhiyā siddhā // PaumaCa.30

jīvāipayasthā jē, jiṇēhiṁ bhaṇiyā tilōyadarisōhiṁ
tivihēṇa sahahantō, sammadiṭṭhī narō hōī // PaumaCa.31

bhaṇiēhiṁ tēhi ēvaṁ, gahiyaṁ narayaṭṭiēhiṁ samma
jaṁ bahubhavakōḍīhi vi, aṇāimantēhi na ya pattaṁ // PaumaCa.32

bhō suravaï! amha hiyaṁ, tumē kayaṁ kāraṇaṁ aïmahanta
sayalajīvalōē, sammataṁ uttama dinnaṁ // PaumaCa.33

bhō bhō sīinda! tumaṁ, gaccha lahuṁ āraṇacuyaṁ kappaṁ
jiṇavaradhammassa phalaṁ, bhuñjasu aïuttamaṁ bhōgaṁ // PaumaCa.34

ēvaṁ mahāṇubhāvō, dēvō kāūṇa tāṇa uvayāraṁ
sōēntō nēraïē, saṁpattō attaṇō ṭhāṇaṁ // PaumaCa.35

sō tattha varavimāṇē, sēvijantō vi amarakannāhiṁ
sariūṇa narayadukkhaṁ, dēvindō addhiī kuṇaï // PaumaCa.36

avayariūṇāḍhatō, paümēṇālaṁkiya imaṁ bharahaṁ
gaya-turaya vasaha-kēsariṭhiēsu dēvēsu parikiṇṇō // PaumaCa.37

bahutūraniṇāēṇaṁ, acchara saṁgijjamāṇamāhappō
paümassa gaō saraṇaṁ, sīindō sayalaparivārō // PaumaCa.38

sabāyarēṇa dēvō, thōūṇa puṇō puṇō paümaṇāhaṁ
tatthēva sanniviṭṭhō, mahivīḍhē pariyaṇasamaggō // PaumaCa.39


[p. 593]
namiūṇa pucchā surō, maya jē ēltha dasarahāīyā
svarṇa-kasā ya bhaviyā, sāhasu kavaṇaṁ gaī pattā! // PaumaCa.10

vaṁ ēva pucchiō sō, baladēvō bhaṇaha āṇaē kappē
vaha aṇaraṇṇasuō, dēvō vimalambarāmaraṇō // PaumaCa.11

tē dō vi jaṇaya -kaṇayā, kēgaha taha suppahā ya sōmittī
avarāiyāe samaya, imāī saggōvavanāī // PaumaCa.42

ṇāṇa-tava-saṁgamavaḍhā, visuddhasōlā lava-kusā dhīrā
gacchōhanti guṇadharā, abābāhaṁ sivaṁ ṭhāṇaṁ // PaumaCa.43

ēva maṇiō surindō, añcanta harisiō puṇō namiuṁ
pucchaï kahēhi bhayava!, saṁpaï bhāmaṇḍalassa gaī // PaumaCa.44

tō bhaṇaï sīradhārī, suravara! nimuṇēhi tāva saṁbandha
cariēṇa tujjha bhāyā, jēṇaṁ ciya pāviyaṁ ṭhāṇaṁ // PaumaCa.15

aha kōsalāpurīē, ghaṇavantō asthi vajakō nāma
puttā asōya-tilyā, tassa piyā mayariyā bhajjā // PaumaCa.46

nivāsiya suṇē, sōya sō duksimō taō jāō
cintēi sā araṇṇē, kaha kuṇaï thiī mahāpōrē: // PaumaCa.47

ahiyē kivāluō sō, saṁviggō juimuṇissa sōsattaṁ
paḍivajiūṇa jāō samaṇō parivajjiyārambhō // PaumaCa.48

aha annayā kayāī, asōga-tilayā gayā juimuṇindaṁ
paṇamanti āyarēṇaṁ, piyaraṁ ca puṇō puṇō tuṭṭhā // PaumaCa.19

sōmaṇa dhammarayaṇaṁ, sahasā tē tibajāyasaṁvēgā
'dōṇi vi juissa pāsē, asōya-tilayā viṇikkhantā // PaumaCa.50

kāaṇa tavaṁ ghōraṁ, kālāmō uvarimammi gēvējē
uvavannō tattha juī, mahājuī uttamō dēvō // PaumaCa.51

tē tatya piyā putā, kukkuḍanayara samujjayā gantuṁ
saṁvēyajaṇiyabhāvā, vandaṇahēuṁ niṇindassa // PaumaCa.52

pannāsa jōyaṇāī, gayāṇa aha annayā samaṇupattō
navapāusō mahāṣaṇataḍicchaḍāḍōvasalilōhō // PaumaCa.53

tō girivarassa hēḍhē, jōgatthā muṇivarā dadadhiīyā
jantēṇa kōsalāē, dihā jaṇayassa puttēṇaṁ // PaumaCa.54


[p. 594]
cintēi imē sāhū, ihaṭṭhiyā samayarakkhaṇaṭṭāē
ghōrē upāsaṇaē, raṇē bahusāvayāiṇṇē // PaumaCa.55

bhāmaṇḍalēṇa ēvaṁ, cintēuṁ pāṇarakkhaṇanimitaṁ
sāhūṇa samāsanē, vijāsu kayē puraṁ paramaṁ // PaumaCa.56

kālē dēsē ya puraṁ, samāgayā gōcarēṇa tē samaṇā
paḍilāmēi mahappā, caṁuvihaāhāradāṇēṇaṁ // PaumaCa.57

ēvaṁ kamēṇa tāṇaṁ, cāummāsī gayā muṇivarāṇaṁ
bhāmaṇḍalēṇa vi taō, dāṇaphalaṁ ajiya viulaṁ // PaumaCa.58

bhāmaṇḍalō kayāī, saha sundaramahiliyāe ujjāṇē
asaṇihabhō ubavanō, dēvakurāē tipaścāū // PaumaCa.59

dāṇēṇa bhōgabhūmī, lahaï narō tavaguṇēṇa dēvattaṁ
nāṇēṇaṁ siddhisuha, pāvaï nastva saṁdēhō // PaumaCa.6

puṇaravi bhaṇaha surindō, ahōgaī lakkhaṇō samaṇupattō
ubaṭṭō ya mahāmaṇi!, ṭhāṇaṁ kavaṇaṁ tu pāvihiha // PaumaCa.11

nijariya kammanibaha, labhihī kavaṇaṁ gaī ca dahavayaṇō:
kō va bhavōhāmi ahaṁ!, ēvaṁ icchāmi nāu jē // PaumaCa.12

bhaṇaï taō baladēvō, suṇēhi dēvinda! āgamissāṇaṁ
uktiṇaṁ bhavāṇaṁ, lahāhiva-lacchinilayāṇaṁ // PaumaCa.63

narayāu samuttiṇṇā, kamēṇa surapavayassa puṣēṇaṁ
vijayāvahanayarīē, maṇuyā tē dō vi hōhinti // PaumaCa.64

tāṇaṁ piyā suṇandō, jaṇaṇī vi ya havaha rōhiṇī nāma
sāvayakulasaṁbhūyā, gurudēvayapūyaṇāhirayā // PaumaCa.65

aïsundarasvadharā, nāmēṇaṁ arahadāsa-siridāsā
kāūṇa sāvayattaṁ, dēvā hōhinti suralōē // PaumaCa.66

cajhyā tatyēva purē, maṇuyā hōūṇa sāvayā paramā
muṇivaradāṇaphalēṇaṁ, hōhinti narā ya harivarisē // PaumaCa.67

bhōga bhōttūṇa mayā, dēvā hōhinti dēvalōgammi
caïyā tatthēva purē, naravaïputtā havīhanti // PaumaCa.68

vāukumārassa suyā, lacchīdēvīe kucchisaṁbhūyā
amarindasarisarūvā, jayakanta-jayappahā dhōrā // PaumaCa.69

kāūṇa tavamuyāra, dēvā hōhinti lantaē kappē
uttamabhōgaṭhiīyā, uttamaguṇadhārayā dhīrā // PaumaCa.70


[p. 595]
tuhamavi iha bharahē khala, caūṇaṁ añcuyāu kappāō
cōisarayaṇāhivāī, cakkaharō hōhisi nirutaṁ // PaumaCa.71

tē cēva surā caïyā, dōṇi vi tuha nandaṇā bhavīhanti
induraha-bhōyarahā, amarakumārōvamasirīyā // PaumaCa.72

paranārivajaṇēṇaṁ, vaēṇa ēkēṇa sō hu dahavayaṇō
jāō ciya indurahō, sammataparāyaṇō dhīrō // PaumaCa.73

sō cēva ya indurahō, labhiūṇa bhavā imā surāīyā
pacchā hōhaï arahā, samatthatēlōkaparimahiō // PaumaCa.74

aha sō vi cakvaṭṭī, rajja rayaṇatyalē purē kāuṁ
hōhaï tavōbalēṇaṁ, ahamindō vējayantammi // PaumaCa.75

sō hu tuma samgāō, caïō arahassa tassa gaṇapavarō
hōmaga tihuyaṇamga, siddhisuhaṁ cēva pāvihisi // PaumaCa.76

ēsō tē parikahiō, dasāṇaṇō saha tumē surāhivaī!
ēttō suṇāhi puṇaravi, lakkhaṇapagayaṁ bhaṇijjantaṁ // PaumaCa.77

jō sō'yaṁ bhōyarahō, cakkaharasuō tavaṣpabhāvaṇaṁ
bhamiūṇa uttamabhavē, kēī daḍhadhammasaṁjuttō // PaumaCa.78

pukkharadīvavidēhē, paümapurē lakṣaṇō u cakkaharō
hōhii titthayarō puṇa, tatyēva bhavē tiyasaṇāhō // PaumaCa.79

satsu varisēsu jiṇō, kāūṇa asēsadōsasaṁghāraṁ
sura-asuranamiyacalaṇō, pāvihii aṇuttaraṁ ṭhāṇaṁ // PaumaCa.8

ēvaṁ kēvalikahiyaṁ, bhavissabhavasaṁkahaṁ suṇēūṇaṁ
jāō saṁsayarahiō, paḍiindō bhāvaṇājuttō // PaumaCa.81

namiūṇa rāmadēvaṁ, tāhē sabāyarēṇa puṇarutaṁ
abhivandaï surapavarō, niṇavarabhavaṇāī vivihāī // PaumaCa.82

nandīsarāiyāī, abhivandēūṇa cēiyaharāī
kuruvaṁ ciya saṁpattō, pēcchada bhāmaṇḍalaṁ dēvō // PaumaCa.83

saṁbhāsiūṇa payaō, saṁbōhiya bhāyaraṁ siṇēhēṇaṁ
vibuhāhivō khaṇēṇaṁ, saṁpattō accurya kappaṁ // PaumaCa.84

tatyāraṇapuē sō, amaravalsayasahassaparikiṇṇō
aṇuhavaï uttamasuha, sīindō sumahayaṁ kālaṁ // PaumaCa.85


[p. 596]
pannarasa sahassāī, barisāṇa tayā''si āuya haliṇō
sōlasa cāvāṇi puṇō, uccattaṁ cēva nāyavaṁ // PaumaCa.86

pēcchaha balēṇa mahayā, niṇindavarasāsaṇē ghiī kārḍa
jamma-jarā-maraṇarivū, parājiyā ghīrasattaṇaṁ // PaumaCa.87

nissēsadōsarahimaō, nāṇāaïsayavibhūsaṁjuttō
kēvalakiraṇujaliō, vibhāi saraē va divasayarō // PaumaCa.88

ārāhiūṇa dhīrō, jiṇasamayaṁ pañcavīsa varisāī
āukkhayammi pattō, paümō sivasāsayaṁ ṭhāṇaṁ // PaumaCa.89

vigayabhavahēugaṁ taṁ, aṇagāraṁ suddhasīlasammattaṁ
sabāyarēṇa paṇamaha, dukkhakkhayakārayaṁ rāmaṁ // PaumaCa.90

pubasiṇēhēṇa tayā, sīyādēvāhivēṇa parimahiyaṁ
paramiḍḍisaṁpaüttaṁ, paṇamaha rāma maṇōrāmaṁ // PaumaCa.91

ikkhāgavaṁsatilayaṁ, iha bharahē aṭṭamaṁ tu baladēvaṁ
taṁ namaha ṇēyabhavasayasahassamukkaṁ sivapayatthaṁ // PaumaCa.92

ēyaṁ halaharacariyaṁ, niyayaṁ jō suṇaï suddhabhāvaṇaṁ
sō lahaï bōhilābha, buddhi-balā''uṁca aïparamaṁ // PaumaCa.13

ujjayasatyō vi rikhū, khippaṁ uvasamaï tassa uvasamgō
ajiṇaī cēva puṇṇaṁ, nasēṇa samayaṁ na saṁdēhō // PaumaCa.94

rajjarahiō vi rajaṁ, lahaï dhaṇatthī mahādhaṇaṁ viulaṁ
uvasamaï takkhaṇaṁ ciya, vāhī sōmā ya hōnti gahā // PaumaCa.95

mahilatthī varamahilaṁ, puttatthī gōttanandaṇaṁ puttaṁ
lahaï paradēsagamaṇē, samāgamaṁ cēva bandhūṇaṁ // PaumaCa.96

dubbhāsiyāī duñcintiyāī duścariyasayasahassāī
nāsanti paümakittaṇakahāe dūra samatthāī // PaumaCa.97

naṁ pi ya jaṇassa hiyaēṁ, avaṭṭiyaṁ kāraṇaṁ aïmahantaṁ
taṁ tassa nicchaēṇaṁ, uvaṇamaï suhāṇubandhēṇaṁ // PaumaCa.98

ēvaṁ dhammōvāyā, siṭṭhā tava-niyama-sīlamāīyā
titthayarēhi mahānasa!, aṇantanāṇuttamadharēhiṁ // PaumaCa.99

niyayaṁ karēha bhatti, jiṇāṇa maṇa-vayaṇa-kāyasaṁjuttā
jēṇa'ṭṭakammarahiyā, pāvaha siddhiṁ suvīsatthā // PaumaCa.10


[p. 597]
ēvaṁ visuddhalaliyakkharahēujutaṁ, askhāṇaēmu vivihēsu nibaddhamatthaṁ
nāsēi duggaïpaha" khalu nicchaēṇaṁ, rāmāravindacariyaṁ tu suyaṁ samatthaṁ // PaumaCa.101

ēvaṁ vīrajiṇēṇa rāmacariya siṭuṁ mahatthaṁ purā, pacchā''khaṇḍalabhūiṇā u kahiyaṁ sīsāṇa dhammāsayaṁ
bhūō sāhuparaṁparāe, sayalaṁ lōē ṭhiyaṁ pāyarḍa, ēttāhē vimalēṇa suttasahiyaṁ gāhānibaddha kayaṁ // PaumaCa.102

pañcēva ya bāsasayā, dusamāē tīsavarisasaṁjulā
vīrē siddhimuvagaē, taō nibaddha imaṁ cariyaṁ // PaumaCa.103

halahara-cakaharāṇaṁ, samaya lavāhivēṇa jaṁ vatta
visayāmisasattāṇa, ithinimittaṁ raṇaṁ paramaṁ // PaumaCa.104

bahujuvaïsahassēhiṁ, na ya pattō uvasamaṁ mayaṇamūḍhō
sō vijāhararāyā, gaō ya naraya aṇimiyappā // PaumaCa.105

jō'ṇēyapaṇaïṇīhiṁ, lālijjantō vi na ya gaō tittiṁ
kaha puṇa annō tuṣṭuiṁ, vañcihii suthōvavilayāhiṁ? // PaumaCa.106

jē visayasuhāsattā, purisā taba-niyama-saṁjamavihūṇā
tē ujjhiūṇa rayaṇaṁ, gēhanti hu kāgiṇiṁ mūḍhā // PaumaCa.107

ēvaṁ vēranimitta, paranārīsaṁsiya suṇēūṇaṁ
hōha paralōyakalī, paravilayaṁ cēva bajēha // PaumaCa.108

sukayaphalēṇa maṇussō, pāvaï ṭhāṇaṁ susaṁpayanihāṇaṁ
dukayaphalēṇa ya kugaī, lahaï sahāvō imō lōē // PaumaCa.109

na ya dēi kōi kassaï, ārōggadhaṇaṁ tahēva paramāuṁ
naï dēnti surā lōē, taha vi hu kiṁ dukkhiyā bahavē? // PaumaCa.110

kāma-stha-dhamma-mōkkhā, ēttha purāṇammi vaṇṇiyā sabaï
aguṇē mōttūṇa guṇē, gēṇhaha jē tumha hiyajaṇaṇē // PaumaCa.111

bahuēṇa kiṁ va kīraï, abō bhaṇiyabaēṇa lōyammi?
ēkkaṣayammi vi bujhaha, ramaha sayā niṇavaramayammi // PaumaCa.112


[p. 598]
viṇasāsaṇāṇuraṇa, hōūṇaṁ kumaha uttama dharma
jēṇa avigdhaṁ pāvaha, baladēvāī gayā natya // PaumaCa.11

ēmaṁ rāhacariyaṁ, sabā vi ya samayadēvayā niyayaṁ
kuāntu saṁsaṇijja, jaṇaṁ ca niyamattisaṁjutaṁ // PaumaCa.114

svatantu bhaviyalōya, sūrāīyā gahā aparisēsā
susamāhiyasōmamaṇā, jiṇavaradhammujjayamaīyā // PaumaCa.115

aṇaṁ ahari bā, jē ēstha kayaṁ pamāyadōsēṇaṁ
taṁ mē paḍipūrē, khamantu iha paṇḍiyā saī // PaumaCa.116

rāhū nāmāyariō, sasamayaparasamayagahiyasabbhāvō
'vijaō ya tassa sīsō, nāilakulavaṁsanandiyarō // PaumaCa.117

sīsēṇa tassa raïyaṁ, rāhavacariyaṁ tu sūrivimalēṇaṁ
sōūṇaṁ puṣagaē, nārāyaṇaṁ-sīricariyāī // PaumaCa.118

jēhiṁ surya vavagayamaccharēhiṁ tabbhatibhāviyamaṇēhiṁ
tāṇaṁ vihēu bōhiṁ, bimalaṁ cariya supurisāṇaṁ // PaumaCa.119


ii paümacariē paümanivyāṇagamaṇaṁ nāma adamuttarasaya pacaṁ samattaṁ


ii nāilavaṁsadiṇayararāhusūripasīsēṇa mahappēṇa puṣaharēṇa vimalāyariēṇa viraïyaṁ sammattaṁ paümacariyaṁ
